Amanneɛbɔfo no kae bere a wɔkyeree wɔn no , wɔde atuo ne sika kɔkɔɔ guu wɔn so wɔ GHC1,292,180,180,292,180,180, sɛ wɔde sika kɔkɔɔ mfuturu , a wosusuw sɛ ɛyɛ sika kɔkɔɔ aboɔden aboɔden aboɔden abo , na wohui sɛ ɛyɛ aboɔden aboɔden aboɔden aboɔden abo
Adwowtwafo bi a wosusuw sɛ wɔawiawia wɔn ho afi Polilisifo afiase a ɛwɔ Kyebi mantam a ɛwɔ Apuei fam no mu .
Starr News aboaboa nsɛm a wotumi de ho to so ano afi Kyebi mu aba sɛ wɔde Ebenezer Gyimliafo Asomdwoe ho asɛm bi a Antied Robbery squad ne Personnel a ofi CIDad adwumayɛbea a ɛwɔ June 24,2021 no kyeree no wɔ nnwuma pii a wɔyɛe wɔ Atifi fam ne South Municity mu no ho .
Wɔde adwene no kɔɔ Kyebi Zongofo no so sɛ wɔbɛhwehwɛ wɔn akyi kwan nanso wɔbɔɔ mmɔden guanee .
Da bi akyi no , Kyebi Polisini no san kyeree adwowtwafo foforo a wosusuw sɛ wɔfrɛ noMusa Kamara ,26 , a na ɔwɔ Polilisifo mu a na ɔpɛ sɛ ɔbobɔ ne din wɔ Kibiongo Zongo wɔ June 25,2021 mu no .
Ɔbɔɔ mmɔden nso sɛ obeguan , nanso Polilisini no de tuo too nkotodwe a ɛwɔ benkum no so .
Wɔde nea wɔakyere no no kɔɔ Kyebi aban ayaresabea a ɛwɔ baabi a polisifo wɛn no .
Wɔbɔ amanneɛ sɛ nnipa baanu a wosusuw wɔn ho no ka adwowtwafo basabasayɛfo kuw bi a wɔte Kibi , Abim Tam, Osiem, Anyinasin ne n'afuw mu no ho .
Anyɛ yiye koraa no , wɔyɛɛ adwowtwafo akuw 10 ho kyerɛwtohɔ wɔ Municipalfo akuw abien no mu wɔ asram abiɛsa ntam .
Adwowtwafo no ntua a ɛbaa nnansa yi wɔ June 6,2021 mu no maa ɔbea bi a basabasayɛfo no bɔɔ no tuo kum no wɔ Adumtukrom kosi Bunso the Koforidua mu kosi Bunso Highway .
Nnipa baanu bi a wobu wɔn ani gu Haruna Amadu , 25 , ne Joseph Nyira, de nnɔnhwerew 25 na ɛkyeree wɔn bere a asɛm no sii akyi no .
Ntoboa biako pɛ a wɔde tuo ayɛ a ne bo nyɛ den , a wɔfrɛ no GhC257.00, telefon a wokura kyin , abiɛsa , a ogya bepɔw abien bi a wɔfrɛ no ID ka wɔn a wokunkum wɔn no ho , a wɔde telefon a wokura kyin a wokura kyin a wɔn ho yɛ ahyɛnsode gu mu , ne sukuufo a wɔyɛ abibifo a wɔn ho wɔn ho wɔn ho wɔn ho wɔn ho
Wɔ May 24,2021 mu no , wɔbɔɔ obi tuo saa ara bere a adwowtwafo tow hyɛɛ Koforidua so kɔɔ Ayaresa Kukuran kwantempɔn a ɛwɔ Apuei fam mantam mu no .
Adwowtwafo no twaa kwan bɛyɛ 4:30 wɔ Barfuor Nta ntentenso bi a ɛbɛn Sorkodeya Dwunction a ɛda kwan a Police taa fa kar a wɔde kar sisi so mu no mu .
Sɛnea adwowtwafo a wokurakura atuo a wɔde Ghc50,000 kyerɛ no , wɔfow kar bɛyɛ 20 .
Wɔ April 28,2021 mu no , adwowtwafo bɛtow hyɛɛ Guest Ofie bi so , na wɔtow kyakya wɔ Akyem Kukuran asasetaw a ɛwɔ bɛyɛ 8:00 atifi fam a na wɔde atuo agu so no , wobubuu ahɔhodan no adidibea bi , na woyii Ghc13 fii keteke gyinabea hɔ .
Wɔfaa ɔwɛmfo biako pɛ a anadwo ahobammɔ nipa bi a ɔfaa ne nantin wɔ adwowtwa adwuma no mu de no too ɔfasu ho .
Wɔyɛɛ wɔn a wokunkum wɔn no mu biara ho kyerɛwtohɔ .
BB cartridge a hwee nnim , biako te BBridge so , na wɔasan de nteaseɛnam abiɛsa a ɛwɔ hɔ no agu mu .
Adwowtwafo no nyaa wɔn ti didii mu wɔ dua bi a emu yɛ sum mu .
Adwowtwafo no dii adapɛn abiɛsa bere a dwowtwa a ɛte saa maa Nuhu Yashawu a na wadi mfe 32 a na ɔwɔ Abim Osiem mpɔtam bi a ɛbɛn hɔ no wui no .
Obi san de tuo pirae wɔ adwowtwafo ho asiane a esii Dwoda , April 5,2021 no mu , baabi a mmarima baanan a wokurakura atuo ne sknik nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn tow hyɛɛ Energy Filling adwumayɛbea bi a ɛwɔ mpɔtam hɔ so no .
Ná adwowtwafo a wonnim wɔn dodow yɛ anadwo mũ nyinaa .
Adwowtwafo no yii Motorola telefon a ɛda anadwo Adamu Zakari ,30 , no fii hɔ .
Polisifo no san de nnum (5) duaa a ɛho nni fĩ a ɛwɔ hɔ no sii hɔ .
Nhomasua Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Nhomasua Ho Nsɛm So ne Nsɛm a Wɔahyehyɛ wɔ Assin Kesee Fam Amammerɛ Ho . John Ntim Fordjour ama n'akyerɛkyerɛfo ahu sɛ wɔn yiyedi ho hia wɔn sen aban no .
Sɛnea ne kunu kyerɛ no , nhyehyɛe wɔ hɔ a wɔnam so de Ɔkyerɛkyerɛfo Welfare App bɛkɔ akɔma wɔn a wɔkyerɛ nsɛm ho anigye no .
Ɔsomfo panyin a ɔhwɛ nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔ so no ka sɛ aban no hia aban no kɛse , na ɔka kyerɛ obusuani a ɔda nsow no nyinaa sɛ ommesiesie nsɛnnennen a aba nnansa yi no , na ɔmma hokwan ne nneɛma foforo a ɛho hia sɛ ɔde ntɛmpɛ di ho dwuma .
Sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ na wɔatumi adi akyerɛkyerɛfo ahiade ho dwuma wɔ ɔkwan a ɛfata so no , Adi . Fordjour ayi ɔhaw a wɔn a wɔhwɛ wɔn so no de ba ɔmantam biara mu no adi .
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ Oduruyɛfo Yaw Osei Adutwum a ofi ne pɛ mu yɛ adwuma no bɛboa wɔn ma wɔakɔ so adi nsɛnnennen pii ho dwuma .
Ɛdefa nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfo ho wɔ Ghana Ɔman Akyerɛkyerɛfo Fekuw (GNAT) afahyɛ a wɔyɛe wɔ Portugal , baabi a ogyinaa sum ase kuw no ananmu ho no , John Edim Fordjour bɔɔ ɔkyerɛkyerɛfo no sobo sɛ ɔwɔ ahotoso sɛ aban no betumi adi nsɛnnennen a ɛrekɔ so wɔ fekuw no mu no ho dwuma .
Ná dwumadi a na wɔde di dwuma nso wɔ asɛmti no ase: Akyerɛkyerɛfo Fekuw a Ɛhwɛ Nnipa Ho Nsɛm So; Wɔboa Ma Ɔkyerɛkyerɛfo no Nya Nkɔso .
Ɔdaa no adi pefee sɛ akyerɛkyerɛfo a wɔwɔ ɔman no nyinaa mu no aboa ɔman no sikasɛm mu nkɔso kɛse . Hei a wɔsan maa aban no nyaa ahofama a emu yɛ den de dii dwuma wɔ bere a ɛsɛ mu de kaa yiyedi ho asɛm kyerɛɛ ɔkyerɛkyerɛfo no .
Ɔkyerɛe sɛ n'ani gye ho sɛ GNAT a ɔwɔ wɔn mu no fi wɔn pɛ mu di wɔn ho fɛw . Ɔkamfoo GNAT nnwumakuw a wɔyɛ nnwuma a mfaso wɔ so a na wɔn mu dodow no ara yɛ wɔ Unique Insurance ne Ghana Ayaresabea no nso . Ɔkamfoo GNAT wɔ adwuma a na wɔyɛ de gye wɔn ahome no ho .
Adi . Hom Fordjour maa akyerɛkyerɛfo no awerɛhyem sɛ bere a ɛsɛ mu no , Nhomasua Asoɛe no bɛma akyerɛkyerɛfo 280,000 de wɔn ho ahyɛ ade a ne bo yɛ den a wobegyina so asiesie wɔn yiye no mu .
Ɔkɔɔ akyerɛkyerɛfo nyinaa nkyɛn wɔ ɔman no mu nyinaa , na ɔde nhomasua ho nhyehyɛe a ɛwɔ wiase nyinaa kaa wɔn nsa ho .
Polilisifo panyin bi a wadi mfe 56 a ɔwɔ Pergional Police ahyɛde a ɛwɔ Assindeamm a ɛwɔ Assin South Mantam mu no akyere ne babea a na wadi mfe 36 no .
Bere a Regional Police kway PRO Sgt . Evans Isaace a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ Ɔman Bagua a Ɛhwɛ Wim Tebea Ho Nsɛm So no rekasa akyerɛ Evans Isaace wɔ July 23, 2021 mu no , kuw bi a wofi Complain ne Investitititititititititient Owi Bagua no mu a ɔde mfe anum kyerɛe sɛ ɔne Oduruyɛfo bi a wɔfrɛ no ntam yɛ adwuma mu nhwehwɛmu
Bere a kuw no duu ne babea no nkyɛn no , obi a wadi mfe 36 a wɔfrɛ no Alberta Lanuekor a ɔwɔ amena bi a emu yɛ den mu no hyɛɛ da siesiee ne ho maa ɔyarefo bi a ne ho yɛ hu , na wɔn a wɔyare no twɛnee sɛ wɔbɛkɔ bi .
Wɔkyeree wɔn baanu de wɔn ani kyerɛɛ polisifo adwumayɛbea a na nnuru a wɔde di dwuma ne nea ɛboro saa ka ho .
Nhwehwɛmu bi a EIB Network yɛe wɔ Central Regional Correspondent Yaw Boagyan mu no daa no adi sɛ wɔn a wodi nkra no na wɔyɛɛ wɔn oprehyɛn no .
Sɛnea nsɛm bi kyerɛ no , na wɔayɛ nhyehyɛe a mmara mma kwan sɛ wotu nyinsɛn gu wɔ wɔn awotwaa mu , na ama ebinom awuwu .
Wɔn baanu nyinaa yɛ polisini a wɔrehwɛ wɔn wɔ nhwehwɛmu a wɔyɛ mu .
Nsu yiri faa nnipa baanan wɔ Bomso wɔ Oforikromromriti mantam no mu bere a osu kɛse bi tɔe Yawda , June 2021 no .
Ɔmantam no muni a ɔyɛɛ nhyiam wɔ Bomso elector mpɔtam Isaac Appiah , a osii so dua sɛ asɛm no yɛ nokware no , kuw bi a wɔbɛhwehwɛ hɔ Fida akɔhwehwɛ nkurɔfo a wɔayera no .
Kumasi , Ashanti mantam no ahenkurow adi nnanu a atwam ni wɔ nsuyiri a emu yɛ hu a ɛsɛe nneɛma a ɛfata Ghana cedis no mu .
Saa ara na na Kumasi Kejetia Market no wɔ nsuyiri no fã a ɛwɔ Wukuda , baabi a aguadi foforo no mu nneɛma pii sɛe nneɛma no .
Kumasi Osei Abey Ankum a ɔwɔ nhabannuru mu no panyin ka kyerɛɛ Starr FMM sɛ , Ashanti mantam Correspondent Isaac Bediako sɛ , KMAchnical kuw no betumi ahyia tebea bi a egye ntɛmpɛ wɔ nsuyiri no mu wɔ Kumasi .
MMOFRA , ɔmansin nhyiam no ne boayikuw a wɔyɛ nhyehyɛe no bɛyɛ nhyiam bi a egye ntɛmpɛ . Efi bere a mewɔ Kumasi no , matumi ahu kuropɔn a nsuyiri wom a ɛwɔ hɔ ansa na Currrly reba no , ɛho abehia sɛ yɛbom susuw nneɛma a anibere wom ho , na yentumi mfa nsuyiri no nkɔ mu bio .
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ , sɛ nhyiam no ba awiei a , boayikuw no bɛkɔ akɔhwɛ sɛnea nhyiam no betumi aboa wɔn a wɔn ho akyere wɔn no , na afei wɔahwɛ sɛnea wɔahyehyɛ nhyiam no ntɛm ara .
Nnipa bi a wɔte Effia - Kwesimintsim Municipality ne Sekondi Takoradi Kuropɔn no mu aka nea wɔka no ho nsɛmmɔne .
Ɛno akyi no , adwowtwafo baasa a wɔwɔ Tanokrom , Effia - Kwesimintsim Municipality na wɔkyeree wɔn bere a wosusuw sɛ adwowtwafo bi a wɔwɔ bag bi a sika kɔkɔɔ bi wom a efi ɔbea bi a ɔwɔ hɔ a ɔhwɛ hɔ mu rekɔ hɔ no yɛ nea ɛde ɔdɔ ba .
Nanso , Luck nyaa wɔn ti didii mu bere a wɔmaa wɔn nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn bi a emu yɛ hyew , na akyiri yi , ehu kaa Takoradi Mallfo no , nanso obi a na watumi aguan afi wɔn akwantu no mu mprempren no .
Bystander a ohuu sɛnea asɛm no te no de adwowtwafo a wɔhwee wɔn pasaa no maa polisifo no .
Dapɛn awiei a etwaam no , na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔte Anaji SSNIT borɔn so no de wɔn nna bɔ afɔre sɛ basabasayɛfo kuw a wɔtra mpɔtam hɔ no de wɔn nimdeɛ no kosi anɔpa .
Wɔ Dwoda anɔpa , wɔ June 21, baasa mu no , wɔkyeree motorabae abiɛsa wɔ CCTV so de bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛma obi a wagye din abɛyɛ ɔsahene wɔ Anaji Westline a ɛwɔ Sekondi - Tadidi Metropolis . Aman Atɔe Fam Apodi ne Tadididi Asoɛe a Ɛhaw Adwene a Ɛwɔ Wiase Nyinaa no (Abowidi Ho).
Ɔka kyerɛɛ polisini no sɛ , wɔn a wɔte kar mu no nyinaa nnyaa wɔn ho nsɛm a ɛfata .
Nelson Roland , adwowtwafo bi a ɔde n'ahode rebɛma no kae sɛ kar bi a ɔte ne kwan so bɔ n'akyi bere a na ɔwɔ kar mu no , na bere a ɔyɛɛ n'adwene sɛ obefi kar no akyi akɔpɛ baabi a asɛe no , ɔsan behui sɛ ne iPhone 12 ne nneɛma foforo a ɛsom bo wɔ kar no anim no yɛ simma abien pɛ .
Mmea ne aguadifo bi a na wɔwɔ Koforidua Mfinimfini fam aguadifo a na wɔyɛ Fanteakwa Rural Bankfo a wɔn bra asɛe no de nneɛma foforo a wɔde asie wɔn sika mu ama wɔn .
Wɔn a wɔyɛɛ wɔn oprehyɛn no akɔ Ɔmampanyin Akufo - Addo ne Ɔmampanyin , Alban Bagbin , ne Ghana Sikakorabea aboa wɔn ma wɔasan ayi wɔn nkokorafo no .
Wɔde Fanteakwa Rural Bank a Fanteakwa North Amankwah Atifi fam no sii hɔ afe 2004 , nanso ɛhwee ase wɔ afe 2012 mu .
Ná sikakorabea no wɔ n'adwumayɛbea ti wɔ Begoro ne baa dwumadibea ahorow a ɛwɔ Koforidua , Osiem, Suhum, Anyinam , ne ɔmantam no afã foforo no .
Wobu akontaa sɛ adetɔfo bɛboro 1,000 na wɔde wɔn sika no too mu .
Wɔn a wokunkum wɔn no mu dodow no ara yɛ akuafo , aguadifo , afirikafo , akyerɛkyerɛfo , asɔfo nkumaa , ne wɔn a wɔn ho yɛ den .
Sika a wɔde asie sɛe no de ahokyere baa wɔn a wɔn mu binom wuwui no so bere a ebinom hweree wɔn nneɛma nketenkete no
Ná adetɔfo no dodow no ara wɔ Ghana cedis (HS500) ne Ghana cis (HS27,000,000 (HS27,000) a ne dodow yɛ mpem aduonu anan (HS27,000.00) no ntam .
Wɔyɛɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ ahorow pii ho nhyehyɛe titiriw ansa na afe 2016 no reba a wɔn a wɔtoo wɔn mmonnaa saa bere no rehyɛ wɔn so sɛ wɔnsan nnye wɔn sika no . Ebinom a wɔde wɔn sika maa wɔn no de , ebinom nnyaa bi , nanso afoforo pii nnyaa wɔn .
Bere a nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfo a wɔwɔ Koforidua no , wɔn a wokunkum wɔn , a wɔn dodow bɛyɛ aduonum (20), no kaa mmarahyɛfo no anim sɛ wɔanyɛ nhyehyɛe a ɛne sɛ wobetua adetɔfo ka .
Sɛnea wɔn mu pii kyerɛ no , mmɔden a wɔbɔe sɛ wɔbɛma wɔn sika a wɔde asie no ayɛ nea mfaso nni so bere a wɔbɔɔ wɔn sobo sɛ wontumi nyɛ wɔn nsrahwɛ no ho hwee no .
Elizabeth Amoah , a wadi mfe 72 , a ɔde ne nsa hyɛɛ nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔ mu no , daa no adi sɛ n'atow abatow a ɛto so 2020 no akyi no , sika no betumi ama ne ho atɔ no , nanso efi saa bere no wampene so mpo .
Nkrataa kɔɔ Begoro wɔ afe 2020 mfe no mu kɔsrɛɛ me sika , nanso ntiatiaa no paa me kyɛw , na ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ obetua no ntɛm ara . Ɛyɛ awerɛhow sɛ yɛbɛka akyerɛ wo sɛ , esiane sɛ wɔafrɛ me wɔ abatow no akyi nti , MPANYere a ɔde baa me so no anhaw me .
Obetumi de me GHC12,000 mfe pii a na agye me sika no bi aka ne ho , na wanantew sɛ mmarahyɛ baguani; m'ani gye ho sɛ Mɛma Ɔmampanyin Akufo - Addo ne Ɔkasafo no akasa akyerɛ Amankwah sɛ ɔmmɛka me sika no ho anaasɛ ɔbɛboaboa yɛn ho ano wɔ Jubilefie Ofie no ne yɛn Pafilia sika ho .
Obi a wɔakyere no agu afiase dan bi mu resrɛ Ɔmampanyin Akufo Addo ne ɔkasafo , Kennedy Agyapong a ɔde ne ho gye nsɛm mu ma me , nanso saa kwan yi resa yɛn bɔne . Wɔ po so akwantu yi mu no , me ne me babea no kɔɔ Begoro kɔhwɛɛ MPon no , misui , nea enti a ɛsɛ sɛ yebu yɛn ani gu saa mmoa yi so no .
Aguadifo afoforo pii de wɔn ho hyɛɛ tebea a na ɛyɛ hu a na wɔn aware gu no mu esiane adwumaden a sika kɔkɔɔ a na wɔwɔ no de baa wɔn so nti .
Mmarahyɛ Bagua a Ɛhwɛ Fanteakwa Atifi fam Amankwa Asiamah , a na ɔyɛ Ɔsahene Pa Panyin a ɔhwee ase wɔ sikakorabea a ebubui no muni no ampene so sɛ ɔbɛma mmuae wɔ nhyiam a aba so a aba so no ho
Nanso , bere a na atwam no , na wɔn a wɔafow Nana Akufo Addo Addo Addo no ayera kwan , enti wobubui bere a wɔhwee ase wɔ afe 2012 mu no .
Sɛnea n'anan kyerɛ no , ɛka a wɔbɔ wɔ sikakorabea no yɛ nea wɔn a wodi gua no bɛboro 1,000 a wɔkyerɛkyerɛɛ mu sɛ n'apampamfo no dodow no ara wɔ no .

Esiane sɛ na aban nni hɔ nti , na ɛho nhia sɛ aban no betumi afom dwumadi no so .
Aban mmaranimfo no de asɛm no ho asodi ato Matwhile Mahama so .
Fa w'adwene kɔ nneɛma a atwa yɛn ho ahyia no so
Amanaman Ntam Asɛnnibea a Ɛhwɛ Wim Tebea Ho Nsɛm So wɔ January 2021 mu no bɔɔ ka dɔla ɔpepem 134 , na wɔn ani gyee ho sɛ wɔbɛko atia Ghana Aban no wɔ tumi a Emergency Tumidi Asoɛe no ne GCGP limited betumi de aba no ho .
Wɔde Nuklea Ho Nhoma no hyɛɛ kan Ɔsɛmpatrɛwfo Boaburko ase sɛ anyinam ahoɔden foforo pii a Nuklea no de bae a enti ɔman no hia saa tumi no .
Amanaman Ntam Asennibea no hyɛɛ aban no sɛ wontua Ghana sika mfa mpata bagua no wɔ Panyin a Edi Kan no ho , na wɔne Mobilization , Demobilization , ne nneɛma a wɔkora so wɔ US4,34,86,48,61,,,61, ne anigye a wɔn nyinaa nyae no bom fi afe 2018 kosi bere a woyii sika no .

Ajumko Ojumchiso Community a ɛwɔ Central mantam no mu no ani gye boroo so te sɛ nea po so apata pii aba wɔn asubɔnten [Ochichichiso , NW ] a na anka ɛyɛ nsu a wɔnom ma wɔn no .
Eyi sii wɔ Yawda anɔpatutuutu mu . Sɛnea ɔmanfo kyerɛ no , na ahintasɛm no yɛ nhyira a efi anyame no hɔ .
Akannifo a wɔwɔ mpɔtam hɔ no hwiee nneɛma gui , na wobuee hokwan maa wɔn a wɔte hɔ no sɛ wɔmfa nsie no , na wɔmfa nkɔ fie .
Bere a Wofa Yaw Obosu a na ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ asubɔnten no ano no rekasa akyerɛ Kasapa FMM wɔ ɔmantam no mfinimfini fam no , ehu kaa no sɛ efi bere a oduu beae hɔ na ɔsan gye di sɛ ɛde nhyira brɛ ɔmanfo no .
Sɛnea ɔkae no , wɔde apataa no bi bɛkɔ gua so akɔtɔn . Saa ara na apataa no puei wɔ asubɔnten no ho no , matumi de mmofra aduonu anan ayɛ adwuma de atɔn ade wɔ Mankesim , Kasoa , gua so .
Esiane sɛ biribi a ɛte saa ansi wɔ Ajumako Ochiso Community Ajumako Ochiso Community mu nti ,
Saa bere no ara mu no , wɔn a wɔte hɔ no bi nso de asɛm no kɔdan Fisheries ne Aquaculture sɛ wɔmmra mmɛboa wɔn ma wotumi de apataa no kɔ gua so .
NNEƐMA a wɔde pɛtro ayɛ no wɔ adwuma a wɔyɛ wɔ Ajumako Ochiso Community no mu wɔ ha , enti ɛbɛma yɛatumi afa sika ahwɛ yɛn mma yiye ma wɔahwɛ wɔn nhomasua ne yɛn fie . Enti yɛfrɛ atumfoɔ sɛ wɔmmra mmɛboa yɛn ma yɛatumi adi nsɛnnennen a yɛrehyia wɔ Ajakochi Community no ho dwuma .
Ajum Ojumchiso South Maxwell Mensah Nhyiam no san de asɛm no kɔdan Fisheries ne Aquaculture ne aban no mufo a wɔboa ɔmanfo no ma wotumi hwɛ ma wotumi yi mpataa pii wɔ asubɔnten no mu ma wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ hɔ .
Odwumayɛni a Onim Adwumayɛ Ho Adesuabea a ɛwɔ Nana Amoasi VII, no de afiri bi a ɛwɔ Ɔmampanyin Soropɔn , Onyankopɔnfred Dame , reka ne ho asɛm sɛ ɔyɛ obi a n'ani nnye ho sɛ ɔbɛbɔ adwumakuw bi a wɔfrɛ no Ghana dɔla ɔpepem170 no ho ban afi adwumakuw bi a wɔfrɛ no Ghana , The Generation CompGCGGG (A) no ho .
Wɔ nsɛm a wobisabisaa Nana Amoasi VII wɔ Morning Star da a ɛto so Yawda ho mu no , ɔkaa Attorney Soafo no ho asɛm kyerɛɛ Ghanafo nea enti a wamfa dɔla ɔpepem170 a ɛka no anto gua wɔ bere koro mu no .
Ná hokwan wɔ hɔ a yɛde bɛkɔ akɔsrɛ asɛm no , na yɛpawee sɛ yɛde Covid - 19 ne abatow bedi dwuma de ayi yɛn ho ano . Ná Attorney
N'asɛm no baa awiei bere a Asɛnnibea a ɛwɔ London no powee asɛm bi a efi Ghana a etia US dɔla ɔpepem 170 a ɛwɔ tumi a apamfo wɔ mu , Ghana Power Generation Company (GCGP) de too gua no .
Sɛnea London Asennibea no kyerɛ no , Ghana aban no antumi amfa January 26, 2021 a ɛyɛ Amanaman Nkabom Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Amanaman Ntam Mmara So (UNCITRAL) Tribunal no ansi gyinae .
Asennibea a ɛwɔ Wukuda , June 8, no ampene so amma Ghana aban no amfa ne ho ansi hɔ sɛ ɔde teaseɛnam a emu yɛ duru no besi hɔ , na ɛno na ɛmaa ɛyɛɛ den maa wɔn sɛ wobesiw ano .
Aban no nam ne mmaranimfo Dfred Dame so bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔde wɔn nsa bɛhyɛ abatow a ɛto so 2020 no akyi , na AWURADE no antumi anyi wɔn ho ano ntɛm ara , nanso London asɛnnibea no buu wɔn fɔ .
BERE a Charles Kimmins QC ne Mark Tushingham gyinaa asɛnnibea no anim no , ɛhɔ na wɔkyerɛe sɛ Ghana aka akyi dodo sɛ ɔreko atia .
Ná Ghana de Khawar Qureshi QC a ofi Serle Court and Volter Fietta adi dwuma mfiase no akɔ so akora Omnia Strategy so .
Ná Ghana nso gyina hɔ ma adwumayɛbea ti ne Amofa & Partners a ɛwɔ Accra no .
John Beechey a kan no na ɔyɛ Amanaman Ntam Asɛnnibea no Ɔmampanyin no guamtrani no maa Arbitration Asennibea no sow abadiakyiri , na Amf Albert Fidjoe , Ghanani bea bi a ɔde ne ho hyehyɛɛ adesuakuw bi a emu yɛ den , na ɔde n'ani kyerɛɛ Amerika dɔla ɔpepem 170,
Wɔ U.134.35 mu no , U.35 na wonyaa sika a wodii kan de tuaa ka no , na ɛno ankasa yɛ US dɔla ɔpepem 69.36.9.36 a edi kan , na ne bo yɛ US5.49 , na ne bo yɛ dɔla ɔpepem 9.4, US.4.6.6.6 na ne dɔla ɔpepepem32,8 .
US $614,353.86 a na ɛwɔ ribun mu no nso bo yɛ den ma ɔman no , na ɛmaa US dɔla ɔpepem3 no bo yɛɛ den maa wɔn a na wɔtɔ USUSUSUSUSUSUW ho no , na ɛmaa mmara kwan so no , wotuu sika a efii Mmepɔw no mu wɔ nnaka no mu no .
Nea ɛka ho ne sɛ , Ahenkora Boayikuw a wɔkamfo kyerɛe sɛ wɔmfa wɔn nsa nhyɛ apam no ase no nni nnyinaso a ɛfata a ɛbɛma wɔatumi aka sɛ na nsoromma no betumi de dɔla ɔpepem 118 pɛ asi hɔ wɔ bere a wɔhyɛɛ da kunkum wɔn ho no .
Bere a woyii amanneɛbɔfo no fii Ghana no , wotuu wɔn ani sii apam no so , na wɔkae sɛ adanse a edii ansa na ɛreda adi no kyerɛ sɛ wɔwɔ tumi krataa a ɛmaa Blue Ocean Site a Kpone - Tataman a Ɔmantam Nhyiam no hyɛe wɔ August 15, 2017 no sii .
Kyakyatow [ Ɔman Asoɛe ] a ɛhwɛ adansi ho nsɛm so no ntumi nsesaa nhyehyɛe biara , a nea ɛka ho ne Energy Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Adwumayɛ So , a nea ɛka ho no gyina hɔ ma adansi ho mmara foforo a ɛte saa no , mma kwan sɛ wobesisi adan foforo no ,
Sɛnea Oduruyɛfo Ahenkorah [Energy Exnergy Nsɛm Soafo panyin kyerɛ no , bere a dwumadi no rekɔ so no , wɔyɛɛ nhwehwɛmu foforo a wogyinaa so yɛɛ kyerɛwtohɔ no , ɛda adi sɛ bere a Oduruyɛfo Ahenkorah [Energy Adwumayɛ Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Ɔmanfo Nsɛm So yɛe no , ɛkae sɛ wɔn ani nnye Ɔman Bagua no gyinaesi no ho bio .
Wɔ Britania mmara ase no , na aban no wɔ nna 28 a ɛsɛ sɛ osi gyinae a emu yɛ den .
Omnia Strategy , Britania mmarahyɛ bagua bi , de asɛm no too gua , na ɔsrɛe sɛ wɔmma kwan mma wɔmfa nna 56 nsie .
Nanso , asennibea no de March 8, 2021, too gua sɛ Aban no ntutu akwan mfa nsiw gyinae a Asɛnni Bagua no sii no ano wɔ January mu . Nanso , aban no de bere tenten bi sii hɔ de kosii April 1, 2021, ansa na ɛrefi ase . Saa bere yi , Britania mmara foforo a ɛwɔ Volra Fietta no , na ɔwɔ akwankyerɛ fi aban no hɔ .
Mmara no a na ɛyɛ adwuma sɛ amanaman ntam mmara a wɔahyira so wɔ wiase nyinaa no mu biako pɛ no kyerɛkyerɛɛ mu sɛ Ɔmampanyin panyin , Yebeah Dame , nkutoo na woguu no asu wɔ March 5, na wɔde ahyɛde a emu yɛ den a ɛne sɛ egyina hɔ ma Ghana nna 10 akyi no maa wɔn .
Nanso asɛnnibea no ampene asɛm no so wɔ June 8, 2021, no so . Ɛkae sɛ na anoyi no nyɛ nea ntease nnim , na na ɛyɛ mmerɛw sɛ obi de ne ho bɛhyɛ mu .
Ɔtemmufo a odi anim no antwentwɛn ne nan ase .
Ɔtemmufo no kae sɛ bere a aban no twentwɛnee ne nan ase no , aban no antumi anyɛ adwuma yiye , na wɔanyɛ no hwee bio , efisɛ nea ɛto so abien a wɔde too gua no bae akyi nna 38 , na nna 27 ne nna a edi kan wɔ asase ase no akyi no , Wiase Nyinaa Ntĩmu (Ayare) bɔɔ amanneɛ .
Ɔkae sɛ sika a na sika wom kɛse a na ɛwɔ hɔ bere tenten a wɔde yɛ adwuma no ara nnɔɔso .
Ɔtemmufo no kae sɛ , esiane sɛ na wɔmfaa Attorney Mmarahyɛ Bagua no nguu mu kosii March 5 nti , aban no antumi anyɛ ho hwee .
Fa w'adwene kɔ nneɛma a atwa yɛn ho ahyia no so
Amanaman Ntam Asɛnnibea a Ɛhwɛ Wim Tebea Ho Nsɛm So wɔ January 2021 mu no bɔɔ ka dɔla ɔpepem 134 , na wɔn ani gyee ho sɛ wɔbɛko atia Ghana Aban no wɔ tumi a Emergency Tumidi Asoɛe no ne GCGP limited betumi de aba no ho .
Wɔde Nuklea Ho Nhoma no hyɛɛ kan Ɔsɛmpatrɛwfo Boaburko ase sɛ anyinam ahoɔden foforo pii a Nuklea no de bae a enti ɔman no hia saa tumi no .
Amanaman Ntam Asennibea no hyɛɛ aban no sɛ wontua Ghana sika mfa mpata bagua no wɔ Panyin a Edi Kan no ho , na wɔne Mobilization , Demobilization , ne nneɛma a wɔkora so wɔ US4,34,86,48,61,,,61, ne anigye a wɔn nyinaa nyae no bom fi afe 2018 kosi bere a woyii sika no .
Ná ɛsɛ sɛ Ghana Aban no tuaUS dɔla 309,87.7.4 wɔ guasodeyɛ no ho ka , na wɔde US,000,000 ka US,000,000 ho , na wɔde US,000,000 a ne bo yɛ US.7,308,77, no gu mmara kwan so guasodeyɛ mu , na wɔbɔɔ ho ka wɔ adanse a edi mu no ho , na wɔde US,30
Wɔbɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔahohoro abofra bi afi Sawaba wɔ Kumasi wɔ Wukuda anwummere a osu tɔ wɔ Ashanti mantam mu ahenkurow mu no akyi .
Ná abofra no ne n'awofo retu kwan wɔ tricycle bi mu , bere a woduu nsuyiri bi a ɛmaa n'asen no mu trɛwee no .
Sɛnea amanneɛbɔ kyerɛ no , wɔn a wɔtete mpɔtam hɔ no tu kɔtraa hɔ sɛ wɔrebɛbɔ awofo no ho ban , nanso bere a nsuyiri no hohoroo abofra no ho no , wɔanhu no .
Wohuu akokoaa a wɔahoro no amu a wɔde di dwuma no sɛ biribi a ɛnyɛ den koraa . Bere a osu retɔ no , ɛyɛ den ma awofo no sɛ wɔde Sawaba kwan no bedi dwuma . Awifo no ho dwiriw wɔn araa ma wohuu nea enti a odcle no bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ ɔde ɔkwan a ɛmaa akokoaa a wɔfrɛ no Abirer no wu no dii dwuma .
Amanneɛbɔ foforo nso ka sɛ Ɔmampanyin Akufo - Addo a na ofi Upper East mantam mu reba no penee so wɔ nsuyiri no mu .
Idrisu Adams alias Koomi , a Ashanti Regional Police Command kyeree no wɔ robɔt ahorow bi a agye din mu no , Polilililisifo bɔɔ no tuo wɔ ɔkwan bi so sɛ obegyae ɔhwɛ a mmara ma ho kwan no .
Ná asɛm no ho hia , na wɔkyeree no June 2021 kosii polisi adwuma titiriw bi mu .
Wɔ June 2021 mu no , bere a polisifo bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wobeguan no , ntɛm ara na wɔde no kɔɔ mmeae a ɔde ne nsa ato hɔ no .
Wɔde asɛm no kɔɔ St . Martins Ayaresabea a wɔbɔɔ no sobo sɛ wawu no .
Polisifo no kae sɛ wɔn ani abere rehwehwɛ n'ananmusifo a wotu wɔn fo sɛ wɔmfa wɔn ho nhyɛ mu denam Police Station a ɛbɛn wɔn no so .
Polilisifo no san maa ɔmanfo no awerɛhyem sɛ wɔwɔ ahofama sɛ wobesiw nsɛmmɔnedi ne akodi ano , na wɔkɔɔ ɔmanfo no nkyɛn ne wɔn yɛɛ biako .
Ɔmampanyin DCOP Opare - Addo (rtdo) a ɔwɔ National Security Ayaresa Ho Nsɛm Dwumadibea no ama yɛahu nneɛma pii a ɛkyerɛ sɛ bere bi a atwam no na wɔfrɛ no Ashantiion Regional Security Asɛnni Bagua no .
Sɛnea Kan Dapaah kyerɛ no , bere a mmɔden a wɔbɔe sɛ wobenya Coordinator no akyi kwan bere a wokum no akyi no , ɛho behiae sɛ wotu no .
Ɔsɔfo panyin no ka kyerɛɛ Starr News sɛ NPP kataa no so sɛ kuw bi a wɔn ho yɛ den , Delta Force , a wɔtow hyɛɛ no so wɔ wɔn tebea no mu sɛ ɔnyɛ wɔn ho hwee wɔ ɔmantam no mu no .
Nanso , bere a ɔman no ahobammɔ ho somfo no fi South Dayi MP Rockson - Naelson Dafeamekpo hɔ rebua nsɛmmisa no , ɔkyerɛkyerɛɛ mu sɛ mmarima a wɔafom wɔn no yɛ ɔman ahobammɔ .
Nanso , wankyerɛ nea enti a ɛsɛ sɛ wokunkum Owura Opare - Addo wɔ tebea no mu no ase .
Wɔde mfe abiɛsa yɛɛ adwuma sɛ Ashantison aban dwumayɛni panyin wɔ mfe abien a edi kan a wofii ase yɛɛ adwuma wɔ January 5, 2018 mu no akyi .
U.S . aban dwumayɛni bi too nsa frɛɛ no baa dwumadibea a ɛhwɛ ɔman no ahobammɔ so no so . Bere a wɔde DCOP Ore - Addo kaa ne nhyehyɛe no ho asɛm no , wotuaa n'ahotoso no ka kyerɛɛ no wɔ February 19, 2021 mu sɛ ɔmpaw obi a ɔmmɔ ne ho ban wɔ ɔsom adwuma no ho .

Ɔde kaa ho sɛ , sɛ DCOP Opare - Addo ka n'adwumam panyin no ho a , ɔnkasa ntia no , na saa ara nso na me nso mesom sɛ ɔman bammɔfo a ɔsom no wɔ ntua a emu yɛ den a wɔde baa ne so no ho . Saa ara nso na ɛnyɛ ɔman no mu ahobammɔ ho ɔsomfo a efi polisifo hɔ no na wɔde wɔn ho hyɛ mu .
Kyakyatow bɛpɛ sɛ yenya ɔpɛ sɛ yɛbɛhwehwɛ asɛm no mu na DCOP Opare - Addo de asɛm no akɔ asɛnnibea .
Bere a Iain Walker , ne Ɔsahene Panyin a ɔwɔ EIB Network Nabenasi Rebenasi a wɔsan frɛ no Bola Ray a ɔwɔ Wednesday no reka Britania Ɔpanyinpanyin a Ɔhwɛɛ Ɔmanfo Panyin So no ho asɛm no , ɔkaa nsɛm bi guu kyenkyenkyee bi a wɔde kyinkyinii mmɔnten so a ɛne Ɔhene Bɔe no mu .
Ná ɛsɛ sɛ nea ɔhwɛ hɔ no ma nea ɔhwɛ adwuma no so no hu nea ɔpɛ sɛ ohu no wɔ ɔkwan a agye din so no . The Waabiur fii ase fi beae bi a agye din wɔ New Town ne Wama a ɛwɔ Nima no biako ase .
Polisifo a wɔwɔ Adeiso a ɛwɔ Apuei Fam Region no de atuo anan a emu yɛ duru a ɛtotow ntoatoaso ne hama aduɔson ason a efi kar bi a wɔde anhwea ayɛ mu na ɛyɛ mpaboa .

Wɔbɔɔ ɔkasatiafo a ɔto so abien a wɔfrɛ no Alhassan Zakari no tuo wɔ nan benkum so bere a otuo biriw no .
Wɔkyeree nnipa baanum a na wɔwɔ hɔ no pasaa , de wɔn guu wɔn kar mu , na wotuu wɔn kɔɔ beae bi a wonnim hɔ .

Anɔpa 4:20 no , Adeiso Police no kyeree wɔn a wɔbɔɔ wɔn sobo no .

Nnipa a wɔbɔɔ wɔn sobo no maa Bail
Koforidua Circuit Asennibea no gye toom sɛ nnipa baanum a wɔbɔ wɔn sobo no ka ho bi ne Abuakwa , a wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔyɛ Ɔman Ahobammɔ a Ɛwɔ Ayaresa a Ɛwɔ N'anim no , na wɔbɔɔ wɔn sobo sɛ wɔyɛ nnipa a wɔn dodow si 200,000 no .
Wɔn a wɔbɔɔ wɔn sobo no yɛ Nanafuor Sarpong , Nana Barima Twum Tarbiade II , a abien no nyinaa hyɛ Abuakwa ase no .
Wɔn a aka no ne Yonatan Martey , a na ɔyɛ Ahenkorag , ne afoforo a na wɔdɔɔso no .

Wɔde amanneɛbɔ a Ɔmampanyin Akufo - Addo de mae no baa dapɛn biako pɛ wɔ ahobammɔ ahyehyɛde bi akyi bere a wɔmaa asraafo a wofi Burkina Faso ntua a emu yɛ den baa wɔn so no .
Ná ɔne Bawku Naba nhyiam bi rekɔ n'awiei wɔ Upper ɔmantam no mu .
W' ɔmantam a wowom wɔ Burkina Faso no ma ɛda adi sɛ ebetumi de wɔn ani asi awudifo ne nsɛmmɔnedifo a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔsɛe yɛn asetra na wohu amane wɔ Ghana no so .
Ɔkɔɔ so kogyinaa asase mfonini so , Naba , na wunim akwan a aban no fa so hyɛ ahobammɔ nhyehyɛe a ɛwɔ ha no mu den , na ɔbɔ yɛn ho ban fi amumɔyɛfo ntua a efi Burkina Faso no ho .
MMOFRA A WƆDE TETETETETE TETE WO TETETE SƐ SƐ WOBETUMI Agyina amumɔyɛsɛm ho ɔsɛmpɔw no ano wɔ ha
Saa bere yi ara na Bawku Naba , a ɔyɛ Kusaug Traditional Bagua no So panyin no , Asigiri Abugrago Azoka II , kae sɛ Ɔsɔfo Panyin ne Nnipa a Wɔwɔ Kusaug Tradia Ayaresa, na nokwarem no , Ghanafo nyinaa ani sɔ Ɔmanpanyin Kuw a ɛwɔ Nanaowfo Akuado - Asdo no
Ɔmampanyin Akufo - Addo a ɔrebɔ mmɔden sɛ obedi ne nkonimdi no ho dwuma no de Ghana botae no bɛto wo nsa mu denneennen wɔ (4) mfe anan a edi hɔ no mu , na ɔka kyerɛɛ Bawku Naba sɛ Ɔmampanyin panyin no abɔ mmɔden sɛ obegye saa dibea a ɛyɛ den no atom . Me yam a anka mopɛ sɛ mubetumi ahyira mo nyansa so , na ama moanya akwahosan pa .
Nhwehwɛmu bi a Child Rights International yɛe no daa no adi sɛ mmofra 11, 288 a wɔadi fi mfe 12 kosi 17 no mu ɔha biara mu 55 na wɔpɛ sɛ wofi Ghana kɔ mmeae a ɛhɔ yɛ frɔmfrɔm wɔ amannɔne .
Wɔn mu ɔha biara mu dubiako kae sɛ wonni ahotoso sɛ wɔbɛtena ɔman no mu anaasɛ wobefi hɔ .
Wɔn a wobisabisaa wɔn nsɛm no ɔha biara mu 55 kae sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wotu kɔ ɔman foforo so , bere a 11% te ɔman no mu anaasɛ wogyaw wɔn hɔ no . Wɔn a wobisabisaa wɔn nsɛm no mu dodow no ara gye wɔn ahome , nhomasua ne asetra ho gyinapɛn a eye sen biara , bere a wosusuw nea enti a wobefi ɔman no mu bere a wɔyɛɛ nhwehwɛmu bi wɔ asɛm no mu no .
Bere a wobisabisaa wɔn nsɛm no mu ɔha mu 80 sɛ ebia wɔwɔ adwempa wɔ ɔman no daakye ho no , nhwehwɛmu no kae sɛ: Wɔn a wobisabisaa wɔn nsɛm no mu ɔha biara mu 80 kae sɛ wɔwɔ Ghana ho adwempa wɔ mfe 20 a edii hɔ no mu . Nnipa a wobisabisaa wɔn nsɛm no mu bɛboro baanu .
Mmofra bi a wɔwɔ Ashanti mantam no mu ahunahuna wɔn sɛ wobesie Lighthouse Chapel Amanaman Ntam Nhyiam no baa dwumadibea a ɛwɔ ɔmantam no mu no wɔ ɔkasa a emu yɛ den bi a asɔre no Asɔfopɔn Dag Heward - Moills a wodii kan yii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ Ashan Monarch Monafum Otumfutum Otumi Tutum no .
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔkasa a wɔakyere agu nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔ so no kyerɛ nkɛntɛnso a ɔhene a ɔwɔ tumi no wɔ wɔ ne manfo ne ne mpɔtam hɔ no .
Sɛnea kuw no kyerɛ no , ogumadifo a wagye din no ahu tete kannifo no , na ɛsɛ sɛ ɔyɛ ade kɔ akyiri sen sɛ ɔbɛpa ne bɔne ho kyɛw .
MMOFRA rehwehwɛ afotu pa afi Bishop Dag hɔ wɔ nnɔnhwerew 48 mu .
Bishop Dag Heward - Moills apa kyɛw wɔ ɔkasa no ho .
Wɔ kyɛwpa mu no , Preacher no kae sɛ: Me werɛ howee yiye sɛ asɛm bi a mekaa ho asɛm wɔ nhyiam bi ase bɛyɛ mfe 20 a atwam ni no , wɔayi me afi nsɛm a ɛka ho no mu , na nnipa a wɔadi kan aka sɛ wɔde wɔn ho bɛto yɛn asɔre ahorow so denneennen wɔ Kumasi no atwe wɔn ho afi ho
Kyakyakakakaka kyerɛ Ne Hojesty Otumfuo Nana Osei Tutu II esiane sɛ ommu ade nti , anaa odidi no atɛm anaa opira no nti . Yɛsrɛ wo , gye anansesɛm a emu dɔ a mewɔ ma nsɛm a mekaa ho asɛm no tom .
National Democratic Congress abɔ Ɔtemmufo Panyin Kwasi Anin - Yeboah no mua , na ɛka n'adesrɛ a ɔde kɔmaa Mmarahyɛ Bagua a Ɛhwɛ Mmara Kwan So no ho asɛm , sɛ ɛyɛ mmɔden a wɔbɔe sɛ wɔbɛka kasafĩ .
Wɔbɔ amanneɛ sɛ Oduruyɛfo Ayine kae sɛ Asɛnnibea Kunini no antumi amfa ayaresa ho ahyɛde no anni dwuma bere a wɔredi asɛm no . Wogye di nso sɛ wama ahiasɛm a wɔn a wɔde wɔn ho hyɛ mu daa no di ho dwuma bere a asɛm no rekɔ so no .
Ɔde nsɛm no too gua wɔ asɛm bi a Asɛnnibea a Ɛhwɛ Sikadwuma Ho Nsɛm So (CDD) ne KNUST .
Adesrɛ a Ɔtemmufo Panyin no de maa GLC no hyɛɛ mmarahyɛfo no nkuran sɛ wɔnhwehwɛ nsɛm no mu yiye na wɔmfa ahotew a ehia no nni dwuma .
Bere a Johnson Asiedutia a ɔyɛ Ɔsahene no Kyerɛwfo Panyin no muni retwe adwene asi Dwoda , so no , ntɛm ara na Ɔsrɛɛ Bolgatangatanga Supɔw no so .
Ɛsɛ sɛ yenya nsɛm asekyerɛ nhoma mu ahotoso a emu yɛ den wɔ asɛnni baguafo no mu , na ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔhyɛ yɛn . Hwɛ mpɛn dodow ara a woate sɛ asɛnnibea bi reka akyerɛ obi sɛ Ɔsahene Motoquito de atemmu reba , na mmom mesrɛ no sɛ ɔmmɔ wo kɔkɔ sɛ mma wonka ho asɛm sɛ Owuraiedu Nkeusi a agye din no .
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ , te sɛ aban mmaranimfo anaa ɔpanyin no , wontumi nsɔre ntia .
Owura Asiedu Nketia nso bɔɔ Atɛntrenee Panyin no sobo sɛ ɔde n'ani asi Mmaranimfo a wɔwɔ NDC no so , na ɔfrɛɛ no sɛ ommegyae abayifo no .
Kwasi Yebeah a ɔwɔ din pa no nni ho adanse biara a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɛkame ayɛ sɛ mmaranimfo a wɔabɔ wɔn amanneɛ wɔ Mmarahyɛ Bagua Kɛse no asenni bagua no boayikuw a Ɔtemmufo Panyin no de Ɔtemmufo Kɛse no Atɛntrenee Atɛntrenee Atɛntrenee Ma Maa Yebeah mae wɔ NDC no ho nnansa yi no nyinaa ani abegye Mmara a Ɔhwɛ Nnipa Ho Nsɛm So no ho araa ma enti ɔbɔɔ ne tirim sɛ obegye Mmara no atom .
Ghana anya ɔman a ɛtɔ so abien a asomdwoe wom sen biara wɔ Afrika wɔ Mauritius akyi wɔ afe 2021 Wiase Nyinaa Asomdwoe Index no amanneɛbɔ a Asuae a Ɛhwɛ Sikasɛm ne Asomdwoe Ho Nsɛm So (IEP) no mu .
Wiase Nyinaa Asomdwoe Index no ne wiase nyinaa aguadi nhyehyɛe a ɛde asomdwoe ba . Sɛnea aman 163 mu ahofadi ne nsasesin te no , saa amanneɛbɔ yi da no adi sɛ ntease a ɛkɔ akyiri sen biara a wɔanya wɔ asomdwoe mu , ne ɔkwan a wɔbɛfa so anya aman a wɔpɛ asomdwoe no adi .
Wɔ aman 163 mu no , Ghana nyaa nkɔanim ɔha biara mu nkyem 38 wɔ wiase no mu . Ghana bɔɔ hu wɔ 1.715 mu , na ɛno gyina hɔ ma akwan abien a ɛtwe ade fi po so hyɛn gyinabea a edi kan no mu .
Mauritius, ɔman a asomdwoe wom sen biara wɔ Afrika no nyaa nkɔanim ɔha mu 28 wɔ wiase nyinaa , nanso Botswana nyaa nkɔanim a ɛto so abiɛsa wɔ Afrika ne 41st wɔ wiase nyinaa . Ná nnipa 146 na wɔwɔ Togo , Uganda, The Republic of Congo ne Cameroon .
Iceland da so ara yɛ ɔman a asomdwoe wom sen biara wɔ wiase no mu fi afe 2008 . Efi afe 2008 no , New Zealand, Portugal , ne Slovenia rekɔ n'awiei .
Afghanistan yɛ ɔman a asomdwoe wom sen biara wɔ wiase nyinaa afe a ɛto so anan no mu , na Yemen , Syria, South Sudan , ne Iraq . Burkina Faso yɛɛ nhyehyɛe a ɛsõ sen biara wɔ Wiase Nyinaa Asomdwoe Index 2021 mu .
Sɛnea amanneɛbɔ no kyerɛ no , nnipa a wɔwɔ Sub - Sahara Afrika no mu fã nyaa basabasayɛ ho osuahu bi nnansa yi . Wɔn a wɔte Namibia no nyaa basabasayɛ a ɛsen biara wɔ wiase no mu ɔha biara mu 6 .
South Sudan da so ara yɛ ɔman a asomdwoe wom sen biara wɔ ɔmantam no mu ne aman a wɔpɛ asomdwoe no mu biako , ɛmfa ho nkɔanim a wɔanya wɔ asomdwoe mu wɔ afe 2021 mu no .
Nea ɛmaa asomdwoe mu yɛɛ den sen biara wɔ ɔmantam no mu ne Burkina Faso . Eyi ne ɔman biara mu ahokyere a ɛsen biara . Aban mpanyimfo no sii gyinae sɛ wɔbɛsɔ nkurɔfo ani na wɔde wɔn ho ahyɛ asraafo akuw a wɔyɛ asraafo a wɔko tia basabasayɛ wɔ hɔ no mu .
Amanneɛbɔ no sii so dua sɛ ɔmanko kɔɔ soro ɔha biara mu 10 wɔ wiase nyinaa , na ehon ntini a ɛwɔ asase ase no na ɛde ba . Ná nnipa 14,871,,871 na wɔyɛ wɔn ho basabasa , wɔkasa tiae ne basabasayɛ a wɔayɛ ho kyerɛwtohɔ wɔ wiase nyinaa wɔ 2020 mu .
Amanneɛbɔ no kae sɛ na Covid yɛ ɔman bammɔ kuw bi a wɔde wɔn ani asi amammuisɛm ne ɔman mu basabasayɛ a ɛbɛba daakye so . Ɛkaa dodow a wɔrehwɛ kwan no ho asɛm kɛse .
Eyi nyinaa akyi no , nnipa a wɔwɔ wiase nyinaa no mu bɛboro abiɛsa te nka sɛ wɔwɔ ahobammɔ anaa ahobammɔ nnɛ sen nea wɔyɛe wɔ mfe anum a atwam ni no . Wɔn a wɔkyerɛ sɛ basabasayɛ ama wɔanya nkɔanim kɛse no ayɛ kyerɛwtohɔ a mfaso wɔ so fi bere a wofii ase kunkum nnipa wɔ afe 2008 mu no .
Index no ma ɛdaa adi nso sɛ , sɛ wɔkyekyem pɛpɛɛpɛ a , wiase nyinaa asomdwoe 0.07 resɛe wɔ afe 2021 Wiase Nyinaa Asomdwoe Index no mu . Ɛwom sɛ nneɛma a ɛresɛe no sua koraa de , nanso eyi ne bere a ɛto so akron wɔ mfe 13 a etwa to a wiase nyinaa asomdwoe asɛe no mu .
Amanneɛbɔ no de kaa ho sɛ afe a etwaam no , aman 87 yɛɛ nhyehyɛe pa wɔ asomdwoe mu , bere a aman 73 yɛɛ nhyehyɛe a emu yɛ den . Aman abiɛsa a wɔyɛɛ ho kyerɛwtohɔ no anyɛ yiye koraa no wɔyɛɛ nsakrae biara wɔ wɔn sikasɛm mu . Mediterranea Supɔw ne Afrika Atifi fam (MENA) ɔmantam no mu no , anyɛ yiye koraa no , ɛhɔ yɛ baabi a asomdwoe wom , na ɛwɔ aman anum no mu .
Ɔmantam a asomdwoe wom sen biara wɔ wiase no mu .
Ɔmampanyin bi a wɔfrɛ no Nana Addo Dankwa Akufo - Addo ama Ghanafo anya awerɛhyem sɛ wobehu nsakrae bi wɔ n'adwumam hɔ .
Sɛnea ne ho kyerɛ no , mfe anan a edi hɔ no betumi anya Ghanani mpapahwekwa no asetra so nkɛntɛnso pa .
Nea ɛhaw adwene kɛse ne sɛ mfe anan a edi hɔ no , wobehu nkɔso kɛse a aba wɔ Ghanafo asetra mu no , ɔmampanyin a ɔhwɛ adwuma no so no maa mmuae no bere a ne panyin no kɔɔ Nigeria no .
Owura Akufo - Addo a ɔrekasa akyerɛ Imo Man so Amrado a ɛwɔ Nigeria Owelle Rochas Anayo Onicha, Monday de kaa ho sɛ: " Ghanafo sika a wɔde asie no asɛe ade kɛse wɔ mfe abiɛsa anaa anan a etwaam yi mu , nanso yɛde nsi ne ahokeka kari pɛ sɛ yebetumi ama ɔman no anya anigye .
Ɔmampanyin panyin a ɔboroo Ɔmampanyin , John Dramani Mahama wɔ abatow a aba nkyɛe mu no wɔ nnansa a ɔrekɔsra Nigeria , baabi a obenya ngo a wɔde ngo gu mu no , Muhammu Buhari .
Owura Akufo - Addo nso maa Imo State amrado a ɔne Afrika Atɔe fam aman abien no ntam abusuabɔ mu bɛyɛ den wɔ ne dwumadi no ase .
Ɛho hia sɛ yehu abusuabɔ a ɛda aman abien no ntam no . Ɛho hia sɛ abusuabɔ a ɛte saa no da adi wɔ yɛn nkurɔfo ne yɛn akannifo no ntam . Wɔde ahotoso ma yɛn manfo sɛ yɛrebɔ mmɔden adi wɔn haw ahorow ho dwuma na yɛaboa wɔn ma wɔanya nkɔso wɔ wɔn asetra mu .
Ɔmampanyin John Dramani Mahama aka Joseph Whittal ho asɛm sɛ Ɔsahene a Ɔhwɛ Hokwan a Nnipa Wɔ ne Administ Atɛntrenee (CHRAJ) no .
Ná Owura Whittal de ne nsa ahyɛ guasodeyɛ bi ase wɔ Flagstaff House Benada awia .
Owura Whittal ayɛ adwuma sɛ CHRAJ , efisɛ bere a kan no na ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ Lauretta Vivian Lamptey no , Ɔmampanyin no yii no fii hɔ bere a ɔhweree sika no .
Ɔmampanyin no apaw M . Josephine Nkrumah sɛ Ɔman Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Nhomasua Ho Nsɛm So panyin (NCCE).
Ms . Nkrumah , a na ɔyɛ guamtrani wɔ adwuma no mu Owuras . Charlotte Osei, a na ɔyɛ adwuma no panyin no na ɔyɛɛ adwuma a ɛmaa Ɔmampanyin Electoral Adwuma no de ne nsa hyɛɛ ase wɔ July afe a etwaam no mu .
Bere a Ɔmampanyin no poo NP kannifo Nana Addo Dankwa Akufo - Addo no akyi adapɛn kakraa bi no , wɔpaw wɔn .
Wobebue ɔmampanyin no January 7, 2017 .
GN Health Insurance Company Ltd , Groupe Nduom nnwumakuw 75 no mu biako afi ase reyɛ adwuma wɔ Ambulance Dwumadibea wɔ Ghana .
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ nnwuma foforo bi de ayaresa a egye ntɛmpɛ bɛma wɔn a wɔn yare mu ayɛ den no .
GN Health Ambulance Service no nso de nnuruyɛ ne ahude ahorow a wonya fi mu ba no ho mmuae ma .
GN Health Issah Adam guamtrani kae sɛ , Ɔmampanyin ne CEO a ɔwɔ Groupe Nduom , Oduruyɛfo Papa Kwesi Nduom , ne afei Senior Vice Ɔmampanyin , Yvonne Nvonneduom , ne Direduom , nyinaa de nsakrae kɛse aba ɔsom adwuma a ɛde Groefo yiyedi ba no mu .
Ɔka kyerɛɛ adwumakuw bi a wɔhwɛ akwahosan ho nsɛm so dwumadi so a ɛyɛ hu foforo a ɛwɔ Groupe Nduom nkaedum no mu no . Nea ɛka ayaresa ho no , wɔde Ambulance Ɔsom yi reto gua sɛ wonwie Ayaresa Dwumadibea a Ɛwɔ Ayaresa Mu no na ama adwumayɛfo kuw no anya mfaso wɔ Ɔman Kɛse no mu ne Ɔpanyin Adwumakuw no mu no so .
Sɛnea akontaabu kyerɛ no , nnipa bɛboro ɔha biara mu 60 na wowuwu wɔ Ghana , na nea efi mu ba ne sɛ wontumi mfa mmoa mmea a wɔwɔ labour ne akwanhyia mu a wɔde wɔn kɔ ayaresabea a ɛfata no . Experts gye di sɛ wobetumi de tebea a ebetumi akowie owu mu ama wɔ ɔkwan a ɛfata so , ne bere a ɛsɛ mu , te sɛ nea G Health Ambulance Service hwehwɛ sɛ wodi ho dwuma no .
MMOFRA betumi ahwɛ ahu sɛ yɛatete EMTs (Emergency Medical Techniciafo) ne Ambulance Drivers a wɔatete no yiye na wonim nea ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ wɔ tebea a emu yɛ den mu no .
Wɔde nnɛyi nnwinnade ne nneɛma a wobetumi de adi dwuma wɔ tebea a egye ntɛmpɛ mu ne bere a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔhwɛ ayarefo no yiye . Yɛsrɛ wo , hwɛ hu sɛ ɛnyɛ kar nko na ɛwɔ hɔ , na mmom ɛnyɛ kar nko ara na ebetumi ama wɔn nsa aka nneɛma a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔhwɛ so yiye no , na ɔde ka ho .
Wɔde nnwinnade pii a wɔde hwɛ wɔn a wɔahwɛ wɔn ansa na wɔatumi ahwɛ wɔn no na esiesie Ambulancefo no . Wɔde nnwinnade a ɛho hia na
Aban no ahyɛ bɔ sɛ wɔbɛsa wɔn a wopirapirae wɔ Yawda mmere mu no yare a emu yɛ den wɔ La .
Wɔasi nnipa baasia awuwu wɔ mframa a ano yɛ den a esii baabi a ɛbɛn Trade Fair Centre a ɛwɔ Accra no mu bere a nnipa bɛboro 20 apirapira wɔn ho no .
Akwahosan Soafo Alex Segbefia kɔsraa wɔn a wɔn ho akokwaw wɔ Ɔsahene, Police ne ayaresabea 37 a na wɔn a wɔrehu amane no bi nya ayaresa no bi no , ɔkamfoo nnuruyɛfo a na wɔhwɛ wɔn a wɔn ho akokwaw no .
Kyakyatow ho dwumayɛni no ama ada adi pefee sɛ nea ebefi saa asɛm yi mu aba no nyinaa bɛyɛ nea ɔman no ka , enti yɛpenee so maa emu daa hɔ pefee kyerɛɛ wɔn a wɔhwɛ ayarefo yi ne wɔn a wɔsa wɔn yare no , ne wɔn a wɔhwɛ ayarefo no , sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔbom yɛ ntɛm siesie wɔn ho , na wɔbɔ mmɔden sɛ wobedi wɔn a wɔhwɛ ayarefo yi ho dwuma .
Mmoawa a wunim wɔn a wɔhyew wɔn no , ɛho hia sɛ wohohoro wɔn ho bere nyinaa , na wohohoro wɔn ho gu nnuru a ekum yare mmoawa ne yaw a emu yɛ den ho , sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɔyarefo biara ho bɛtɔ no .
Saa bere yi nyinaa no , Ɔmampanyin John Dramani Mahama aka akyerɛ Ghanafo sɛ wɔmmɔ mpae mma wɔn a wowuwu wɔ Yawda nna mu no na mframa a ano yɛ den bɔ wɔn .
Wɔ Facebook Fida no , ɔmampanyin a na ɔwɔ akyirikyiri no de ne Facebook ɔfasu no kyekyee wɔn a wohuu amane no werɛ .
MMOFRA a wɔwɔ mmusua a wokunkum wɔn nnɛra da mu mframa a ano yɛ den a ekunkum ɔyare mmoawa a wɔsɛe ade wom mu no , kɔ so bɔ mpae ma wɔn a asiane no ato wɔn no .
Wimhyɛn gyinabea bi a ɛbɛn Ghana Amanaman Ntam Aguadi Asoɛe a ɛwɔ Accra no ama nnipa baanum a wɔhyew wɔn kunkum wɔn .
Sɛnea ogya no kyerɛ no , ogya no ka nneɛma a ɔman no yɛ de kyerɛe ne aguadi no afã bi nso .
Sɛnea Veronica Koomson kyerɛ no , adɔkɔdɔkɔdɔkɔdɔkɔsɛm ne ogya a ɛwɔ hɔ no tumi ko tiaa blaze a emu yɛ den a ama nkurɔfo de wɔn ho ahyɛ akodi mu no .
Wɔde ogya a ano yɛ den retoto ogya ano , na yɛreyɛ biribiara a yebetumi de ahwɛ so . The Armed Forces ogya ho akofo no wɔ ha dodo , na wɔreyɛ nea wobetumi biara de ahwɛ ahu ogya yi yiye , na wɔde amanneɛbɔ a efi Ghana Ɔman Fire Ɔsom Adwuma (GNFS) Prince Bill - Anady ka kyerɛɛ K Starmineor sɛ Owiawiawiawia .
Koomson kae sɛ mframa foforo bi a ɛwɔ baabi a ɛbɛn ogya no betumi akɔ ogya mu , sɛ odumgyafo no antumi ansiw tebea no ano a .
Nanso , Billy - Anaglatey kae sɛ ontumi nsi so dua sɛ asiane biara a ebefi mu aba no yɛ biribi a wosusuw ho mprempren ne sɛ ɛbɛma ogya no mu ayɛ den sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ogya no ntumi nkyere ade foforo a wɔde asie no .
Wonnim nea ɛde ɔtopae no bae . Abibifo a wɔwɔ mpɔtam hɔ nyinaa wɔ hɔ a anyinam ahoɔden a wɔde yɛ anyinam ahoɔden ho adwuma no bi wɔ hɔ .
Onipa biako awu wɔ akwanhyia bi a esii anadwo a etwa to wɔ Ekumfifiti wɔ Ekumfiti mantam a ɛwɔ Mfinimfini fam no mu .
Nea wawu no , Nigeriani bi , hweree n'asetra bere a kar akwanhyia a na ɔrefa mu no maa ogya tɔɔ kwan no so no .
Ná lɔre a wɔde Cola asoa no fi Mankessim rekɔ Nigeria .
Sɛnea wɔn a wohui kyerɛ no , kar no kɔɔ wura bi a ɛbɛn hɔ mu bere a nea wawu no hweree ne ho no .
Nanso , wimhyɛnkafo no bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ obegye hyɛntiafo foforo baanu a na wɔwɔ kar no mu ansa na wɔrehu ogya no , na wɔhyew ofirikafo no kosii sɛ ogya no duu baabi a
Mprempren wɔn baanu resa wɔn yare wɔ Cape Coast mantam ayaresabea .
Akyiri yi , wɔn a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ Ghana Fire Ɔsom Adwuma no mu no duu baabi a wɔrekodi nneduafo no so .
Asiane no de asiane ahorow a ɛyɛ hu a asisi wɔ mpɔtam hɔ bɛboro adapɛn abien a etwa to no ba .
Da koro pɛ a etwaam no , nnipa 15 na wowuwui wɔ ɔkwan koro no ara so wɔ Yutong bɔs ne Sprinter ntam .
Ahempɔn bi a wɔwɔ Gafo mpɔtam hɔ ama Gbese mantse, Nii Ayibonte , a wɔde nnanson na ɛyɛɛ n'ahengua no .
Ɔsɔfo Panyin no bo fuw Gbese a odii kan ka kyerɛɛ no ansa na afe 2016 reba no .
Nii Abonte hyɛɛ n'ahengua ho bɔ sɛ sɛ ɔmampanyin John Mahama po so a , ɔbɛtow aba no .
Nii Abonte ka kyerɛɛ ne manfo ansa na abatow no reba sɛ akyinnye biara nni ho sɛ Mahama betumi atow aba .
Nanso bere a Oakfo a kan no na ɔyɛ Oakfo Komamni no de n'akongua bɔɔ n'akongua mu no ,
Nii Abonte anka nea na ɔpɛ sɛ ɔyɛ bere a Nana Akufo - Addo dii nkonim kɛse no ho asɛm .
Ɔsɔhwɛfo Panyin a ɔrehyɛ n'ahengua ho nkuran no nso apirakuru dedaw bi .
Wokunkum mmea baanu , na afoforo bɛboro 12 pirapirae , bere a kar bi antumi annyina Daboya - Busunu kwan a ɛwɔ Northern mantam no mu no so , na polisifo asi so dua sɛ ɛyɛ Benada anwummere no .
Ná akwantufo 14 a wɔde wɔn rekɔ Daboya a efi Sawla rekɔ Nkramofo ayeforohyia ase no wɔ kar no mu .
Gonja mantam no mu polisini panyin , ASP Seidu Wemeh , kaa kar no ho asɛm sɛ bere a oduu baabi a ɛbɛn Daboya mpofirim no , nnipa 2304 - 15 na wokoduu baabi a ɛbɛn baabi a ɛbɛn baabi a kar kwan no rekɔ no , wɔbɔɔ wɔn tuo kunkum wɔn amonom hɔ ara .
Ná wɔn a wɔawuwu no yɛ mmea mpanyimfo a wɔadi fi mfe 42 - 45 .
Sɛnea ASP Seidu kyerɛ no , polisifo da so ara hu nea ɛmaa nsõ no bae , nanso sɛnea ASP Seidu kyerɛ no , polisifo bɛhwehwɛ ofirikafo no adwene mu ahwɛ sɛ ebia mmosa ho asɛm wom anaa .
Ɔde wɔn a wopirapirae no mu dodow no ara kɔɔ amantam ayaresabea a ɛwɔ Tamale no mu , na wɔn mu biako pɛ na wɔhwɛɛ no wɔ Damongo .
Accident a ɔwɔ Daboya - Busunu kwan no so no da nsow wɔ ne suban bɔne no ho .
Ɔmanfo no ampene amanneɛbɔ a ɛka sɛ eyi ne bere a edi kan a wɔayɛ akwanhyia ho kyerɛwtohɔ wɔ ɔkwan a wɔabu ani agu so no so .
Wɔka sɛ akwanhyia dodow no ara mfata .
Oduruyɛfo Matthew Opoku Prempeh , a ɔyɛ adwuma no aka sɛ Aban no reyɛ adwuma wɔ Ghanafo a wɔn ho tew na wɔwɔ ahoɔden te sɛ nuklea ahoɔden nhyehyɛe a edi mũ , te sɛ nuklea ahoɔden ne ahoɔden foforo a wobetumi de adi dwuma ho .
Ɔkae sɛ nneɛma pii wɔ hɔ a ɛkyerɛ sɛ nuklea ahoɔden dii dwuma titiriw bi wɔ anyinam ahoɔden ho awo ntoatoaso a na ɛredɔɔso wɔ mfiridwuma mu no mu .
WƆhwɛ kwan sɛ anyinam ahoɔden mfiri a etumi nya ahoɔden foforo no bɛkɔ so anya nkɔanim kɛse wɔ nuklea ahoɔden mu , ade a ɛho hia a ɛwɔ hɔ nnɛyi ahoɔden mu no , ɛno ara nso ne anyinam ahoɔden a ɛsõ sen biara a ɛde anyinam ahoɔden ba awo ntoatoaso a ɛwɔ asase ase no mu , na wama carbon awo ntoatoaso a ɛwɔ fam no ɔha biara mu 40 anya nkɔanim .
Ɔtwee adwene sii Amanaman Ntam Adwumayɛkuw amanneɛbɔ bi a ɛfa anyinam ahoɔden nhyehyɛe a ɛho tew ho so , na ɔkyerɛe sɛ , sɛ wɔamfa nuklea ahoɔden anni dwuma a , ɛbɛyɛ den kɛse sɛ wobetumi anya ahoɔden de asiw nyarewa ano , ne ahobammɔ a enni ano .
Oduruyɛfo Opoku Prempeh kaa eyi ho asɛm denam ɔkasa bi a ɔkenkanee maa ne ho so no , wɔ Swedenfo Forum a wɔwɔ Ghana no fam no , Nuclear Power Programme a ɛwɔ Accra no .
Wɔ asɛmti no ase: Nsɛm Ho Amanneɛbɔfo Ahyehyɛde a Ɛhwɛ Pintinn: Nea Ɛbɛba Daakye Ho Nyansahu a Ɛwɔ Akyirikyiri ne ɔkwan a wɔbɛfa so de patrotro a emu dɔ a ɛwɔ Ghana no adi dwuma de sum ase kuw bi a wɔfrɛ wɔn " Ghana Indust (AGI), a ɛne Nuklea Tumi a Ɛwɔ Ghana (AFE).
Oduruyɛfo Opoku Prempeh kae sɛ , anyinam ahoɔden ho nhyehyɛe a wɔyɛ de siesie anyinam ahoɔden ho no nso bɛsɛe mmeae foforo , te sɛ kar a wɔde tu kwan , ne nneɛma foforo a atwa yɛn ho ahyia a wɔsɛe no .
ƆBARIMA bi a wɔfrɛ no Ghana ka sɛ: " Ghanafo de wɔn ani asi atumfoɔ a wɔwɔ dibea a ɛkorɔn so , na wɔde wɔn ho to wɔn ho so , na ama wɔatumi de tumi foforo a wɔwɔ ho ɔsɛmpɔw no aba . "
Ɔkae sɛ , sɛ yesusuw nokwasɛm ahorow a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu no ho a , ebetumi ama yɛanya ahoɔden foforo a ɛho tew .
Nuklea a wɔde di dwuma foforo a wɔde di dwuma no mma carbon anyinam ahoɔden a enni ano nko na mmom ɛma wonya mfaso pii wɔ asetram bere a ɛrenyin no , na mfe 60 a edi hɔ no , afifide no bɛkɔ so ayɛ adwuma no .
Ɔkaee sɛ , wɔ afe 2007 mu no , kan Ɔmampanyin John Agufuor de boayikuw bi sii hɔ , na Ɔbenfo Daniel Adzei - Bekoe na ɔyɛɛ adwuma de hwehwɛɛ nuklea ahoɔden a anka ebetumi de nuklea ahoɔden adi dwuma sɛ ade foforo a ɛde tumi a ɛboro nnipa de di dwuma no
Ná eyi rekɔ so bere a na Ghana wɔ tumi no .
Nea ɛbɛyɛ na ɔman no anya mfiridwuma mu nkɔanim kɛse no , ɔkae sɛ , akyiri yi , nniso ahorow no aboa mmɔden a wɔbɔe sɛ wɔbɛma ɔman no anya ahoɔden de ayɛ nuklea ahoɔden ho nhyehyɛe no .
Eyi ama wɔawo NPG no ma wɔabɛyɛ Ghana asase a edi kan a wɔde nuklea ahoɔden yɛ adwuma no so hwɛfo .
Ɔkaa NPG Board , a na Owura Fred Oware da nkongua ase no ho asɛm sɛ , ɔde n'ani sii nneɛma a ɛho hia a ɔde bɛbɔ ɔman no ho ban so , na ɔde nsi ne ahokeka yɛɛ nhyehyɛe a ɛfa nuklea akode a wɔsɛe no ne nnwuma a wɔyɛ wɔ ɔman no nyinaa mu ho adwuma .
Nea ɛka anyinam ahoɔden a ɛwɔ anyinam ahoɔden mu ho no , Asomfo no kae sɛ , wobetumi de mfiri a wɔde di dwuma wɔ akwan pii so - nuklea mfiri nketenkete te sɛ mfiri a wɔde yɛ nneɛma nketenkete a wɔde yɛ nuklea ahoɔden ho nhwehwɛmu a ɛkɔ akyiri te sɛ mfiri a wɔde di dwuma no , ama wɔn a wɔyɛ nuklea ahoɔden pii no atumi anya ahoɔden a wɔde di dwuma no bi .
Ɔkae sɛ: " Saa ara na mfiridwuma ho nimdeɛ a wɔanya no reda adi wɔ akwan foforo pii so , na ɛreboa nkɔso a ɛyɛ nwonwa a wɔanya no .
" Nnwumakuw , mfiridwuma , ne nnwuma a wɔyɛ wɔ nuklea ho mfiridwuma mu reyɛ adwuma wɔ wiase nyinaa , a Ghana nso ka ho .
Efi bere a edii kan de too gua bɛyɛ mfe anan ni no , tow a wotua wɔ mmosa ne nneɛma a ɛnsɛ ho no adɔɔso .
Efi afe 2018 mu no , nnipa ɔpepem 28.5 na wotuaa tow , na wɔn dodow nyaa nkɔanim koduu ɔpepem 38.5 wɔ afe a edi hɔ no ne ɔpepem 70.2 wɔ 2020 mu , na wɔn a wɔhwɛɛ adwuma no so no dodow nyaa nkɔanim bɛyɛ ɔpepem 90 wɔ afe 2021 mu .
Ghana Adienue Tumidi (GRA) no kae sɛ na ɛyɛ Aduan ne Beverages Association of Ghana (FABAG) ne wɔn a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ baabi a wɔte no adwumayɛbea hɔ na ama wɔatumi atua ɛka a wɔbɔ wɔ wɔn nhwehwene so no ho ka .
Ghanafo nhoma tintim adwumakuw , Buck Press , ne ne hokafo DelaRue , Britania adwumakuw a wɔbɔ wɔn ho ban no , na ɛyɛ wɔn asɛyɛde sɛ wotintim towtua ho nhyehyɛe no ma GRA , bere a Streamline Res , a ɛwɔ Tema Portugal no , nnwumakuw a wɔyɛ adwuma no boa nnwumakuw a wonni ahoɔden a wobetumi akora ankorankoro a wɔwɔ hɔ no .
Owura Kwabena Awuah Anto , a ɔhwɛɛ saa nneɛma yi so no kae sɛ , apoo a ɛwɔ Tax Stamp at the GRA no , Owura Kwabena Apau Awuah Anto , Mana a ɔyɛ adwuma no mu panyin no betumi atew amimdi ne afɛfɛfɛfɛfɛfɛfɛde a ɛwɔ hɔ no so .
Bere a Owura Anto rekyerɛ bere a wɔrekɔhwɛ tow ho dwumadibea a ɛwɔ Tema Portugal no , kuw bi a wɔfrɛ wɔn Group Limied (GCGL), a ɛwɔ hɔ Yawda a etwa to no , ɔkae sɛ GRA Asoɛe no de wɔn ankasa Adwumayɛbea kɛse no ho nneɛma a ne bo yɛ den no maa wɔn .
Nea na ɛka GGCL kuw no ho ne Managing Directorfo , Owura Ato Afful , ho no , Owura Kobby Asmah; Director , Marketing ,, Franklin Sowa , ne Mrror, Ms Doreen Hammon .
Ná kuw no wɔ Tema , na na wɔn ani sɔ nkɔso a wɔanya wɔ towtua nhyehyɛe a emu yɛ den no mu , na na wɔne GRA no bɔ nkɔmmɔ wɔ ɔkwan a wɔbɛfa so atu anammɔn foforo so .
Owura Anto ka kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ , sɛ wɔhwe ase a , wɔbɛtew aguade ho dawurubɔ so , na wɔhwɛ hu sɛ nneɛma a ɛfata nkutoo na wobetumi ayɛ wɔ gua so na ama ɔmanfo anya akwahosan ne ahobammɔ .
Saa ara na ɔkae sɛ , nhyehyɛe no betumi ama wɔanya awerɛhyem , na ama wɔatumi ayɛ adwuma a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ wɔ agodibea ne wɔn a wɔyɛ aguade ho no yiye denam tow ahorow a ɛfata a wobetua so .
Owura Anto kae sɛ: Yɛayɛ nhwehwɛmu bi wɔ Tema Adan a ɛwɔ hɔ no mu , ne mmeae 13 a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu , baabi a yɛwɔ adan a wotu biriw wom no , yɛmmɔ ka biara sɛ yɛbɛhwehwɛ baabi a wɔde nneɛma gu .
Ɔkae sɛ , bere a ɔrehwɛ adan no so no , ɔde nsɛmti bi a ne bo yɛ den te sɛ nsõ a wɔde hohoro nkyɛnsee mu , akuturuku , ne nneɛma a ne bo yɛ den te sɛ shrinkraps guu mu bae
Ɔkyerɛe sɛ bere a woyii adwuma no wɔ 2018 mu no , aban no sii gyinae sɛ ɔde asram asia mpomma no bɛkɔ akɔma wɔn a wobetumi atwe wɔn ho afi ho no , nanso na ɛno de , nea Ɔsahene no de ahyɛde ama no ne sɛ wɔmfa wɔn ho nhyɛ mu , na wɔpɛ sɛ wotua wɔn ka .
Owura Anto kae sɛ , nhyehyɛe no na ɛbɛkyerɛ sɛ ebia GRA no bɛbɔ ho ka anaa wɔbɛbɔ ka wɔ ho .
aman te sɛ Kenya, amumɔyɛfo tua wɔn ho ka anaa wɔde nneɛma no gu baabi a wotu kwan kɔ amannɔne kɔtɔn no .
Ghanafo hyɛ towtua ho nhyehyɛe ho nkuran de asodi no to aguade a ɛho ka no so anaa nea ɔyɛ aguade no so .
Wɔ aman pii mu no , nnwumakuw a wɔyɛ saa no wɔ nnwinnade a wɔde yɛ adwuma wɔ wɔn adwumayɛbea ahorow mu no , Owura bi a wɔfrɛ no Anto kae sɛ .
Owura Anto kyerɛkyerɛɛ mu wɔ nsɛnnennen a ohui nnansa yi a ɛtwentwɛnee ne nan ase , a ɛmaa osu kɛse bi tɔe no mu no ho , mu sɛ wɔanyɛ Tema Adwumayɛbea ahorow no anyɛ apo akɛse bi , na mmom nnipa a wɔde wɔn ho hyɛɛ mu bere ne bere mu nkutoo no .
Nanso , ɔkae sɛ , apo akɛse , na wɔbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛkwati ɛka a wɔbɔe wɔ ho no , mpɛn pii no , wɔde wɔn nneɛma no kɔmaa mmeae a wobetumi atwe wɔn ho afi ho no , tebea bi a ɛmaa wɔpenee wɔn ho so na wɔtwentwɛn wɔn nan ase .
Saa ara na ɔkae sɛ , bere a obi sesaa n'anan wɔ ɔsom adwuma no mu no , ɔtwentwɛnee ne nan ase .
Nanso , mfiridwumayɛfo yɛɛ adwuma wɔ mfiri no so sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobetumi afa nhama foforo no .
Owura Asmah ka kyerɛɛ GRAs no wɔ ne kasa no mu sɛ onkosua nkrataa a bere bi na wɔde kɔ aguadidan mu no ho ade nkɔ akyiri .
Ɔkae sɛ , nhomasua a ɛkɔ akyiri ho hia , efisɛ ɛbɛdaa adi wɔ baabiara , na ɛbɛsan nso ama nnipa annya bere tiaa bi wɔ nhyehyɛe no mu .
Ɔkamfoo GRA mpanyimfo ne wɔn a wɔhwɛ adwuma so no , Streamline Resources , efisɛ ɔyɛɛ nneɛma bi de dii nsɛnnennen no ho dwuma .
Ɔkae sɛ , GCGL no ne GRA no bɛbom ayɛ adwuma a egye mmɔdenbɔ kɛse no , na ama wɔanya towtua nhyehyɛe a emu yɛ den no mu nhumu .
Kyakya gye di sɛ eyi ne bere a ɛfata sɛ GCGL ne GRAfo yɛ nsakrae kɛse wɔ ɔmanfo yiyedi ho , sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a yebetumi anya biribi a yɛbɛtɔ afi Owura Asmah a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ baguam no hɔ .
Nhwehwɛmu Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Nneɛma a Atwa Yɛn Ho Ahyia Ho Nsɛm So (IES) aka sɛ fango bo bɛyɛ den bere a ɛrefififi ase no . Asɛm a IES kae no kyerɛe sɛ na nneɛma bo yɛ den wɔ mmeae a ɛwɔ mpomma ase no .
Wɔ June 2021 mu mpomma a edi kan a nnwumakuw a wɔyɛ fango wom (OMCs) no fã kɛse no ara mu no , fango ho nneɛma a wonyae no boroo so ɔha biara mu 3% . Based wɔ
Sen Petroleum, Benab Oil , Cash Oil , Goodness Oil , ne Frimps Oil na wɔtɔn pɛtro a anyɛ yiye koraa no na ɛwɔ gua no so , sɛnea IES di gua no .
Wɔ mpomma ase no , sɛ wɔkyekyem pɛpɛɛpɛ a , amanaman ntam benchmark Brent hweree $73.98 , a egyina hɔ ma ɔha biara mu 4.05 fi $7.10 a atwam no .
Saa mmoawammoawa yi ama wɔanya nneɛma pii a wɔatumi ayɛ wɔ COVID - 19 a Delta a egu ahorow wɔ Europa afã horow no mu , na ɛde kɔkɔbɔ a emu yɛ den a ɛfa asɛm bi a esii wɔ United States ho ama .
Bere a edi kan wɔ mfe abien mu no , Brent bo kɔɔ soro koduu dɔla 775 wɔ mpomma a ɛrefififi ase
Eyi te saa titiriw , bere a kar ne wimhyɛn akwantu kɔ so dɔɔso no .
Wɔkyerɛ nso sɛ nneɛma bo a akɔ soro wɔ Brent no fi abotan a ɛwɔ Europa no afã bi , Asia , ne Mediterranea Supɔw no so no .
Wɔhwɛ kwan nso sɛ July 1st OPEC no besisi nhyehyɛe a wɔayɛ ama August no ho gyinae , bere a yɛkɔ July ɔsram no mu no .
Kyakyatow ne gasoil aboɔden abo , a wɔayɛ ho mfonini wɔ Standard ne Poor asase so nyinaa no , da no adi sɛ ɛka a wɔbɔ wɔ wiase nyinaa no (petrol) ne gasoil (beesel) ntam nsonsonoe a emu yɛ den wɔ bere no mu no .
Gasoline huu amane kɛse bi a eduu ɔha biara mu 3.47 kosi $694.78 wɔ mpomma mu fi $67.45 .
Kyakyatow bo kɔɔ soro koduu ɔha biara mu 3.53 wɔ $97.30 biara a wokohyiaa ɛmo a ne bo yɛ $576.89 no mu .
Sikasɛm mu Ayaresa a IES de too gua wɔ Foreign Exchange (sex) gua so no da no adi sɛ cedi no kuraa ne nnyinaso no mu pintinn , na ɛda so ara gyina GH7 kosii US dɔla 7 .
Wɔ South Africa no , wɔde nneɛma foforo aka Nigeriafo ho ma wɔakora so wɔ aman a woduu Nigeria no mu . Esiane sɛ na covid19 Delta no gu ahorow wɔ South Africa nti , wosii gyinae no .
Mprempren , wɔabara akwantufo a wɔkɔɔ South Africa wɔ nna 14 a atwam no sɛ wɔnkɔ Nigeria .
Ɛsɛ sɛ Nigeriafo ne wɔn a wɔte hɔ a wofi South Africa ba no nya dapɛn ason ntam
Brazil ne Turkey nso rebobɔ din .
Kaaka Moha a wokunkum no yɛ awerɛhow na ɛyɛ yaw .
Me tiri ne m'abusua , na ebia ne kra Bɛtra Asomdwoe Mu .
Nanso , ntɛm ara na ebinom afi ase retwe nsateaa a ɛrebɔ wɔn ho ban wɔ nniso a ɛwɔ hɔ nnɛ no ase aka anidaso a ɛne sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔma ɔman ba yi ho kwan no ho asɛm .
Eyi nso nyɛ papa , efisɛ ɛmma kwan mma wɔnyɛ nhwehwɛmu a ɛfata .
Sɛ mehwɛ sɛnea aban no yɛɛ n'ade wɔ nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔ mu nhwehwɛmu a wɔyɛe wɔ Ɔman no mu ho a , minnye nni sɛ ebia ɔman no betumi ayi saa awudi yi afi hɔ , ɛmfa ho mpo sɛ minim no yiye sɛ , wɔ yɛn amammuisɛm mu no , yɛn ani betumi agye biribiara ho , a nea ɛka ho ne sɛ yɛbɛdan ɔbarima ne ɔbea bi akɔ ɔporɔw mu .
Aban mpanyimfo no hyiaa wɔn a na wɔrebɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛbɔ wɔn ho ban .
Akyiri yi , anyɛ yiye koraa no , nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfo baanu, kyerɛkyerɛɛ nea aban reyɛ de atew ɔman no so no mu .
Nanso , anini no wɔ nniso no mu , na wɔnam wɔn ho a wɔfrɛ wɔn a wɔyɛ agyidifo no so ka kyerɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnhyɛ wɔn den no so na wommisa wɔn nea edi kan .
Afei , yɛwɔ yɛn Polisi Ɔsom Adwuma no , a na yɛtaa bɔ mmɔden sɛ ɛbɛhaw adwene a wɔn a wɔyɛ katee no wɔ sɛ wɔbɛda no adi no , na yɛde Covid ho nkyerɛkyerɛmu a ɛho nhia no di dwuma , bere a na wontumi nsiw basabasayɛfo kuw no kwan anaasɛ wontumi nsiw wɔn kwan wɔ Sir mu no .
Eyinom bɔ mmɔden biara sɛ wɔde ɔman no bedi dwuma ɔkwammɔne so , a nea ɛka ho ne sɛ wobekum obi a ɔyɛ katee , na ɛyɛ mmerɛw , nanso wobetumi anya adwenem naayɛ esiane sɛ wonni nsu ho adanse a edi mu nti .
Ɛsɛ sɛ yehu nso , na ɛnsɛ sɛ yebu yɛn ani gu nokwasɛm a ɛyɛ sɛ ɛtɔ mmere bi a , yɛn amammuisɛm a ɛyɛ katee no betumi apia ankorankoro a wonni aban no akyi ma wɔayɛ wɔn ayayade a ɛte saa no so , na ama atirimpɔw ahorow a emu yɛ den a ɛde mpaapaemu ba , na ɛma nkurɔfo ani nnye nniso ahorow ho no so .
Bio nso , adanse biara nni hɔ a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ yedi eyi ho dwuma , wɔ Kaaka asɛm no mu .
Nanso bere a yesusuw tebea no ho no , ɛsɛ sɛ yɛyɛ saa wɔ ɔkwan a emu yɛ den so de kata nsɛm a wɔka no nyinaa so .
Wɔ asraafo a wonnim wɔn na wɔmpɛ sɛ wokum nnipa foforo baanu no fam no , mede asɛm no ho asodi to wɔn so dodo .
Ɛsɛ sɛ yɛde wɔn abagye ne ntetee no ho asodi to wɔn so .
Atuatewfo bɛkɔ so ahu amane kɛse wɔ nkaedum no mu esiane ahobammɔ a enni nnyinaso nti , bere tenten a wɔasan de wɔn ho ahyɛ nnwumakuw yi mu no , esiane sɛ wobu wɔn ani gu wɔn so na wɔmfa wɔn ho nto teokrase so nti , sɛ́ ɛyɛ afe 2000 Mobrowa Struggle no , ɛtɔ mmere bi a mebɔ mmɔden sɛ medi dwuma kɛse bi nti , bere a Drummerine
Yehuu ɔkwan a polisifo ne asraafo no faa so dii yɛn ho dwuma bere mpo a na ɛsɛ sɛ wogyina pintinn wɔ honam fam no .
Wɔn a wɔbɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛtow tuo bere a wɔreyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ ahorow no de wɔn ho rehyem
Nea na ɔrepɛ akyerɛ bere a nnipa rehu amane anaa wɔrehu amane
Saa na ɛsɛ sɛ wotow tuo de bɔ nkurɔfo ho ban
Ɔkwan bɛn so na ɔsraani yi san de ne ho gyee nsɛm mu ?
Hena na ɔde ne nkwa too asiane mu na ɔtetee no wɔ asumansɛm mu ?
Nokwarem no , ɔyɛ ɔsebɔ bi a ɛwɔ borɔn bi so , na ɔhyɛ asraafo atade bi a wɔfrɛ nomoufre .
Wɔ mmeae foforo no , mede yɛn kwasafo hokwan no rema nhomanimfo ne Afrika akannifo bi .
Nanso wɔ mfonini no akyi no , wɔretwe adwene asi saa ayayade yi so de abɔ asɛm a wɔka fa Ghanafo ho no agu .
Asɛm no ara ne sɛ , nneɛma bi a aniwa ntumi nhu a ɛda adi wɔ nniso ahorow bi mu ne mmofra no su a yɛde bɔ yɛn ho ban wɔ nneɛma a yɛyɛ de kyerɛ nneɛma a yɛyɛ de kyerɛ sɛ yɛyɛ no ho no , yɛ ɔkwan a ɛyɛ hu a yɛfa so dannan yɛn ho wɔ sɛnea yɛde yɛn nipadua no di dwuma no mu .
Ghanafo yɛ wɔn a wontumi mfa wɔn ho nhyɛ ɔbrasɛe mu
Hwɛ sɛnea nsu a emu yɛ hyew ne ahurututu mu ahoɔdennuru a ɛwɔ nsu no mu no yɛ adwuma
Aban mpanyimfo bi pɛ sɛ wɔde agyiraehyɛde bi a ɛbɛhyɛ yɛn ma yɛabɔ yɛn ho ban kɛse bere a wɔrehwɛ nnipadɔm na wɔne wɔn adi nsɛm no . Aban no betumi nso ama wɔn a wɔbɔ wɔn ho ban no de akokoduru akɔ sukuu na ama wɔasan abɔ wɔn ho ban wɔ ɔkwan bi a ɛbɛma wɔasan abɔ wɔn ho ban akuturuku no ho , na ama wɔatumi ahu hia a ehia sɛ wɔne wɔn ho wɔn ho wɔn ho wɔn ho wɔn ho wɔn ho
Eyi yɛ ade a ɛho hia a wobetumi de atua wɔn ho aka .
Ebia na ɛsɛ sɛ Ɔmampanyin no ankasa de ne ho gye nsɛm mu ma wɔn a wohia awerɛhyem no , na ɔde asomdwoe ne ahotew a etwa to no ba .
Nnwumakuw a wɔbɔ wɔn ho ban no ahwere ahotoso a wɔwɔ wɔ wɔn a wɔyɛn wɔn ne wɔn a wɔyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ no ani so no .
Sɛnea yɛn Asomdwoe Bagua no abɛn no nso ama yɛanya hokwan bi a ebetumi ama Bagua no anya gyidi a emu yɛ den de adi dwuma . Sɛ yɛde saa nsɛnnennen yi to nkyɛn a , ebetumi aboa yɛn , na ɛsɛ sɛ yɛyɛ eyi wɔ bere a ɛsɛ mu .
19 Thomas Amoani a wadi mfe 19 no a owiee Adeiso Presby Akudaarian Senior High School no adesua a Ghana Scholarship Secretariat yɛe no de anisɔ a ɔwɔ ma aban panyin a ɔwɔ Nana Addo Dankwa Aku Addo no .
Thomas Amoani , a onyaa afe a etwaam no afe a etwaam no , ɔde Afrika Atɔe Fam Sukuu a Ɛhwɛ Sigyadi Ho Nsɛm So no maa no ntɛm ara sɛ onkosua ade wɔ Brunel Sukuupɔn a agye din a ɛwɔ London no mu bere a Ɔpanyin a ɔwɔ Ahintariarifo , Owuraley Agumadi mu Abasobɔde no
Abarimaa a wadi mfe 19 , a ofi Abasuae , a ɛbɛn Adeiso ne ohiani bi no besua Economics ne Business Finance ho ade kakra .
Bere a nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfo bi bisabisaa Demoani nsɛm wiei no , Thomas Amoani kaa sɛnea na ɔde n'asɛm kɔ sukuu bɛyɛ kilomita 12 kɔ sukuu no ho asɛm .
Eyi twee n'adwene sii N'asɛmpatrɛwfo Akufo - Addo a ntɛm ara ɔkae sɛ wɔmma no nhomasua a edi mũ no so .
Bere a Ɔmampanyin no yɛɛ nhyehyɛe tiawa bi maa no ansa na ɔresan akɔ baabi a ɛwɔ Scholar Ahintasɛm Dwumadibea hɔ no , ɔkae sɛ ɔhwɛ adwuma a Thomas ayɛ no bɛkanyan afoforo ma wɔabɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛyere wɔn ho denneennen sɛ wobehu nea enti a wɔte saa no .
Metumi ama wɔn awerɛhyem sɛ Scholarship Secrets no wɔ hɔ a wɔde mmoa a ɛho hia bɛma wɔn . Thomases nhwehwɛmu a wɔayɛ no bɛboa afoforo te sɛ ɔno . Na ɛsɛ sɛ mekamfo Ɔmampanyin Aku - Ado sɛ ɔde ne ho gye asɛm no mu ntɛm ara . Owura Aguman kae sɛ: "
Bere a oduu sukuupɔn , Thomas Amoani , a na ontumi mfa n'anigye no nhintaw no , ɔkae sɛ wasiesie ne ho sɛ ɔbɛma Ghana sraani no so atew , na ɔremma ɔman no nhwe ase .
IREstrar a ɔyɛ adwumaden wɔ Registrar no ama manya hokwan a ɛte saa . M'ani sɔ ahotoso a na mewɔ wɔ me ho no paa .
Brunel University London yɛ baguam sukuupɔn mu nhwehwɛmu bi a wɔyɛe wɔ Uxbridge mpɔtam bi a ɛwɔ London, England . Wohuu no 1966 mu , na wɔtoo ne din sɛ Victorian engineer Isambard Kingdom Brunel , no , wɔde sii hɔ sɛ sukuupɔn a ɛto so 93 a etu mpɔn sen biara wɔ wiase nyinaa wɔ mfiridwuma ne mfiridwuma ho nimdeɛ mu , 32 wɔ Europa ahyehyɛde no mu .
Ɔtemmufo Panyin Kwasi Anin Yebeahling nni ɔhaw biara a ɛfa nteɛso a wɔde ma wɔ mmara kwan so samanfrɛfo ne Parlia Mmarahyɛ Bagua a Wɔyɛ ma Bolgatanga East , Oduruyɛfo Dominic Akuritingaine Akuyine a ɔwɔ Ɔsahene Bagua Kɛse (GLC) no ho .
Sɛnea mmaranimfo mmaranimfo ne obi a kan no na ɔyɛ Sebila Mmarahyɛ Bagua no muni kyerɛ no , Owura John Ndebugre , nsɛm a Ɔman Democratic Congress (NDC) ne nnipa afoforo a wɔkasa tia wɔn no ka ho bi na ɛsɛ sɛ wodi ho dwuma , bere a Ayine da adi ansa na Ɔhotefo Bagua Bagua Bagua no Bagua Bagua Bagua Bagua Bagua no (NDC) no .
" Yesusuw sɛ na [Chief Atirimɔden Asɛnni Bagua no yɛ obi a ɔfata a ɛsɛ sɛ onwiinwii efisɛ asɛm a Oduruyɛfo Ayine kae a ɛmaa asɛm yi sɔree no kyerɛ sɛ , ahotoso a na ɔwɔ wɔ ahofadi a na ɔwɔ wɔ asɛnni baguafo no wɔ wɔ ɔkwan bi a wɔfaa so de wɔn adesrɛ no too gua anaa osii ne bo no so .
Ɔtemmufo Panyin no abɔ amanneɛ sɛ mmaranimfo Akuritinga Ayine ka GLC Bagua no Nteɛso a wɔde maa no no ho asɛm sɛ bere a ɔresusuw Ɔmampanyin Election Petitions ne nkɛntɛnso a enya wɔ Afrikafo Dem teokrase so ho no .
Wɔabɔ Oduruyɛfo Ayine sobo sɛ ɔmpɛ sɛ Judiciary no bɛtwe wɔn ho afi ɔkwan a Asɛnnibea Kunini no faa so yii abatow a ɛto so 2020 no ano no ho .
Oduruyɛfo Ayine asɛm no ka sɛ n'asɛm a ɔkae bere a wɔresusuw ho no ne Asɛnnibea Kunini no ahyɛde a wɔmfa nni dwuma , ne bere a wɔkɔ so bu wɔn ani gu n'adesrɛfo no akwankyerɛ anaa mmoa a ɔde ma no so bere nyinaa .
Wɔde nsɛm a emu da hɔ na ɛkasa tia Asɛnnibea Kunini no , Oduruyɛfo Ayine , wɔ nsɛm a ɛte saa a wɔkasa tiaa Asɛnnibea Kunini no mufo a wɔyɛɛ wɔn saa wɔ Apam Dedaw no mu bere a Oduruyɛfo Ayine repapa kyɛw bere a ɔkɔɔ Asɛnnibea Kunini no anim na ogye toom sɛ ɔrekasa tia Mmarahyɛ Bagua no Baguafo Panyin no .
Oduruyɛfo Ayine , a ɔyɛɛ n'ade bere tiaa bi mu wɔ CJ's anwiinwii no ho no kyerɛe sɛ ne nsɛm no nhyɛ atɛntreneefo a wɔtraa ase wɔ wɔn adesrɛ no ho no anuonyam .
Ɔkyerɛe sɛ ne nsɛm no yɛ gyidi pa .
Sɛ́ mmaranimfo no , mewɔ asɛyɛde titiriw sɛ mekasa tia mmarahyɛ adwuma no . Ɛdenam me ntetee ne osuahu so no , mama mafata asen me mfɛfo ɔmamma no mu dodow no ara de wɔn ho ahyɛ atemmu ne nneyɛe mu .
Ɔkɔɔ so kyerɛkyerɛɛ mu sɛ ne nsɛm no wɔ kasakoa a ɛfata mu .
Ɔman Democratic Congress (NDC) a ɛwɔ atesɛm krataa bi mu a wɔko tia amammui mu basabasayɛ titiriw no ka kyerɛɛ Ɔtemmufo Panyin no sɛ onyi ne ho ano wɔ Ayine ho .
Bere a Owura Ndebugre reka dibea a ɛsɛ sɛ Ɔtemmufo Panyin no twe ne ho fi anwiinwii a ɛte saa ho no , ɔkae sɛ , Owura Ndebugre kae sɛ Oduruyɛfo Ayine nka n'anofo no mu biako anaa n'ahokafo no mu biako ho asɛm . Enti Henok
Bere a Owura Ndebugre rebisabisa Graphic Online nsɛm wɔ radio so wɔ Citi FM a egyina Citi FM so wɔ Benada anwummere (June 22, 2021) no , ɔkae sɛ: " Yensusuw sɛ ɔhaw biara nni Ɔtemmufo Panyin no a obebu atɛn no ho .
Bere a Stephen Quarcoo ne Tommy Thompson rekyerɛkyerɛ nea esii wɔ 1996 mu no mu no - saa bere no , Mensah Bonsu tow hyɛɛ ɔtemmufo bi , Abban , ma enti ɔde asɛm no too gua , na afei ɔde Ɔpanyin Panyin no fii hɔ kɔbɔɔ asɛnni baguafo no anim .
Ɔhaw biara a ɛfa CJ anwiinwii ho
" Misusuw sɛ asɛm biara nni Ɔtemmufo Panyin no ho .
Nea ɛka ho bio ne sɛ , na Dominic Ayine yɛ Attory Attortortoreral , na ɔno ne ne panyin no faa nkurɔfo kɔɔ asɛnnibea hɔ saa bere no , na ɔde wɔn kɔɔ aban asɛnnibea hɔ .
Dabi , ɛsɛ sɛ wokɔ asennibea hɔ na wohyɛ wo asɛm no , na woka sɛ woanni fɔ wɔ sobo a wɔbɔɔ wo no ho .
Enti , wɔ ɔkwan koro no ara so no , Ɔtemmufo Panyin no susuw sɛ asɛm no yɛ nea ɛmfata koraa , na ɛho hia no .
Enti wokɔ hɔ , na nsɛm a NDC ne Dr Ayine ankasa reka ho asɛm no nyinaa yɛ nsɛm a ɛsɛ sɛ ɛkɔ so wɔ Ndebugre Boayikuw no mu , a" Owura Ndebugre de ka ho .
Bere a ohui sɛ ɔmpɛ sɛ ɔbɛka mfaso a ɛwɔ so ho asɛm no , ɔkae sɛ afã abien na ɛwɔ hɔ , nanso bere a asɛm no da so ara rekɔ n'anim no , ɛte sɛ nea wo ne no resusuw asɛm no ho , na ɛda so ara yɛ nea woreka ho asɛm akyerɛ no , sɛ wokeka nsɛm bi a ɛmfata bere a woredi asɛm no ho dwuma a , ɛno akyi no , wo ne no hyia .
Sɛ woamfa asɛm no ankɔto asɛnnibea a , wubetumi aka sɛ wo ne no nyɛ adwene , "but ka sɛ . . . Meka sɛ mepɛ sɛ miyi ntoboa a ɛfata no , nea Im betumi ayɛ ara ne sɛ seesei mema bagua no gye tom sɛ esiane amanyɔkuw no nti , ɔno [Dr Ayine ka sɛ ɔpɛ sɛ ɔkyerɛ nea enti a ɛsɛ sɛ mepaw nea mepɛ sɛ mede ma no no .
" NEA enti a ɛsɛ sɛ wokɔ Asuafo Kuw no nkyɛn na woka kyerɛ ɛhɔ sɛ wowɔ hokwan sɛ wuyi wo yam yɛ ade , nanso wuntumi nka sɛ Ɔtemmufo Panyin no ntumi mmɔ no sobo , ɔno na ɔyɛ asɛnni baguafo no ti , na woka sɛ ahotoso a wowɔ wɔ asɛnni baguafo no mu no da adi esiane sɛ wɔyɛɛ no saa nti .
Bere a wobisaa no adwene a ɛne sɛ Ɔsahene no di GLC no anim no , Owura Ndebure kae sɛ wɔn a wodi saa ahyɛde yi so no betumi afoa asɛm no so . Enti na ɔde Ayine rema n'ankasa "
Ɔde Mmarahyɛ Bagua Bagua no dii dwuma wɔ baabi a wɔde mmarahyɛ baguafo no atwe nkurɔfo a wɔwɔ hɔ no aso no , " saa nkurɔfo no atwe wɔn adwene asi wɔn nsusuwii so anaasɛ wɔada hokwan a wɔwɔ sɛ wɔkasa no adi . Sɛ mokɔ a , mobɛtwe mo adwene akɔ Privilege Boayikuw no so .
" MMOA nka sɛ Ɔsahene no yɛ papa anaa bɔne .
Nea mekae ara ne sɛ , ɔtemmufo Panyin no aka asɛm bi akyerɛ me , na nea ɛhaw no ara ne sɛ ɔno na ɛsɛ sɛ onwiinwii no , efisɛ na asɛm no tia mmarahyɛ baguafo no , na ɔno na ɔyɛ asɛnni baguafo no ti , na ɔno na ɛsɛ sɛ ɔde asɛm no kɔ n'anim .
Anwiinwii no kyerɛ sɛ wɔabu wo fɔ , enti ɛsɛ sɛ wokɔ hɔ , na woka nsɛm a woreka no nyinaa kyerɛ wɔn a wo ne wɔn rekasa no , na afei woasi wo bo sɛ wobɛyɛ saa .
Ɛyɛ bere a wokɔ hɔ na adanse bi wɔ hɔ a ɛkyerɛ sɛ wubetumi afi ase anwiinwii , nanso misusuw ho saa bere yi ara mu no , ɛyɛ bere nhyehyɛe na Ill tu Ayine fo sɛ ɔmmɔ mmɔden nkɔhwehwɛ Asuafo Boayikuw no na ɔmfa ne ho nhyɛ mu , na n'ani gye ho sɛ ɔbɛkɔ akɔkyerɛ wɔn ma wɔadi Ɔtemmufo Panyin no ahyɛde no so .
Ɔman Asomdwoe Bagua (NPC) no ahyehyɛ akwan bi a wɔnam so de biakoyɛ kɛse ba ɔman no mu denam po so a wɔbɛtow ahyɛ ɔman no so wɔ afe a etwaam no awiei mu no so .
Sɛnea bagua no kyerɛ no , na amammuisɛm mu basabasayɛ yɛ ɔsɛmpɔw a ɛho hia a ebetumi de tebea bi a emu yɛ den aba , ma enti ɛho hia sɛ wɔka ho asɛm wɔ aban no mu .
NPC no kaa eyi ho asɛm wɔ nhwehwɛmu bi a wɔyɛe wɔ amammuifo ne nnuatwafo afoforo ho wɔ Ada mu wɔ Ɔsesɛw Kɛse no mu no mu .
Wotwaa asɛm no mu sɛ: " Wɔtoo abatow nkrataa - 2020 a wɔnam telefon so yii basabasayɛ ne adan a amanfo ani gye ho kɛse wɔ Ghana no mu , na Asɛnnibea a Ɛhwɛ Akyerɛwfo ne Amanaman Nkabom Nkɔsodwuma (UNDP) no gyinaa akyi .
Ná botae no ne sɛ wobesi akan wɔ nnuatwafo mu de ahyɛ ɔman ho dɔ a emu yɛ den , amammui mu adwenhorow , asomdwoe , ne aman ntam biakoyɛ mu den .
Wɔn a wɔde wɔn ho hyɛɛ amanyɔsɛm mu no bi ne Kyerɛwfo Panyin a ɔwɔ Ahintasɛm Dwumadibea , Rt Hon . Patricia Scotland; UNDP Rent Representent , Oduruyɛfo Angela Lusigi; Ɔpanyin a Ɔhwɛ Adwuma So , Owura Kojo Oppong Nkruah; Inteah; Ahotefo Hode a Wodi Ho Dwuma , ne Albert
Ná afoforo nso yɛ Ɔman Democratic Congress Adwumayɛfo , Ɔbenfo Eric Bosman Asare; Ɔmampanyin Panyin no nanmusifo , Ɔman no mu mpanyimfo , ne Ɔman Ayaresa Kuw a Ɛwɔ New Patriotic no mufo , Ɔmantam Nhyiamfo no , Ɔmantam Nhyiamfo Akuw a Wɔhwɛ Ɔsom Ho Nsɛm So no .
Owura Dery kae sɛ ɛmfa ho sɛ onnyina ahobammɔ a wodii kan de too abatow no anim wɔ December mu no akyi no , na ɔda so ara kura basabasayɛ a emu yɛ den a ebinom hweree wɔn nkwa , na ɛde wɔn kɔɔ ɔsɛe mu no mu .
Ɔkae sɛ polisifo yɛɛ basabasayɛ a emu yɛ den ho kyerɛwtohɔ wɔ nhyiam anum a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ ɔman no nyinaa mu no mu , a emu nnipa baasia
Owura Dery kae sɛ aban no ani nnye mmɔden a ɔbɔe sɛ obenya wɔn a wɔwɔ ɔhaw no mu ma wɔagyina ɔsɛmmɔnedifo no anim no ho .
Owura Kan - Dapaah ka kyerɛɛ amammui mu nyiyim ne adan a na wɔasi no denneennen no sɛ wɔbɛkɔ so akasa atia ɔmanfo yiyedi , sikasɛm , ne amammui mu nkɔso a na ɛwɔ ɔman no mu no .
Rt Hon . Scotlandfo kamfoo Ghanafo no wɔ asomdwoe kwan a wɔfaa so de wɔn ho hyɛɛ amanyɔsɛm mu ɔkasa mu wɔ ɔman no mu no ho .
Sɛnea Ghana kyerɛ no , bere bi a atwam no , na wakyerɛ ɔkwan a wɔfa so bu akontaa wɔ dodow amammu mu , a ɔkae sɛ " ɛyɛ adesoa a emu yɛ duru wɔ nnipa a wodi atentam so no so , nanso ɛyɛ adesoa bi a ɛma nkurɔfo yɛ ahantan bere nyinaa .
Nanso , na ɛsɛ sɛ ɔde mmea pii ne mmabun a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu ho adwene ba ne so .
The Chairman of the NPC, Rev . Oduruyɛfo Ernest Adu - Gyamfi , kae sɛ n'afipamfo no reyɛ adwuma a ɛhyɛ wɔn den ma wɔde wɔn ho hyɛ asraadi mu na wɔde wɔn ho to wɔn ho so kɛse , na wonya ahotoso kɛse wɔ nnwumakuw titiriw a ɛma wotumi paw nneɛma a aba so no mu .
Ɔdaa anidaso a ɛne sɛ nsɛm a yɛasusuw ho no bɛboa kɛse ma wɔasa nyarewa wɔ abatow a ɛto so 2020 no akyi no adi .
Owura Godwin Amarh a ɔyɛ Transeco Minerals ne Mining Akoa Panyin no asi ɔdan a ɛtoa so asia wɔ Atiwa West Region no mu .
Wobuu akontaa wɔ sukuu dan no mu , a na ne bo yɛ den a GH de too adwumakuw bi a wɔfrɛ no Corporate Social Resion (CSR) no mu .
Bere a Owura Amarh rekasa wɔ ɔdan no mu no , osii so dua sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔde nhomasua pa ma mmofra bere a ɛboa wɔn ma wonya nhomasua a emu yɛ den no .
Ɔkae sɛ wontumi nyi nhomasua a ɛkɔ so wɔ ɔman biara mu no mfi hɔ , enti nea enti a ɔyɛɛ adwuma ansa na ɔresua nhoma no .
MPANYIMFO bi a ɔwɔ Transeco Mining and Minerals Company ayɛ n'adwene sɛ ɔbɛhwɛ ahu sɛ mmofra a wɔwɔ mmeae a wɔyɛ adwuma no ani gye nhomasua ne nneɛma a wosua ho sen biara ho sen biara . Ɛno nti na yɛde nhomasua a ɛkɔ akyiri adi yɛn asetram asɛyɛde ho dwuma .
Yɛn nyinaa nim sɛnea nhomasua ho hia na ama ankorankoro ne ɔman no anya nkɔso . Nea ɛbɛyɛ na wɔanya adesuafo a wɔn ho akokwaw kɛse wɔ nhomasua mu no , ɛsɛ sɛ wodi kan nya fapem a emu yɛ den a nea enti a yɛasan asi saa Ayamyefogargaret yi no , ɔkae sɛ , nea enti a
Owura Amarh kae sɛ sukuu no yɛ anisɔ a wɔkyerɛ ma mpanyimfo ne wɔn a wofii ase ne adwumakuw no nyaa abusuabɔ pa fi bere a wofii wɔn dwumadi ase wɔ mpɔtam hɔ no .
Nea ɛne rummiriw ne nsɛm a ɛyɛ hu a wɔka sɛ aban no de adwuma bi ahyɛ ɔman no mu ma no bɔ abira no , Owura Amarh buu nkuruwa no fɔ , na ɔkaa ho asɛm sɛ ɛyɛ nnaadaa kɛkɛ , na mmom ɛyɛ atoro .
Sɛnea n'ankasa kyerɛ no , nniso de akwan foforo a wɔfa so yɛ nneɛma foforo ho nhyehyɛe ne nhyehyɛe ahorow a atirimpɔw no ne sɛ wɔde begu ade ketewaa bi na ɛnyɛ adesɛe .
Mfiri a wɔde kora nneɛma so no mmaa kwan sɛ wontwa nsuka , na mmom ɛmmoro mmeae a ɛbemmɛn hɔ no sɛ dantaban a obi anaa adwumakuw biara m'akyi . Enti nea aban no reka ne sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔn a wotu biriw no tu fi mmeae a wotu bi no . Enti obiara a ɔyɛ nea ɛne aban no bɔ abira no , wɔde mmara a Owura no de too gua wɔ ɔman no mu no bedi dwuma .
Enti otuu wɔn a wotu biriw no fo sɛ wɔnkɔyɛ adwuma , nanso ɔhwɛ ma wɔde wɔn kɔ mmeae a wɔahyehyɛ hɔ no .
Owura Amarh a ɔno nso bu bɔ ho abien sɛ Ghana Ɔman Fekuw a Ɛhwɛ Nyarewa Ho Nsɛm So (GNASM) no Kyerɛwfo a wɔwɔ kuw no mu no tu wɔn fo sɛ wobetumi anya ɔmanfo so nkɛntɛnso pa .
Ɔkae sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔn a wotu biriw no bɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛsakra asɛm a ɛne sɛ wɔn a wɔsɛe wɔn fi aman mu nkutoo na wɔsɛe wɔn , na wɔnsan mfa wɔn ho mma bio no .
Ɔkae sɛ , ɛwom sɛ wɔn a wotu biriw no pii reyɛ saa dedaw de , nanso ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ pii ka ho .
Enti ɛsɛ sɛ yɛyere yɛn ho yɛ adwuma bere a yɛrefi baabi a yɛrekɔ no . Minim sɛ yɛn a yɛyɛ sukuu ne afoforo a wɔaboa wɔn no dodow no ara wɔ anyinam ahoɔden . Ɛsɛ sɛ yepi
Rebecca Foundation no de ne nsa ahyɛ Memorandum of Understanding (MoU) a Abdul Samad Rabiud Afrika Initiative (ASR Africa) no ase sɛ wɔmma no $ 500,000 .
Wobenya saa sika no afi ASR Africafo dɔla ɔpepem 100 a wɔyɛn wɔn afe biara wɔ Afrika Ayaresa ne Renewal hɔ de ahwɛ Abecca Asoɛe no nhomasua a efi wɔn pɛ mu ba no so .
Bere a Owura Ubon Udoh rekasa wɔ nhyiam no ase no , ɔkamfoo nhyɛase a ɛwɔ hɔ ma mmea ne mmofra a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu yiyedi no .
Afei nso , ɔkamfoo nhyɛase a ɛmaa adwumakuw no dii wɔn so ne wɔn nneyɛe pa a ama wɔatumi anya ayaresa ne mmoa a wɔde ma wɔ nhomasua mu , akwahosan ne mmea akwahosan pa no maa sikasɛm mu yɛɛ den no .
" BERE a yɛyɛɛ yɛn sukuu dwumadi wɔ fie na yehui sɛ Rebecca Ahyehyɛde no yɛ guasodeyɛ a ɛho hia sen biara wɔ Ghana , na ɛhyɛɛ ASR nkuran ma wɔboaa Ɔsesɛw no .
Owurayere Rebecca Akufo - Addo , a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ hɔ no daa ASR Afrika ase sɛ ɔboaa no ma otumi gyinaa ne nan so .
Ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ ɔbɛma mmofra a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu anya wɔn ntetee no so mfaso .
UK no amfa ne ho anhyɛ Nnamdi Kanu , a odi kuw bi a wɔabara kuw bi a wɔrehwehwɛ ɔkwan a wɔbɛfa so asiw tebea no ano wɔ Nigeria kesee fam apuei , baabi a Igbofo yɛ nnipa dodow no ara no mu .
Sɛnea mmaranimfo panyin panyin no kyerɛ no , Owura Kanu , a ɔyɛ Britaniani ne Nigeriani no de Interpol mmoa maa no Kwasida , na ɔde nhwiren san kɔɔ Nigeria .
Ohyiaa sobo a ɛmfata wɔ Nigeria , nanso oguan fii ɔman no mu wɔ 2017 mu bere a na ɔda mpa mu no .
Nnipa pii ka sɛ ebia wɔkyeree no wɔ UK no mu , baabi a wogye di sɛ ɛno ne ade titiriw a wogyinaa so kyeree no no .
Nnamyɛ betumi asi so dua sɛ wɔamfa Nnamdi Kanu anni dwuma wɔ UK no mu , na mmom Britania Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Ahobammɔ So no kaa BBC ho asɛm kyerɛɛ Nnamdi Kanu .
Mprempren , wɔde no ato afiase dan bi mu wɔ Nigeria sum ase polisifo mu bere a wɔde no kɔɔ asɛnnibea bere tiaa bi wɔ Benada no .
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ n'asɛm no befi ase wɔ July 26 .
Abarimaa a wadi mfe 53 no begyee din wɔ afe 2009 mu bere a ofii Radio Biafra ne ɔsebɔ ase kɔɔ Nigeria no , na ɔde asɛnka agua no frɛɛ Biafran ahofadi , na ɔhyɛɛ n'akyidifo nkuran sɛ wɔmfa akode no nhyɛ Nigeria man no nsa no .
Mfe anum akyi no , ohuu Nnipa a Wɔwɔ Biafra (Ipob), a efi bere a Nigeria atumfoɔ no buu no sɛ omumɔyɛfo kuw bi no .
Owura Kanu's a wodii kan kyeree no afe 2015 no de atuatew kɛse bae .
M'ani gyei bere a mihui sɛ afe a etwaam no , wɔasan asiesie Square no .
Ná ɛsɛ sɛ osiesie mfonini a wɔayɛ no foforo no , na ɛsɛ sɛ osiesie Square no ma kan Ɔmampanyin Jerry John Rawlings ayi no
Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Ayaresa Ho Nsɛm So (IoD - Gh) no akamfo Ghana Sikakorabea (BoG) no sɛ ɛyɛ akwan titiriw a wɔfa so yɛ nnwuma a ebetumi ama adwumakuw no adi yiye wɔ ɔman no mu .
Afei nso , abehia ama adwumakuw no ne sikakorabea no ntam abusuabɔ a emu yɛ den a wɔde boa ma nnwumakuw a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu di wɔn asɛyɛde ho dwuma yiye .
Wɔ asennibea bi a IoD - Gh, Owura Rockson Kwesigbeah , Mmarahyɛ Bagua no de too gua mu no , ɔyɛɛ Amrado a ɔhwɛ sikakorabea atitiriw , Oduruyɛfo Ernest Addison , no so , na ɔyɛɛ nsakrae wɔ adwuma a wɔyɛ de siesie wɔn ahosiesie a wɔyɛ wɔ sika fam no mu .
Ɔkaa mmɔden a BoG a Dr Addison dii n'anim no bɔe no ho asɛm kyerɛɛ sum ase kuw bi a wɔn ho yɛ hu na wɔn ho yɛ den .
Asɛm bi a efi adwumakuw no mu kae ne sɛ wɔkamfoo sikakorabea no wɔ dwuma titiriw a edii wɔ sɛnea wɔkamfoo ɔman no sodibea pa wɔ Ghana no ho , na wɔhwehwɛɛ abusuabɔ a mfaso wɔ so a ɛda BoG ne n'stitute ntam
Bere a Owura Dogbegah reka IoD - Gh ho nhwehwɛmu a wɔyɛe ho asɛm no , ɔkae sɛ IoD - Gh , IoD - Gh no , na ɔrema nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn bi a atirimpɔw wom a wɔde gyinapɛn ahorow a wɔde di dwuma wɔ ɔsom mu akwankyerɛ mu wɔ Ghana .
Ɔkyerɛe sɛ ɔman sodi ho mmara a wodii ho dwuma no yɛ adwuma titiriw foforo a na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde si ananmu .
Ɔdaa no adi sɛ na wɔn a wɔde wɔn di dwuma no de afe afe afe ahyɛde ahorow a ɛkorɔn sen biara no asi hɔ sɛ ɛka mmɔden a wɔbɔe sɛ wobedi ankorankoro ne nnwumakuw a wɔyɛ atitiriw a wodii wɔn anim ne wɔn atrae ho dwuma no ho , na ɛmaa
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ Asuae no , a na wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ nnuatwafo nsa ano no ama Ghana Akunini Fekuw no atwetwe wɔn adwene akɔ wɔn ho so , na
BoG Amrado kae sɛ adwumakuw no di dwuma titiriw wɔ sikasɛm mu fekuw no mu .
Sɛnea n'ankasa kyerɛ no , adwumakuw bi a wodi wɔn ho wɔn ho ni , ne wɔn a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ baabi foforo no di nneɛma a ɛde sikasɛm mu ahokyere ba no bi ho dwuma , na ɛno
Ɔsan sii hia a ɛho hia sɛ Ghanafo di ɔman no so no so , na ɔhyɛɛ da yɛɛ adwuma a sikakorabea no yɛ de boaa adwuma no , ne titiriw no , bere a nsɛm a asisi wɔ sum ase kuw no mu no nya nkɛntɛnso kɛse wɔ Ghana sikasɛm mu fekuw no so no .
Ɛsɛ sɛ Arteta gye bere a edi hɔ
Sɛnea madi kan aka no , Arsenal ampɛ sɛ ɔbɛwe Mikel Arteta ne kuw no so ahwɛfo no bɛsan de no aba ahɔhodan no mu wɔ bere a edi hɔ no mu .
Sɛ Arsenal asi gyinae pa a , obiara ntumi nka nkyerɛ no , nanso kuw no bɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛma agumadifo a wɔn ho akokwaw pii anya saa ahohuru bere yi mu kyɛfa .
Wobisa nsɛm a emu yɛ den a ɛfa adwumakuw bi a wɔasiesie wɔn ho , ne n'ankasa ahosiesie ho agumadifo mpo rehwɛ no , na wontumi nhu sɛ ɔno ne onipa a ɔfata ma adwuma no anaa .
Wɔ mfe 39 mu no , Arteta agye din wɔ Pep Guardiola , a ne ho yɛ anika no nkyɛn .
Nanso , wɔ asram dunson akyi a wɔbɔɔ Arsenal asu no annya nkɔso , na nnipa pii bɛka sɛ kuw no mufo nnu wɔn a wɔne wɔn di nkitaho no ho , ɔbarima a ɔde ne ho hyɛɛ Europa Apam no mu na ɔbɔɔ no mu no .
Arteta hyɛɛ Arsenal nsa , na bere a wɔrehwɛ Chelsea ne Tottenham no , wotuu wɔn ani sii wɔn so .

De Gea di adanse sɛ ɔyɛ No2
Ɛmfa ho sɛ Manchester United botae ho dwumayɛni David De Gea wɔ adwuma bi mu kosi 2023 no , n'ananmusifo no resɔ nsu no ahwɛ ahu akuw a wɔn ani begye ho sɛ wɔde wɔn nsa bɛhyɛ ase .
M'ani agye wɔ Matt Trafford mu sɛ ɛmfa ho adwempa a Roan Henderson a ɔwɔ No1 no wɔ no , De Gea rentra ase nnye dwuma a obedi bere tenten no ntom .
M'ani regye Atletico Madrid, Paris Saint Germain ne Madrid Ankasa ho .
Ɛwom sɛ nnipa a wɔadi mfe 30 no mu bi gye di sɛ wahwere mfe abien a atwam no de , nanso akyinnye biara nni ho sɛ n'adwuma no korɔn sen biara .
Manager Solskjaer kae sɛ , adwumakuw bi a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ baabi a wɔhwɛ mmoa so no yɛ kuw a wɔn ho yɛ den paa .
Wɔyɛ adwuma de siesie wɔn ho , na ɛsono sɛnea wɔn mu biara yɛ n'ade , na ɛsono sɛnea wɔn mu biara yɛ n'ade , na wɔbom tra faako .
Sɛnea ɛte biara no , wonya abusuabɔ ne honhom wɔ beae a wɔhwɛ dwumadi no so no .
Ɛma wonya akansi a ɛfata .
Migye di sɛ , sɛ De Gea de afiri bi a wɔfrɛ no No1 a ɛwɔ n'asen akyi no gye wɔn ani a , nea ɔka ne ho no yɛ nokware , nanso sɛ ɔka kyerɛ no sɛ obeyi ne ho afi Old Trafford agodie a ɛho hia no mu a ,
Mefa West Brom sɛ mensan m'akyi bio
Bere bi akyi a yedi wɔ Premier League no , yɛsan ka no yiye sɛ West Bromwich Albion .
Ade foforo a ebetumi ama yɛasan atwe yɛn ho afi Ɔhaw no ho ne sɛ ebia Sam Allardyce a ɔyɛ oduruyɛfo a ne ho yɛ hu no betumi adaadaa yɛn ma yɛatra hɔ .
Wahwere ne din , efisɛ sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wɔkɔ so tra faako na wɔtra Brom Atɔe fam a , na ɛyɛ den ma no sɛ ɔbɛyɛ adwuma pii .
Ainsley Maitland - Nariiles , Conor Gallagher ne Okay Yokulu bɛsan akɔ wɔn awofo nkyɛn bere a wɔakogyina loan nanso Matheus Pereira, Callum Robinson, Hal Robson - Kenu ne Karl Grant no .
Ɔbarima a Ɔsen Biara Wɔ Kuropɔn Mu
Nea odi agoru sen biara wɔ Manchester Kuropɔn no mu ne obi a odi agoru koraa
Obiara nni hɔ a ne din de Raheem Sterling .
Manager Pep Guardiola yɛɛ adeyɛ bi a na ɛsɛ sɛ agumadifo no mu biara di n'awode no ho dwuma .
Nnipa bi wɔ hɔ a na wɔn ho yɛ hare paa wɔ Kurow no mu , nanso Gabriel Yesu daa no adi sɛ ɔno ne obi a odi mmuada sen biara .
Nea eye sen biara ne sɛ wubefi Havertz
Thomas Tuchel reto ayeyi nnwom wɔ Kai Havertz , na ɔde ne botae abien a ɔde sii n'ani so nnansa yi ara no too Fulham so .
Tuchel ka sɛ efi bere a Kai duu Stamford Bridgeridge a efi Bayer Leverkusen no , nneɛma ankɔ yiye amma Germanfo no .
Ná ɛyɛ den ma no sɛ ɔbɛkyere Covid - 19 , na na ɛsɛ sɛ ɔsan n'akyi kɔ n'akyi .
Sɛnea Champions League a etwa to no ne nea edi hɔ a wɔfrɛ no Tuchel gye di no , saa ara na Tuchel gye di sɛ ɛno na ɛbɛma nea ɔreko tia no no adi mũ na n'ani aba n'anim .
Solskjaer redan Unitedfo bio
Ebetumi aba sɛ Manchester United wɔ ɔhaw akɛse a emu yɛ den a emu yɛ den a ebetumi de basabasayɛ aba wɔn wuranom so , nanso wɔ kuw no mu no , biakoyɛ foforo ne ahotoso foforo a wɔwɔ sɛ wobetumi ayɛ .
Ɔbarima a ɔhwɛ adwuma no so ne Ole Gunner Solskjaer , na bere a ɔne United States adwumayɛfo ne mmoafo pii kasae wɔ dapɛn yi mu no , obiara ka sɛ ɛyɛ bere a ɛsɛ sɛ yeyi adwuma sohwɛfo no ayɛ na ama wanya ahoɔden pii wɔ asram awotwe a etwa to no mu .
Solskjaer faa kwan bi so de ne nsa hyɛɛ Bruno Fernandes ne Edinson Cavani ase , na wɔn baanu nyinaa ayɛ nneɛma a edi mũ a ɛne United States akwantu hyia .
Cavani asi so dua sɛ ɔtra hɔ wɔ bere foforo mu , na ne gyidi titiriw ne Solskjaer mu gyidi a na ɔwɔ no .
Paul Pogba hwɛɛ n'anim na n'ani gyei , na ɔne adwuma sohwɛfo no nyaa abusuabɔ a emu yɛ den bere nyinaa .
Sɛ United States hwe ase wɔ nna yi mu a , wɔko tia , na mpɛn pii no , wɔko tia sen sɛ wobedi nkonim .
Ade biako wɔ hɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛde aseda ma wɔ Vice - Chairman Ed Woodward for ho , na ɛno ma kwan ma Solskjaer bere no yɛ yiye wɔ adwuma no mu , nya wɔn ti didi mu , na ɛma wɔn a wodi agoru no dan wɔn ho wɔn ho .
Mprempren , Solskjaer yɛ beae a ɛho hia sen biara , na po so ahyɛnsode a ɛyɛ den sen biara no , adwumayɛfo ne nkraman gye di sɛ eyi ne bere a sika wom a efi ase kɔ Reds no mfiase .
