Kane susuw ho sɛ wubefi hɔ
Mihuu kommyɛ bi a ɛho hia bere a na me ne Leeds di nkitaho wɔ dapɛn awiei no .
Mpɛn pii no , Harry Kane tu mmirika sen ɔfɛmdifo foforo biara , na bere nyinaa ɔde ahyɛde ne akwankyerɛ ma agumadifo afoforo ma wodi agoru yiye .
Ná ɔyɛ dinn paa wɔ Leeds anim sen sɛnea misusuw sɛ mahu no pɛn .
Misusuw sɛ eyi yɛ sɛnkyerɛnne a edi mũ a ɛkyerɛ sɛ Harry nnye ne ho nni koraa wɔ Spurs , na ɔrehwehwɛ ɔkwan bi afi mu dedaw .
Akuafo a wɔn ani abere rehwehwɛ obi a wɔabɔ no
Nuno Espirito Santos ahu nnansa yi ara sɛ bere a ɔrefi ase no , ɛsɛ sɛ ɔde ne nsa hyɛ biribi foforo ase .
Winger Pedro Neto atifi fam ne Ruben Neves yɛ wɔn a wodi wɔn anim a ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔyɛ mmerɛw wɔ Wolves no mu .
Nea edi hɔ no , Fabio Silva ne Raul Jimenez abobɔ Jimenez din afi Jimenez akyi fi November , bere a ne ti so tew no .
Afe a etwaam no nnu botae 13 .
Akuafo no ahyɛ Nuno sika ho bɔ sɛ wɔde wɔn nsa bɛhyɛ botae bi a wɔde asisi wɔn ani so ase .
Sɛ Jimenez di agoru abien a etwa to wɔ saa bere yi mu no a , nea ebefi mu aba ne May 18 .
Watete no asram abien , nanso na wɔabara sɛ ɔmmɔ bɔɔl no , na ɔne ne mfɛfo a ɔne wɔn bɔ fekuw no nni nkitaho wɔ nipaduam .
Owura Alex yi McTominay ayɛ
Bere a Sir Alex Ferguson kɛse no ka Manchester United ho asɛm no , ɛfata sɛ yetie no bere nyinaa .
N'anim a ɔde maa Scott McTominay no mu yɛ den , na ne wura no ka sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ okunkɛse no di agoru wɔ United agodie biara mu .
McTominay a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ po so hyɛn bi mu no reda adi mprempren sɛ United States bɔɔl akɛse no mu biako , na Sir Alex kae sɛ .

Oduruyɛfo Madzorera kae sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ akwahosan ho som adwuma no nso ma yehu ɔyare no ho nsɛm , ne telefon a wɔda no adi wɔ ɔman no afã horow nyinaa mu sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a nkurɔfo betumi aka yare no ho asɛm bere biara .
Wɔsan hyɛ hygiene nhwehwɛmu ho nkuran , na ɛnyɛ sɛ wɔretwɛn sɛ obi a wobu no sɛ wako atia no de wɔn akɔ ayaresabea .
Caps Unitedirman Lewis Uririri ka sɛ wɔadi wɔn haw ahorow a wɔrehyia wɔ wɔn kuw no mu no ho dwuma , na agumadifo a wodi agoru no afi ase resiesie wɔn ho ama Castleer Socer League no .
Uririri ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7, no sɛ wɔmaa agodifo no sika a ɛda nsow .
Nanso ɔkae sɛ ɔsram a etwaam no , wobetua n'ayaresa ho ka ama agumadifo no ntɛm ara . Ɔkae nso sɛ nnipa bi a wɔmmɔɔ wɔn din a na wɔwɔ Caps a wɔbɔ bɔɔ bɔɔl no so .
Uriri kae sɛ ɔkaa asɛm no kyerɛɛ agodifo no , na ɔkae nso sɛ nea enti a wɔtwentwɛn wɔn nan ase sɛ wobetua agodifo no ne sɛ na nneɛma mu yɛ den ma obiara wɔ ɔman no mu , na na aban ankasa no mfa afe a etwaam no akatua mma .
Ɛho hia sɛ wɔhyɛ mmara a ɛma nyinsɛn gu gu ho nkuran na wɔbɔ mmeawa ne mmea asetra ho ban .
Nsɛmendisa Ndlovu a ɔwɔ SayWhat ka sɛ ɔmanfo nnim nyinsɛn a wotu gu no ho hwee , na ɛka sɛ ɛho hia sɛ aban no bɔ mmara no ho dawuru .
Ndlovu ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔkyerɛw mmara no bere tenten a atwam ni . Ɔkae sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde mmara no ka nneɛma foforo a ebetumi ama obi apɔn yafunu ho .
Ndlovu kae sɛ nneɛma bi te sɛ adwenemyare , HIV / AIDS anaa dɛmdi yɛ nneɛma a wobetumi abu no sɛ ɛde nyinsɛn a wotu gu no bi .
Ndlovu kyerɛkyerɛɛ mu nso sɛ mmara no mma kwan sɛ aban ayaresabea ahorow bɛtew nyinsɛn a wotu gu so , na enhia sɛ abofra hwɛfo anaa oduruyɛfo bi tu obi fo wɔ mmara kwan so .
Ms . Tendaishe Changamire , ɔman hokwan ho dwumayɛni bi a ɔwɔ Hokwan a Ɛwɔ Hɔ Nnɛyi Dwumadi no ase , ahwehwɛ mmara a ɛka sɛ wobetumi asiw nyinsɛn a wotu gu no ano .
Ms . Changamire ka sɛ nhwehwɛmu pii kyerɛ sɛ mmeawa nkumaa nam nyinsɛn a wotu gu so rehwere wɔn nkwa .
Ɛwom sɛ mmofra pii repia mmara no de , nanso mmea mpanyimfo binom sɔre tia , na wɔka sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ nyinsɛn a wotu gu no ma wogye tom kɛse , na wɔka sɛ ɛbɛma mmofra a wonni obu mma wɔn ho wɔn ho .
Mmarahyɛ bagua bi a wɔyɛe wɔ 197 mu ansa na ɔman no refi wɔn pɛ mu ayɛ adwuma wɔ Ɔman no Mmarahyɛ Bagua no ase .
Polisifo akyere MDC - T a Nelson Chamisa dii wɔn anim no mu pii bere a wɔbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛkɔ adwumakuw no adwumayɛbea ti a ɛwɔ Morgan Tsvangirai House no .
Eyi bae bere a Ms Thokozani Khupe dii MDC a Ms Thokozani dii
Asɛnnibea Kunini no abu Ms Khupe sɛ onnyina Morgan Tsvangirai's wu akyi mfe abien a atwam ni .
Nnwumakuw abien , Tendai Biti ne Lynett Karenyi Kore , ne David Chini, Lovemore Cadys Hlatywayo ne afoforo ka wɔn a wɔhwɛ abofra so no ho .
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ na ataine no rekɔ adwumayɛbea ti hɔ , baabi a na polisifo a wokurakura akode atwa wɔn ho ahyia no .
Studio7 ntumi ntee sɛnea wɔkyeree nnipa pii no , na sobo a wɔde baa wɔn so bere a polisini Paul Nyathi ammua ne telefon no .
Chamisa MDC kasamafo , Fadzai Mahere , kae sɛ ɔkyere no maa ne ho dwiriw no .
Tebea a ɛwɔ MDC mu no yɛ hu bere a Asɛnnibea Kunini no dii saa afe yi a edii so sɛ Chamisa ne Ms Khupe n's asraafo no nyɛ asraafo , na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ Mmarahyɛ Bagua bere a Ms Khupe yɛ adwuma no .
Bere a wodii tumi no , Ms Khupe de n'ahokafo baanan ne wɔn a wɔn ani ku wɔn ho no guu afiase , na ɔkae sɛ nkurɔfo no mfa wɔn ho nhyɛ wɔn apontow no ase bio .
Thabitha Khumalo , Prosper Mutseyami , Lilian Timveous and Charlton Hwende .
Zimbabweanfo bi a wɔwɔ aman horow so ka sɛ esiane Robert Mugabe nniso nti , wɔhyɛɛ wɔn ma wofii ɔman no mu .
Ɔbenfo Victor Chimtu ka sɛ ɛmfa ho sɛ wobuu Owura Mugabe sɛ Afrikafo abusua bi muni wɔ Norway Sukuupɔn mu no , Zimbabwe Yibuya / Maybuya / Mayibuye Zimbabwe ahyehyɛde no muni no , ɔka sɛ ɛmfa ho sɛ na wobu no sɛ biakoyɛ a ɛwɔ Afrikafo abusua bi mu no , biako mpo ammu no saa .
Oduruyɛfo Chimtu ka sɛ Owura Mugabe's ka Afrika akannifo afoforo a wɔne wɔn di nkitaho no ho biako ne nea enti a wanya obu kɛse afi Afrika akannifo hɔ no .
Wɔka sɛ Owura Mugabe nso bedidi na wada n'adwenkyerɛ a ɔwɔ wɔ Atɔe fam no adi , na ɔbɛkasa atia aman akannifo te sɛ United States ne Britain akannifo no .
Owura Mugabe kaa no pen sɛ , sɛ ne Sanu Kuw no mufo di dɛm anaa wodi wɔn ho fɛw mpo a , ɔboro akraman no , na ɔhwe wɔn .
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ wɔde Owura Mugabe bɛto hɔ Kwasida , ɛwom sɛ wonnya mmɔɔ no amanneɛ de .
Nnuruyɛfo ne ayarehwɛfo a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ ɔmanfo ayaresabea no aka akyerɛ aban no sɛ , sɛ wontua wɔn ka ansa na December awiei aba a , wobegyae adwuma a wɔreyɛ no ɔsram a edi hɔ no mfiase no .
Ná Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Dɔktafo Fekuw no titrani , Fortune Nyamande , a ɔkae sɛ n'ahyehyɛde no ne Zimbabwe Nurses Fekuw no wɔ abusuabɔ no akyerɛw krataa akɔma aban no ma wakyerɛ wɔn baabi a wɔrekɔ no .
Dɔkta Nyamande kae sɛ na wakyerɛw aban no ma waka ne ho asɛm akyerɛ no wɔ January 1 a edi hɔ no mu .
Wɔka sɛ wɔne ayarehwɛfo a wɔwɔ aban ayaresabea ahorow no afa saa kwan yi so esiane kar ho ka a wɔmmɔe bere a wonnya nnya nnyaa wɔn da wɔ ɔsram biara da , ne wɔn nnwetɛbona a aban no hyɛɛ ho bɔ no nti .
Ɔbenfo Nyamande kasa tiaa aban mpanyimfo a wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔde nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfo di dwuma no nso sɛ wɔmfa wɔn ho nhyɛ atesɛm nkrataa mu .
Ɔmampanyin Panyin Patrick Chinamasa abɔ amanneɛ dedaw sɛ aban no ntumi ntua n'adwumayɛfo no bi ka afe yi esiane sika a wonni nti .
" MMr Chinamasa de atesɛm nkrataa aka sɛnea yɛn bere yi mu nsakrae bɛba ho asɛm , enti yɛde akwan koro no ara bedi dwuma .
Wɔaka nnwontofo kuw a na ɛsɛ sɛ wotua wɔn ka wɔ Dwoda no ho asɛm wɔ Tuada , nanso wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ afe a edi hɔ no , wɔde wɔn akatua no bɛma ɔmanfo , a nnuruyɛfo ne ayarehwɛfo ka ho no .
Nanso , amanfo pii a wɔne Studio 7 kasae no kae sɛ wonni ahotoso sɛ wɔn nsa bɛka wɔn sika wɔ atesɛm foforo no mu .
Yɛantumi anhyia Akwahosan Soafo , David Parirenyatwa , ne Labor Asomfo , Priscah Mupfumira , na yɛahwehwɛ akwan a wɔbɛfa so asiw ɔhaw bi ano .
Ɔsɔretia titiriw a MDC kuw no de aba no anwiinwii sɛ polisifo reteetee emufo .
Zimbabwe Mmarafo a Wɔhwɛ Hokwan a Nnipa Wɔ So no ka sɛ wɔakyere nnipa 47 nnansa yi ara , a wɔn mu dodow no ara yɛ MDCfo ne adesuafo baason a wɔwɔ Allen Wilson Sukuu mu wɔ Harare , a wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔkasa tiaa wɔn no .
Makomborero Haruzivishe , obi a kan no na ɔyɛ sukuuni a ofi ZINASU , a okopuee asɛnnibea nnɛ , ne ne yɔnko Allan Moyo no ka ho .
Na yentumi nkɔɔ polisifo kasa mu , Sɛnea Ɔsahene Paul Nyathi , bere a na wɔn telefon no nni hɔ no .
Haruzihe ne Moyo a ɔyɛ Mmarahyɛ Bagua no mmaranimfo no kae sɛ Haruzihe ne Moyo bɛsan akɔ asɛnnibea Dwoda asusuw gyinae a Asɛnnibea no sii no ho .
Amanaman Nkabom Wiase Nyinaa Akwahosan Ahyehyɛde (WHO) no de ato gua wɔ China sɛ mogya mu ɔyare mmoawa a ekunkum nnipa 233 wɔ China no abɛyɛ wiase nyinaa yaredɔm .
Wɔ nnanu a edi akyiri no nkutoo mu no , wobu akontaa sɛ nnipa bɛyɛ 2,000 na wonyaa ehon ntini mu ɔyare mmoawa no bi , na 9,800 anya yare no bi wɔ wiase nyinaa wɔ aman 244 mu .
WHO panyin Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus kae sɛ bere a na wɔwɔ ahotoso sɛ Chinafo rebɔ mmɔden sɛ wobesiw yare no ano no , na wosuro sɛ sɛ sɛ ɛtrɛw kɔ wiase no afã foforo a , ebetumi akunkum nnipa pii .
Oduruyɛfo Obadiah Moyo a ɔyɛ adwuma no sohwɛfo ka sɛ Zimbabwe resɔ nnipa bɛboro 200 a wofi China anaa aman a kokoram yare mmoawa wom ahwɛ .
Wɔredi nkurɔfo a wɔrehwehwɛ wɔn mu wɔ Zimbabwe no fie nna 14 .
Kan akwahosan ho somfo Henry Madzorera ka sɛ Zimbabwe hia sika pii na asiw yare no ano .
Wɔbɛbɔ kan ɔmampanyin Robert Mugabe amu no ho amanneɛ wɔ Harare awiabere ne n'ayi mu .
Wɔbɔɔ eyi ho amanneɛ wɔ Ms Monica Mutsvangwa , wɔ nhyiam bi a wɔyɛe wɔ asɔredan bi mu akyi .
Ms Mutsvangwa kae sɛ aban boayikuw ahorow resiesie wɔn ho ama Owura Mugabe's ayi .
Bere a wobisaa Mugabes ayi no ho asɛm no , Mutsvangwa ne Foreign Affairs Minister Sibusi Moyo kae sɛ ɛyɛ "unusual " na ɔreka n'ayi ho nhyehyɛe a wayɛ bere a Mugabe abusua no duu Singapore no ho asɛm .
Ɔkae sɛ aban ne Ɔmampanyin Mugabe's abusua no bom yɛ adwuma .
Saa bere no ara mu no , Ɔhene Katizagombo's kasamafo , Gibson Jenami , kae sɛ asɛm biara nni Mugabes ayi no ho bio sɛ aban no , a Emmerson Mnangagwa dii n'akyi no .
Saa bere no ara mu no , wɔde Major General Trust Mugoba , a ɔno nso wui wɔ dapɛn a etwaam no mu no bɛto awiabere wɔ Heroes Acre amusiei asase a ɛwɔ Harare no so .
Wɔ nsɛm foforo mu no , aban no ka Zimbabweanfo ho asɛm sɛ basabasayɛ a ɛrekɔ so wɔ South Africa no anya wɔn so nkɛntɛnso , na Zimbabweanfo baanu awuwu wɔ basabasayɛ no mu .
Moyo kae sɛ , na aban no reyɛ nhyehyɛe de nipadua no akɔ fie .
Aban no ka nso sɛ , wɔn a wɔhwɛ akwahosan ho nsɛm so , a nnuruyɛfo ka ho , anya wɔn mfaso no ɔha biara mu 60 , na ɛnnɛ , nnuru a wɔde sa nyarewa ne sika ho nhyehyɛe no asi gyinae sɛ akwahosan ne sika ho adwuma no bɛtra ase ahwɛ ahu sɛ wobetua adwumayɛfo no ka ɔkwan a ɛfata so .
Oduruyɛfo Obadiah Moyo , a ɔyɛ Ɔpanyin no ka sɛ ɔbɛtra ase de sika ayɛ asɛnka adwuma no sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobenya sika kɔkɔɔ no .
Dɔktafo kɔɔ so nwiinwii wɔ dapɛn a etwaam no mu sɛ wɔn salade no so tew dodo .
Ahyehyɛde bi a wɔhyehyɛe sɛ wɔnkae hokwan ahorow a nnipa wɔ , ne bere bi a atwam no , Afrika Biakoyɛ Square kannifo Itai Dzamara , a ɛwɔ Itai Dzamara Trust no , dii Amanaman Ntam Mmea Da no .
Wɔyɛɛ guasodeyɛ no wɔ Highfield , baabi a wɔmaa mmea ne mmeawa a wɔkɔɔ hɔ no de nnwinnade anaa mpaboa ne nea ɛkeka ho maa wɔn .
Ɔkasamafo bi a ɔyɛ Dzamara abusua no muni a ɔno nso yɛ Itai Dzamara Trust , Owurason Dzamara , kasamara , no ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ ohui sɛ ɛfata sɛ ɔda ɔdɔ adi kyerɛ mmea wɔ ɔsram yi mu , ɔsram a ne nuabarima Itais's de dii dwuma mfe anum a atwam ni no .
Ɔkae sɛ ɛwom sɛ na ne nua no de ne ho ahyɛ amammuisɛm mu de , nanso esiane ɔdɔ ne Itai Dzamara Ahotoso nti , ɔkɔɔ so daa ayamye adi kyerɛɛ no .
Ɔkae sɛ n'ahyehyɛde no ayɛ ne dwumadi wɔ Highfield akuraa no ase efisɛ ɛyɛ Itai awoda , nanso ɔkae sɛ wɔbɛkɔ mmeae foforo akɔboa mmea ne ahiafo a wɔwɔ nimdeɛ ne osuahu pii wɔ mmeae pii a mmara ne nhomasua ne akwahosan ka ho .
Wɔn a wɔkɔɔ hɔ nnɛ no bi ne kaeance Zuze , a ɔkae sɛ ɛwom sɛ na Owura Dzamara nnya nhuu no de , nanso n'ani gyee adwuma a ahyehyɛde no yɛe wɔ n'asetra mu no ho .
Abeawa bi a wɔammɔ ne din ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ wanya mfaso pii nnɛ .
Saa bere yi nyinaa no , Partson Dzamara abɔ amanneɛ sɛ , sɛ obi a onni din wɔ Glen View no di mfe anum a , wɔbɛkae no Benada wɔ Harare .
Ɔkaa saa no , na wonnim baabi a ne nua no wɔ anaasɛ ebia ɔte ase .
Ɔkae sɛ polisini , hokwan a nnipa wɔ , Zimbabwe Human Rights Comion ne afoforo a wɔne Itai Dzamara yɛɛ adwuma no ka wɔn a wɔtoo nsa frɛɛ wɔn kɔɔ nhyiam no ho .
Bere a wiase no di aguanfo da , ɔkyena , no , Zimbabwefo binom a wɔte South Africa no ka sɛ biribiara nni hɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ wodi bere a South Africa yɛ hu no .
Zimbabweanfo bi ka sɛ South Africafo nkyerɛ obu mma nhyehyɛe a ahyehyɛde ahorow te sɛ Amanaman Nkabom no ayɛ wɔ hokwan a aguanfo wɔ ho no .
Zimbabwe Migrant Support Network , Shelton Chiyangwa , ɔkyerɛwfo panyin ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ ɛwom sɛ aguanfo da no ho hia de , nanso wɔyɛ South Africa aguanfo atrae .
Chiyangwa kae sɛ Zimbabwefo abusua a wɔte South Africa no nso yɛ wɔn a wokunkum wɔn .
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ na n'ahyehyɛde no ne Zimbabweanfo ne aman foforo reyɛ adwuma de aboa wɔn ma wɔanya akwantu ho nkrataa
Zimbabwe Dwumadi a Ɛhwɛ Hokwan a Nnipa Wɔ So no kae sɛ n'ahyehyɛde no ani gye aguanfo nhyehyɛe no ho , nanso na nnipa hokwan a wonni no ho .
Dewa Mavhinga ka sɛ aguanfo da no ho hia wɔ South Africa bere a Zimbabwefo pii te hɔ sɛ aguanfo no .
Owura Mavhinga kɔɔ so hyɛɛ South Africa aban no nkuran sɛ wonsiesie mmara no , ne titiriw no , wɔ mmeae a ɛhɔ yɛ fɛ no .
Zimbabwean, George Manyika nso kaa Mavhinga's ho asɛm kyerɛɛ wɔn .
Gabriel Shumba , Zimbabwe Exiles Forum, no titrani aka Amanaman Nkabom no ho asɛm sɛ , AU ne SADC no fa aguanfo a SA , titiriw Zimbabweans dii wɔn no ho .
Lions no san de asɛm no kɔdan South Africa's yɔnko dwumayɛni Aaron Motseledi , de gye n'ahome , na ama watumi adi mmara horow so sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a aguanfo ntumi nnya nkrataa .
Ɔhyɛɛ nnipa hokwan akuw nkuran sɛ wɔne n'ahyehyɛde no mmɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛko atia hokwan ahorow a aguanfo nyinaa wɔ no .
Aguanfo no mu biako , Francis Mukono , kae sɛ ohuu hia a aguanfo da ho hia bere a na tebea no yɛ den wɔ South Africa no .
Oguanfo foforo a wɔfrɛ no Steven Chiweshe nso kae sɛ onnim nea ɔreyɛ no .
Mandela Madumise, South Africas kwankyerɛfo panyin a ɔhwɛ aguanfosɛm ho nsɛm so no ka sɛ na n'adwumam panyin no abɔ Amanaman Nkabom no Hokwan Ahorow Bagua no sobo sɛ wɔmmoa wɔn mma wonsiesie ɔhaw ahorow a na wɔrehyia wɔ adwumayɛbea hɔ no .
Madumise kae sɛ ebedu ɔsram a edi hɔ no awiei no , na n'adwumakuw no ahu nea ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ de di saa nsɛm yi ho dwuma .
Wobu akontaa sɛ Zimbabweanfo bɛboro ɔpepem abiɛsa na wɔaguan afi South Africa akɔ South Africa , na wɔabɔ wɔn ho ban sɛ aban .
Nanso Zimbabwea aban no ka sɛ nnipa bi aguan akɔ nkuraase akɔhwehwɛ adidibea pa .
Ayaresabea adwumayɛfo , a ayarehwɛfo ne nnuruyɛfo ka ho , akɔ so adi boro nnafua 33 , na wɔka sɛ wɔn sala no nnɔɔso sɛ wɔbɛyɛ adwuma a wonni ano aduru biara .
Tebea a ɛwɔ ɔmanfo ayaresabea ahorow mu no yɛ hu , na wɔn a wɔyare no bi de wɔn kɔ fie a wɔmma wɔn ayaresa .
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ tebea a ɛwɔ ayaresabea ahorow no bɛsɛe koraa bere a Oduruyɛfo Aaron Musara Ayaresa Fekuw no abɔ amanneɛ dedaw sɛ , sɛ sikasɛm mu nsɛm ne nnuruyɛfo a wɔhwɛ wɔn so no ammɔ wɔn din a . Spokesman esiane sɛ Oduruyɛfo Aaron Musara ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ , sɛ wɔanyɛ nneɛma a ɛkɔ so wɔ ayaresabea hɔ no bi a .
Ɛwom sɛ na Musara ka kyerɛ aban no sɛ wabɔ ne tirim sɛ ɔnam nkrataa so bɛkɔ adwumayɛbea ahorow de , nanso na onnyaa ho mmuae .
Ayarehwɛfo a wɔwɔ ɔmanfo ayaresabea no nyɛ adwuma , na wɔrehyɛ wɔn sɛ aban no mfa US sika a wonyae wɔ October 2018 mu no tua wɔn ka , na wɔmfa nnwinnade a wɔde bɔ wɔn ho ban fi nyarewa ho bere a wɔreyɛ wɔn adwuma no .
Zimbabwe Nurses Fekuw no titrani , ZINA, Enock Dongo , ka sɛ , kasa a wɔne aban no kasa no yɛ mmirekyie ti .
Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Ntam Dɔkta (ZHDA) kasamafo Oduruyɛfo Tapiwa Mungofa kae nso sɛ , sɛ aban no annya ayaresa ho mmoa a , ɛmma ayarefo nnya ayaresa .
Owura Mungofa kae nso sɛ bere a mmofra a wɔyɛ ayarehwɛfo no kunkum wɔn no , na wɔn abusuafo no pii wɔ fie a na wɔreko atia AWURADE - 19 no .
Ná Studio 7 ntumi nte nsɛm a aban no ka kyerɛɛ akwahosan ho adwumayɛfo a bere bi na wɔyɛ akwahosan ho ɔbenfo Amon Murwira no ampene ne telefon so

Oduruyɛfo Paulinus Sikosana a ɔyɛ Akwahosan Asoɛe no titrani kae sɛ wɔaba nhyiam bi a wɔyɛe wɔ COVID nsanyare no ase , ma enti wontumi ne yɛn nkasa .
Akwahosan ho abenfo ka nso sɛ , sɛ aban no nka ayarehwɛfo a wɔasan aba wɔn adwuma mu ho asɛm nkyerɛ wɔn , na saa ara nso na ɛnsɛ sɛ nnuruyɛfo kɔ so de wɔn ho hyɛ ogya mu , titiriw bere a ɔman no rehyia Ɔ COVID nsanyare a ekunkum nnipa 25 wɔ akyirikyiri no .
Chinhoyi Kuropɔn Bagua no ka sɛ wɔayɛ krado sɛ wobedi Asɛnnibea Kunini no so wɔ Dwoda sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ bagua no si adan a asɛe wɔ kuropɔn no mu no .
Bere a bagua no kyerɛwfo Abel Gotora rekasa wɔ nhyiam bi a wɔyɛe wɔ aguadifo a na Chinhoyi bagua no asɛe wɔn adan no ase no , ɔkae sɛ , asɛnnibea no bɛhyɛ mmara ama baguafo no asi adan a aguadifo bi asɛe no .
Nanso Owura Gotora kae sɛ bagua no rensi adan a na asɛe no nyinaa , na mmom na wobesi adan a na asɛnnibea kɛse no ahyɛ ama nnipa baasia a wɔfaa bagua no kɔɔ asɛnnibea hɔ no .
Tafadzwa Marimo, Emmanuel Ngwaru, Richard Svosve, Pepukayi Marega ne Devis Shopo ka wɔn a wɔde Chinhoyi kɔɔ asɛnnibea no ho .
Emmanuel Gwaru a ɔyɛ baasia no mu biako kae sɛ ogyee asɛnnibea no de anigye kɛse gyee asɛm no toom bere a aban no ka kyerɛɛ baguafo no sɛ wɔnhohoro beae no nkutoo , na ɛnyɛ adan a ɛyɛ hu no .
Owura Gwaru kae sɛ n'adidibea no mu biako ne sɛ na otua sika ma baguafo no ma wosisi adan a ɛyɛ fɛ . Gadzema Bagua panyin Patricia Chibaya , na ɔkae sɛ n'ani gye asɛnnibea no gyinaesi no ho bere a na ɔwɔ tebea a emu yɛ den mu no , efisɛ bere koro no ara na otua baguafo no ka sɛ ɔno nso de sika no bi na ɛyɛ wɔn ananmusifo no .
Owura Gotora bɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ baguafo no besi gua so aguadifo 50 wɔ Gadzema gua so .
Zimbabwe Mmarafo a Wɔhwɛ Hokwan a Nnipa Wɔ Ho Nsɛm So , Kumbirai Mafunda , no kasamafo no kae sɛ karkafo reba wɔn adwumayɛbea ahorow a wɔhwehwɛ mmara kwan so gyinabea no nkyɛn .
Afifide pii a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu regu adan a wɔka sɛ mmara mma ho kwan no .
Nanso aguadifo a wɔwɔ wiase afã horow no resɔre tia wɔn wɔ asɛnnibea dekode a wɔn mfɛfo no reyɛ no .
Esiane sɛ Morgan Tsvangirai wui nti , nnipa pii pɛ sɛ wohu wɔn a Richard Morgan Tsvangirai yɛ wɔn wura ankasa no .
Asennibea no kyerɛe sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ Ms Thokozani Khupe di MDC - T no akyi kosi sɛ wɔbɛtow aba .
Nanso asɛm a ɛfa wɔn a wɔhyɛn adwumakuw no adwumayɛbea ti ho no yɛ den kɛse bere a nnipa baanu a wɔhwɛ ɔdan no so , a wɔfrɛ wɔn Ian Makone ne Reverend Tim Neil , a kan no na ɛyɛ Afrika Mfinimfini anaa CPCA Asɔre no ti no .
Nhoma kyerɛwfo a ɔhwɛ MDC Alliance , Charlton Hwende , so no gye di sɛ beae no wɔ nnipa baanu no nsam , na seesei wɔn nkutoo na wɔma kwan ma wɔde di dwuma .
Douglas Mwonzora , a wɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔno nso yɛ kuw no kyerɛwfo no , asan akɔ kuw no mu wɔ 2014 mu . Ɔkyerɛ nso sɛ kuw no wɔ Makone ne Neil nsam .
Nanso wɔkae sɛ wɔbɛma wɔn kwan ma wɔayɛ adwuma wɔ wo mu . Yɛantumi ne Owura Makone ne Owura Niel ante wɔn asɛm no .
St Marys mpɔtam a ɛwɔ Chitungwiza no guamtrani a ɔhwɛ MDC a Nelson Chamisa dii anim no ka sɛ , St Mary Sikhala a ɔyɛ St Marys mpɔtam a ɛwɔ Chitungwiza no woo ahayɔfo a wɔboa ma woguan kɔ wɔn afie mu no .
Sikhala , a kan no na ɔyɛ Sengeza West MPMP , no , kae sɛ polisini panyin bi a wɔfrɛ no Jabangwe a ɔhwɛ beae a wɔakyere no so no hwehwɛɛ n'aboafo no .
Yɛbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ yebehyia Owura Jabangwe , nanso na ɔmpɛ sɛ obebua yɛn nsɛmmisa no .
Ná Studio7 nso ntumi nte asɛm no mfi polisini bi hɔ . Ɔsahene Paul Nyathi , nea enti a nkurɔfo pɛ sɛ polisifo kyere wɔn no .
Nanso wɔkyerɛ sɛ MDC akyitaafo a wɔkyeree wɔn no de wɔn ani sii wɔn so sɛ wɔbɛkasa atia ɔman no ananmusifo no .
Sikhala , a ɔsram a etwaam no , wɔbɔɔ no sobo sɛ obekum Emmerson Mnangagwa aban no , ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ nnipa pii reguan afi wɔn afie esiane sɛ wosuro sɛ wɔbɛkyere wɔn nti .
Wɔkyeree nnipa bɛboro 90 wɔ Harare a etwaam no Fida a etwaam no , na MDC no kasa tiaa wɔn da koro no ara .
MDC no pɛ sɛ wɔkasa tia nkurow akɛse a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu no , nanso polisifo de Baguam ne Atirimɔden Adwuma no fã bi rehyɛ wɔn nsa sɛ wɔnnkɔ so nsɔre ntia wɔn a wɔsɔre tia wɔn no .
Polisifo abara MDC no koraa afi Harare, Bulawayo, Gweru ne Masvingo kasa a wɔkasa tiae no mu .
Amammuisɛm mu nhwehwɛmufo ka sɛ eyi betumi aba wɔ Mutare , baabi a MDC nhyehyɛe a wɔayɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ biribi atia Yawda no nso .
Asɛnnibea Kɛse no de Ɔtemmufo Ziyam Ziyambi Ziyambi ne Finance Minister Mthuli Ncube a wɔde MDC -T a Thokozani Khupe dii n'anim wɔ mmara a ɛka koma mu no ama .
Ɔtemmufo Panyin Priscilla Munangati Manongwa dii ade Yawda sɛ ɔde Ziyambi ne Ncube a ofi MDC - Tyion bae , a wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔyɛ amanyɔkuw bi a mmara ma ho kwan , na wodi amanyɔkuw bi a wɔwɔ Amanyɔ Kuw no ase (Finance).
MDC no fi RTGS no mu ɔpepem 7,500 wɔ RTGS .
Animdefo ka sɛ Nelson Chamisa's MDC akɔ asɛnnibea wɔ Ms Khupe's Khupe'syion akyi na wɔkyerɛw nkrataa kɔmaa sikakorabea ahorow a wɔpɛ sɛ woyi Chamisafo a wɔwɔ hɔ no fii nnipa a na wɔhwehwɛ sɛ wɔde wɔn nsa hyɛ nkrataa ase de sika fi adwumakuw no Sikakorabea hɔ no hɔ
Cmisas MDC - kuo no kasamafo , Luka Tamborinyoka , kae sɛ n'ani gyee tumidi no ho .
Nanso Morgen Komichi, a ɔkyerɛe sɛ ɔyɛ adwumakuw no guamtrani wɔ Asennibea Kunini bi a edii tumi a Chamisa ne ne amanyɔkuw no penee so sɛ wɔbɛyɛ MDC kannifo no akyi no , ɔkae sɛ ɔbɛfa akwan bi so anya sika no , efisɛ ɔno ne adwumakuw no panyin no .
Nanso Owura Tamboryoka kae sɛ sika no fata no bere a MDC MDC M no de ne din hyɛɛ mmara ase no .
Nanso Komichi ka kyerɛɛ Owura Chamisa ne afoforo sɛ mmara mma wɔn kwan .
Saa bere no ara mu no , Harare mmaranimfo , Kudzai Kadzere , kae sɛ wobetumi de asɛm no akɔdan asɛnnibea no wɔ nnafua 10 ntam .
Ziyambi ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 wɔ telefon so sɛ , sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wɔko tia tumidi no sɛnea asɛnnibea no hyɛe no a , wobetumi nso de wɔn nkrataa agu asɛnnibea nna 10 .
Yɛantumi ne Yakob Mudenda , anaa Finance sɔfo no akasa bere a wɔtoo no din wɔ asɛnnibea nkrataa mu no .
Mmara ho abenfo bi ka sɛ asɛnnibea no de ahyɛde a wɔde maa wɔn no too gua sɛ sɛ wɔampene so amma Chamisa MDC no a , asɛnnibea no betumi asi gyinae sɛ wɔde sika no bɛhyɛ Chamis MDC no ase .
Eyi nyɛ bere a edi kan a MDC no adi saa sika yi ho dwuma .
Wɔ afe 2006 mu , bere a kan MDC kyerɛwfo panyin Welshman Ncube sɔre tiaa Morgan Tsvangirai wɔ October 2005 mu , na ɔde n'ankasa MDC hyehyɛɛ n'ankasa MDC no , ɔkɔɔ so gyee MDC fɛwdi no nyinaa , na ogyaee Tsvangirai , a na wɔn mu dodow no ara nni sika biako no .
Zimbabwean, Oduruyɛfo Rita Nyampinga , a ɔwɔ Female Prisoners Support Trust , a ɛko tia hokwan ahorow a mmea wɔ wɔ afiase no , kae sɛ n'ani gyei sɛ onyaa Amanaman Ntam Mmea a Wɔwɔ Akokoduru no .
Akatuafo no hu nnwuma a mmea yɛ wɔ wiase nyinaa no , na United States Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Amanaman Ntam Nsakrae Ho Nsɛm So no ka ho asɛm .
Oduruyɛfo Nyampinga kae sɛ onsusuw da sɛ obenya nidi a ɛte saa , na ɔkae sɛ n'ani agye sɛ wɔne mmea foforo 11 a wofi wiase nyinaa nim no .
Nyampinga ka sɛ wɔbɛkɔ United States mmeae pii akosua afiase tebea ho ade sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobetumi ahyɛ wɔn adwuma no mu den wɔ fie .
Oduruyɛfo Nyampinga ka sɛ wɔn adwuma no gye akokoduru na wɔn ani gye sɛ afoforo ahu adwuma a wɔreyɛ wɔ fie no .
Bere a Michael Pompeo reka dwumadi no ho asɛm no , ɔkae sɛ mmea 12 no dwumadi no yɛ nea ɛho hia na egye akokoduru .
Wɔyɛɛ dwumadi no mfe 14 a atwam ni .
Mmea foforo a wɔanya saa akatua yi no fi Afghanistan , Armenia, Azerbaijan, Bolivia, Burkino Faso, Kazakhstan, Nicaragua , Pakistan , Syria , Jmen ne Zimbabwe .
Owura Pompey kae sɛ dwumadi a ɛtete saa no ho hia bere a wɔmaa mmea hokwan ma wɔyɛɛ adwuma maa afoforo a wɔwɔ wiase nyinaa no .
Bere a ɔbea a odi kan a ɔwɔ United States, Melania Trump rekasa no , ɔkae sɛ n'ani gye hokwan a mmea a wɔwɔ wiase nyinaa reyɛ no ho .
Ɔkae sɛ , esiane sɛ wodii kan hyiaa mmea a wɔapaw wɔn sɛ wonnye wɔn ntom mfe anan a atwam ni no nti , wɔakɔ so ahyia mmea a wɔyɛ adwuma a mfaso wɔ so wɔ wiase nyinaa ɛmfa ho sɛ wɔn mu binom yɛ saa nnwuma yi na wɔhaw wɔn ho nanso wɔkɔ so yɛ saa no .
Oduruyɛfo Nyampinga ka sɛ ofii n'adwuma ase sɛ onipa hokwan a ɔde di dwuma mfe 30 a atwam ni .
Wɔ Ms Nyampinga kuw no akyi no , Mmea Nkɛntɛnso Kuw a Ɛwɔ Zimbabwe, Crisis In Zimbabwe Coalition no muni bi da so ara yɛ Mmea Mmea Asuae a Wɔko Tia Wɔn a Wodi Atirimɔden ne Mmea ne Mmoa Ho Dwuma .
Zimbabwefo mmea a wɔde Ms . Jenni Willaims , Ms . Magodonga Mahlangu , Ms . Jestina Muko ne Ms . Beatrice Mtetwa ka ho .
Akwahosan ho som adwuma no kae sɛ ɛsrɛɛ South Africa sɛ ɔnsɔ nhwɛ sɛ ebia Zimbabweni bea bi a ofi China baa ɔman no mu wɔ Benada a na ɔyare bi a wɔfrɛ no ehon ntini mu yare wɔ hɔ no anaa .
Nhwehwɛmu bi a wɔyɛe wɔ Zimbabwe no da no adi sɛ ɛnyɛ South Africas Ɔman Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Nyarewa Ho Nsɛm So no na wɔwɔ nimdeɛ sen biara wɔ South Africa atifi fam sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobehu sɛ obi anya ehon ntini no bi anaa .
Ɔbea no wɔ Wilkins Ayaresabea wɔ Harare . Oduruyɛfo Portia Manangazira , ka sɛ wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ wobehu sɛnea tebea no te wɔ nnanum ntam .
Nhyɛso ne bɔs ahorow a ɛwɔ ZUPCO bɔs adwumakuw no ase a wɔbaraa wɔn no de ɔhaw ahorow aba esiane kar a wɔmfa nkɔ nti , na ɛno ama nkurɔfo agyae bɔs gyinabea bere a ɔman no bɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛtrɛw Covid nsanyare no mu wɔ ɔman no mu no .
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ nnipa pii rehu amane esiane kar a wonni nti , titiriw wɔ anwummere no mu , a ɛma wotumi de wɔn ho hyɛ bɔs kakraa bi a ɛwɔ hɔ no mu .
Aban no ayɛ mmarahyɛfo bi a wɔabara nnipa a wɔretu kwan akɔhwehwɛ nkurɔfo wɔ Covid - 19 mu sɛ ɔkwan a wɔbɛfa so asiw ɔyare mmoawa no trɛw ano , na ɛka sɛ ZUPCO - bɔs nkutoo na wɔma kwan ma wɔsoa hyɛntiafo .
Nanso wɔkyerɛ sɛ bɔs ne bɔs ahorow bi mpɛ sɛ wɔde wɔn ho bɛhyɛ nhyehyɛe no ase esiane nneɛma ahorow bi a ZUPCO ka ho nti .
Wɔ Dwoda no , wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ adwumam no ne ZUPCO mpanyimfo yɛɛ nhyiam bi de bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wobedi wɔn haw no ho dwuma , a nea ɛka ho ne wɔn bɔs a wobetua no .
Wɔ Benada no , na wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ bɔs no ne aban mpanyimfo no besiesie akasakasa no .
Studio 7 ntumi ntee nhyehyɛe a ɛwɔ ZUPCO no ase nkyerɛɛ kar ho kwan .
Nanso Harare Residents Trust, Precious Shumba ti no kae sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ aban no di kar ho nsɛnnennen no ho dwuma ntɛm ara ansa na nneɛma akɔ so .
Agyata ka sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ aban no de polisifo , asraafo anaa baguafo ba bɔs gyinabea na ama wɔatumi ahwɛ ma mmara bi abɔ nkurɔfo ho ban afi yare no ho .
Wɔka nso sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔhwɛ akwahosan ho nsɛm so no de bɔs a ekunkum ɔyare mmoawa no di dwuma de hwehwɛ mu hu sɛ wɔwɔ HIV anaa Covid - 19 .
Nhabamma a ɛwɔ Bulawayo no ne nkurow akɛse mu ahyehyɛde ahorow hyiam susuw ɔhaw ahorow a wɔka ho sɛ nsu ho yɛ na , a wɔkyerɛ sɛ efi bere tenten na ɛde ba no ho .
Fekuw a Ɛhwɛ Sisiness a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe (ABUZ) no titrani , Victor Nyoni , kae sɛ , akuturuku no asɛe nnwuma pii a na wɔyɛ no bere a na wɔn nkurɔfo no hia nsu na ama wɔayɛ wɔn da biara da nnwuma no .
Owura Nyoni kae sɛ aban mpanyimfo a ohyiaa wɔn wɔ dapɛn a edi hɔ no mu no ama no awerɛhyem sɛ ɔbɛnom nsu wɔ dapɛn a edi hɔ no mfiase , bere a bagua no hwɛ kwan sɛ wobewie n'adwuma no wɔ dapɛn no awiei no .
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ na Bulawayo kurow no adu ne dapɛn a ɛto so abien no mu a nsu nni hɔ bere a piuncil no tu kɔ beae a wosiesie nsu wɔ Criterion Waterion Works no .
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ eyi fi nsu a ɛyow wɔ nkurow akɛse mu no titiriw na ɛmaa nsu yowee ne Magwegwe ne afei nsu a na ɛwɔ nsu a ɛsosɔ mu no .
Owura Nyoni ka sɛ wonim no yiye sɛ Bulawayo kurow no adi boro mfe 120 , na mfiri ne nsuka a ɛwɔ hɔ no akyɛ .
Ɔkɔɔ aban no ne baguafo no nkyɛn sɛ wɔnkɔfa ɔkwan a wɔbɛfa so adi ɔhaw no ho dwuma prɛko ne nyinaa ho dwuma .
Studio7 ante bagua no nka .
Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Ntam Dɔkta Fekuw a egyina hɔ ma nnuruyɛfo a wɔboro wɔn so no kae sɛ , sɛ Ɔmampanyin Emmerson Mnangagwa hyiam wɔ Wednesday nhyiam bi ase a , na wɔretwɛn
Ɔkyerɛkyerɛfo Prince Butau a ɔyɛ nhyiam no ademude no kae sɛ bere biara a Owuragagwa bɛba Yawda anaa Fida no , na ɔhwɛ kwan sɛ ɔbɛte asɛm no wɔ Mnangagwa .
Owura Mnangagwa a na wafi fie no san bae ntɛm ara sɛ ɔrebɛbɔ mmɔden sɛ ɔbɛbɔ oduruyɛfo no ho ban .
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ nneɛma a ɛwɔ ɔmanfo ayaresabea nyinaa fi bere a nnuruyɛfo kɔɔ hɔ December 1 a etwaam no .
Nanso Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Akwahosan Ho Nsɛm So panyin no kae sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ aban no di ɔhaw no ho dwuma ntɛm ara , na ɔma nnuruyɛfo a wɔwɔ sika a wɔde besiw ntɛtea ano .
Zimbabweanfo bi a wɔwɔ South Africa akasa atia Groote Schuur Ayaresabea wɔ Cape Town , baabi a wɔresa Dey Ɔmampanyin Constantino Chiwenga yare no , na wɔka sɛ Chiwenga san kɔ ayaresabea a wɔhwɛ wɔn wɔ hɔ no .
Wɔbɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔbɔɔ Owura Chiwenga fii ɔman no mu wɔ dapɛn awiei wɔ ayaresa ho wɔ South Africa no , ɛwom sɛ na Studio 7 ntumi nhu adanse biara a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɔwɔ South Africas ayaresabea a ɛsõ sen biara de .
Media Minister Monica Mutsgwa and Information Secretary Nick Mangwana ampene so sɛ wɔbɛka asɛm no Kwasida bere a VOA's Studio 7 kɔɔ Zimbabwe, na ɔhyɛɛ wɔn nkuran sɛ wɔnkyere George Charamba no .
Nanso Studio 7 antumi anhu sɛ ɛyɛ nokware sɛ Chiwenga yare , na wɔsaa no yare wɔ ayaresabea hɔ anaa .
Zimbabwean, Carlos Chimbi , a ɔte Cape Town no , kɔkaa Zimbabwefo foforo ho ma wɔsɔre tiaa wɔn .
Chimbi kae sɛ " na ne werɛ ahow yiye " sɛ ɔmampanyin bɔne no abu hokwan a nkurɔfo wɔ wɔ ɔman no mu no so bere a na onim sɛ sɛ ɔyare wɔ amannɔne a , ɔbɛhwehwɛ ayaresa no .
Ɔkae sɛ n'ani gyei sɛ otumi de n'asɛm no kɔmaa ayaresabea no sɛ ayaresabea panyin no ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ ɔne no nkasa , ɛwom sɛ na ɔnka sɛ Owura Chiwenga wɔ ayaresabea anaa
Chimbi ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ ayaresabea panyin no aka akyerɛ no sɛ mmara no mma no kwan sɛ ɔbɛka ayarefo a wɔbɛkɔ ayaresabea no ho asɛm akyerɛ wɔn .
Chiwenga bo fuwii afe a etwaam no mu bere a dɔktafo kɔbɔɔ nkurɔfo , na wɔkae sɛ wɔnyɛ adwumayɛfo a wɔn ho akokwaw , na saa ara na aban no ammɔ mmɔden sɛ obedi ɔhaw ahorow a ɛwɔ ayaresabea ahorow a ɛma nkurɔfo nya ayaresa a ɛfata no ho dwuma no .
Wonim Groote Schurr Ayaresabea no yiye sɛ ɛyɛ wiase no mu ahintasɛm a edi kan .
Polisifo abara MDC kuw no sɔre tiaa MDC no titiriw a na wonkura kyenkyenee bi mu , bere a na wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ kuw no kannifo , Nelson Chamisa , no de akwankyerɛ ne nhyehyɛe ahorow bɛma no wɔ afe yi mu no .
Bere a ɔkasafo Luka Tamborinyoka a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ Ɔmantam Nhyiam a wɔyɛe wɔ Harare no akyi no , ɔkae sɛ polisifo abara sukuu ahorow no denneennen , na ɔkae sɛ wonni adagyew koraa .
Tamborinyoka kae sɛ wɔrenyɛ nhyiam no ɔkyena efisɛ na MDC no pɛ sɛ wɔn a wogyina MDC akyi no kwati sɛ polisifo bɛhwe wɔn anaa wɔbɛtow ahyɛ wɔn so .
Ɔkae sɛ ɛda adi pefee sɛ na polisifo no rebɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛtow ahyɛ wɔn a wɔhwɛ adwumakuw no so bere a na kuw no ayɛ nhyehyɛe sɛ wɔbɛko atia nkurow ne nkurow a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu nyinaa no .
Ɔkae sɛ wɔbɛyɛ nhyiam no , na ɛsɛ sɛ wodi Agenda 2020 no asɛmti ho dwuma wɔ Ms Musodzi Hall a ɛwɔ Mbare no , na wɔde wɔn ho bɛhyɛ Benada , dapɛn a edi hɔ no , na wɔabɔ ho amanneɛ akyiri yi .
Owura Tamboryoka kae sɛ MDC no abrɛ esiane sɛ wobu no sɛ ɔyɛ omumɔyɛfo ahyehyɛde bi nti , na ɔresusuw ho sɛ ebia ɔbɛkɔ so adi mmara no so anaasɛ ɔbɛsesa nhyehyɛe no .
Na yentumi nte efi Zimbabwe Police , ZRP kasamafo Paul Nyathi , bere a na wɔn telefon a wokura kyin no nyɛ adwuma no .
Masimba Kuchera a ɔyɛ amammuisɛm mu nhwehwɛmufo no ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ ɔte nka sɛ polisifo reguan MDC .
Wɔ August a etwaam no mu no , ZRP baraa MDC no wɔ nkurow ne nkurow a ɛwɔ ɔman no nyinaa mu no ho , na ɔkae sɛ suro a wosuro sɛ atuatew no de basabasayɛ bɛba sɛnea ɛbae wɔ January mu no .
Wɔde din ato Ethiopiani Prime Minister Abiy Ahmed so wɔ afe yi mu sɛ n's Nobel Peace Prize . Norway ma eyi ho kwan .
Wɔkamfoo Ahmed sɛ ɔde asomdwoe baa ne man ne Eritrea ntam wɔ mfe 20 ntam akodi a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ aman abien ntam no akyi .
Onipa a odi kan a odii abiriw no ne Albert Luthuli a ofi South Africa wɔ 1960 mu no .
Nelson Mandela a aba foforo a ɛwɔ South Africa , Anwar Sedatat of Egypt ne Kofi Annan a ofi Ghana no ka ho .
Wɔn a wodi nkonim no bi ne Archbishop Desmond Tutu , Liberian Ɔmampanyin Ellen Johnson Sirleaf , ne Wangari Maathai a ofi
Wɔ Zimbabwe wɔ 2011 mu no , na wɔfrɛ Prime Ministeran Tsvangirai sɛ ommenya nkonimbo bi , ɛwom sɛ na onni bi de .
Ɔmampanyin Emmerson Mnangagwa ka sɛ Oduruyɛfo Ped Ruhanya , a ɔyɛ amammuisɛm ho nimdefo wɔ Johannesburg Sukuupɔn mu no wɔ nneɛma pii a ɛsɛ sɛ osua fi Ahmed's akanni nhyehyɛe mu .
Asono ne mmoa foforo pii na ɔkɔm ne nsu rekunkum wɔn wɔ Hwange National Park no mu , na ɛka wɔn ma aban no bɔ mmɔden sɛ ɛbɛtew asono dodow so .
Bere a yɛkɔɔ Studio7 a ɛwɔ Hwange National Park mpɔtam hɔ no , yehuu asono pii a aduan pa a wonnya nni a efi ɔpɛ mu bae wɔ mmeae bi wɔ afe yi mu no amu .
Zimbabwe Parks ne Wuram Mmoa Ahyehyɛde (ZimParks) kasamafo Tinashe Farawo ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ asono 85 awu fi September ne 200 na ɔkɔm akunkum wɔn afe yi .
Faraos no san kae sɛ ɔkɔm no akyi no , nneɛma atitiriw a ɛde owu ba no mu biako ne aduan ne nsu a ɛho ayɛ na ama asono ne mmoa foforo so atew no .
Sɛ ɔsono bi didi a , wɔkyerɛ sɛ ohia srade bɛboro kilogram 13500 a efi aduan mu ba no , na ɛsɛ sɛ ɔhwehwɛ nsu a emu duru boro galɔn abien .
Nanso seesei ZimParks bu akontaa sɛ asono bɛboro 45,000 na wɔwɔ mpɔtam hɔ .
Mmoa hokwan ho animdefo bi ka sɛ nnipa dodow a ZimParks yɛ atoro , na wɔka sɛ wɔreyɛ eyi sɛ ɔkwan a wɔnam so nya mmoa a wɔde ma asono .
Lenin Chisaira a ɔwɔ atifi fam no gye tom sɛ asono ne mmoa foforo di kɔm na wonnya aduan pa nni , nanso ɔyɛ ZimParks nanmusifo no mu biako .
Sɛnea Chisaira kyerɛ no , nneɛma titiriw a ɛde kɔm ba mmoa so wɔ Hwange National Park no mu biako ne aban no gyinaesi a ɛbɛma nkurɔfo ayɛ nneɛma te sɛ tu a wotu , a ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ wɔ beae a wɔte no .
Nanso Owura Farawo kae sɛ mmoa hokwan a wɔn a wɔyɛ wɔn ade no wɔ ho asɛm haw no , na ɔkae sɛ wɔmpɛ sɛ wogye nokwasɛm a ɛne sɛ asono ne mmoa afoforo renya nkɔanim esiane n'adwuma pa nti no , na ɔde ka ho sɛ wɔn a wɔpɛ sɛ wohu tebea a ɛwɔ mmoa yɛmmea hɔ no nyinaa bue hokwan ma wɔn a wɔpɛ sɛ wohu tebea no nyinaa .
Zimbabwe ne Afrika atifi fam aman foforo , a Botswana ka ho , ka sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ Amanaman Ntam Nhyiam a wɔyɛe wɔ Trade ho no ma wɔtɔn wɔn asono no bere a mmoa no dodow anya nkɔanim no , na ɛde ɔhaw pii aba , a nea ɛka ho ne nnipa ne mmoa a wowia wɔn ho ka ho .
Efi saa afe yi rekɔ no , mmoa a wɔwɔ ahyehyɛde no mu no akunkum nnipa a wɔn dodow si aduasa anum .
Wɔ CITES amanneɛbɔ bi a ɛwɔ Geneva, Switzerland wɔ August mu no , ahyehyɛde no pow ahyɛde a ɛne sɛ wɔmmara asono ne wɔn asonse ho kwan no .
Zimbabwe Ayarefo Fekuw no titrani , Emmanuel Fundira , kae sɛ ɛho hia sɛ CITES ne mmoa ho adwumayɛfo hu ɔhaw ahorow a Zimbabwe ne aman foforo a asono dodow a wɔwɔ saa aman yi mu de ba no .
Ɔsɔfo a ɔwɔ Climate ne Tourism , Nqobizitha Ndlovu , ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ aban no rebɔ mmɔden sɛ ɔbɛma aman foforo anya adwene foforo wɔ CITES no ho .
Nanso wɔkae nso sɛ wobetumi atu akɔ baabi a wɔfrɛ hɔ kwa , na ama wɔatumi de asono akɔ aman foforo a ɛwɔ CITES no so .
Hwange National Park buei wɔ 1928 mu , na ɛno ne ɔman agodibea a ɛso sen biara wɔ ɔman no mu .
Wobuu akontaa sɛ asono bɛyɛ 2,000 pɛ na wɔwɔ ahyehyɛde no mu .
Zimbabwe , FUZ , Paul Gundani , FUZ , Football Union Kyerɛwfo panyin no wui wɔ Kwekwe Wukuda awiabere wɔ Wednes yare bi a emu yɛ den akyi .
Nanso ɛda so ara nnim sɛnea nneɛma sesae .
Sɛnea FUZ, Gundani wui wɔ Topomasi Private Ayaresabea a ɛwɔ Kwekwe no .
Kuw no san ka sɛ , bere a wonni hɔ no , ɛyɛ den ma wɔn sɛ wɔbɛbɛn wɔn a wɔbɔ bɔɔl no .
Gundani, a bere bi a atwam no na odi agoru ma Zisco Steel no , ɔno nso dii agoru maa Young Warriors no , na ɔbɔɔ mmɔden maa Warriors no bere a na wɔfrɛ kuw no " Teream Team Team Team Team " wɔ Reinard Fabisch a aba so no .
FUZ nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfo Marlene Gadzirayi kae sɛ ne ho dwiriw no bere a ɔtee sɛ Gundani awu no .
" SƐNEA me ne wɔn kasae nnɛrara , na yɛayɛ nhyehyɛe dedaw sɛ yɛbɛyɛ no . Nanso metee sɛ wɔayera , nanso saa bere yi de , minnim nea Owura Gundani didi no , Ms Gadzira ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 .
Ms Gadzirayi ka sɛ , ɔman no abɔ bɔɔl kɛse bi a wɔfrɛ no hero Ms Gadzirayi . Ms Gadzirayi kae nso sɛ bere a Owura Gundanis reyɛ ayi no , na onni nhyehyɛe biara a ɔde retwɛn sɛ obetie n'abusua bere a wɔde no rekɔ akogye n'ahome no .
Zimbabwe Football Association (ZIFA) abɔ ne wɛbsaet ho amanneɛ sɛ Gundanis wu na abusua no begyina n'ayi nhyehyɛe no nyinaa mu .
MPANYIMFO bi a wɔfrɛ no Xolisani Gwesele kae sɛ Gundanis wu yɛ ɔman mu asiane , na ɛbɛyɛ den sɛ wobehu ɔbarima bi a ɔbɔ bɔɔl .
" Gwesela kyerɛw ne ho asɛm wɔ ZIFAbsni so sɛ: " Paulo Gundani Gwesela wɔ wo so .
Kan Ɔmampanyin Robert Mugabe amu no ntumi nkɔɔ ne fie wɔ Zvimba nnɛ bere a ne yere, Grace Mugabe yare no .
Abusuafo bi ka sɛ nipadua no fi Zvimba wɔ Dwoda .
Nnipa a wɔn dodow yɛ 1,000 na wɔretwɛn Ɔmampanyin Mugabes amu da koro wɔ Zvimba awia yi
Mugabe abusua no kasamafo , a ɔno nso yɛ owufo no , Leo Mugabe , na ɔkae sɛ Mugabefo ntumi nhu no nnɛ esiane sɛ ɔkae sɛ onnim sɛnea Ɔhene Zvimba asoma no nti .
Leo Mugabe kae sɛ nipadua no bedu fie anɔpatutuutu .
Nanso Ɔhene Katizagombo a wɔsan frɛ no Gibson Jenami no kae sɛ nipadua no renkɔ Zvimba sɛnea na wɔhwɛ kwan fi bere a na Ms Grace Muga yare no .
Ɔhene Katizagombo kae nso sɛ amu no bɛhyɛ aban nsa de akosi da a wɔbɛhome .
Nanso eyi ne Leo Mugabe , a ɔkae sɛ Mugabes abusua no de wɔn nkwa bɛto asiane mu kosi sɛ wobewie ɔdamoa kɛse bi no bɔ abira .
Ɔmampanyin Mugabe's ayiyɛ mu anibiannaso ama nnipa pii ho adwiriw wɔn esiane sɛ ebia Mugabe amu no bedu hɔ bɛyɛ nnafua 30 ansa na wɔasie no nti .
Leo Mugabe kae sɛ Mugabe's amu no bɛtra Zvimba da koro , na afei wasan akɔ Harare a wɔde no ato hɔ no .
Leo Mugabe kae sɛ nkurɔfo ahyiam wɔ Ɔmampanyin Mugabes fie wɔ Harare .
Ɔsɔretia a Nelson Chamisa de baa Nelson Chamisa so no mu biako a na ɔhwɛ kwan sɛ obewu wɔ Zvimba nnɛ no , Lloyd Tarubwa a ɔwɔ Banket no , a wɔde no too afiase asram akron a na wonnii n'asɛm no kae sɛ wɔaba bɛhwɛ sɛ Ɔmampanyin Mube awu ampa anaa .
Owura Mugabe's ayiyɛ no ama nnipa pii ho adwiriw wɔn wɔ ɔman no mu , na wɔkyerɛ sɛ Owura Mugabes yare no na ɛde ne wu no bae .
Owura Mugabe wui wɔ Singapore September 6 bere a yare bi a emu yɛ den bɔɔ no no .
Amalgamated Rural Teachers Union of Zimbabwe, anaa ARTUZ ka sɛ , wɔn akannifo no mu biako , Godfrey Chanda , huu wɔn , na wɔde nnɔnhwerew abien yɛɛ adwuma wɔ Gweruoutfo no nimdeɛ mu .
Nanso , bere a wɔhyɛɛ Chanda , a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ Ɔhotefo Panyin Boayikuw a ɛwɔ Midland mantam mu no ma wɔde nnwontofo kɔyɛɛ nhyiam wɔ Gweru no , wɔayi no adi .
TUZ Obert Masaraure kae sɛ Chanda's bɔ akuturuku a ɔhyɛ n'amenade nnanu no ase no kɔɔ soro mprɛnsa .
Masaraure ka sɛ fekubɔne bi redɔɔso wɔ ɔkwan a wɔfa so hwɛ wɔn ho wɔn ho so .
Wukuda na ɔyɛkyerɛ no ba awiei .
Nanso Masaraure kae sɛ wɔbɛyɛ nhyiam bi bere a wɔabɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛyɛ ho biribi no .
Yɛantumi ne Ms Sekai Nzenzafo a wɔyɛ adwuma no anni nkitaho , na mmom yɛannya ne telefon a wokura kyin no ho mmuae .
FC Platinum's fi Caf Champions League no de nsemmisa pii a ɛfa Zimbabwean bɔɔlbɔ ho no
Ɛwom sɛ wɔda so ara wɔ agodie abien wɔ akansi no mu de , nanso FC Platinum rentumi nkura Esperancefo a wɔwɔ nyansahyɛ awotwe no mu bio , na saa ara nso na wɔrentumi nhwe Horoya Athletic Club a wɔwɔ nsɛntitiriw ason no . Bere a wɔhwee wɔn wɔ fie ne Horoya a Horoya a wodii kan hwɛɛ so no .
Saa bere no , FC Platinum wɔ agodie anan pɛ , enti wɔrebɔ mmɔden sɛ wobedi wɔn agodie a aka no ho dwuma sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobenya Spr Mushambadope agodie no mu anigye foforo .
Mushambadope ka sɛ biribi pa biara remfi mu mma wɔn a aka no .
Afe a etwaam no , Angolafo Primeiro de Agosto de , bere a Lunda san hwee wɔn wɔ fie no , woyii kuw koro no ara adi
Wɔ 2017 mu no , Caps United duu nsrahwɛ no fã bi a ɛyɛ hu nanso bere a wɔhwee nnipa 4 - 2 wɔ fie wɔ Ahli Tripoli of Libya no , wɔantumi annu anan no .
Afe koro no ara mu no , wɔbɔɔ Ngezi Platinum Stars a na wogyina Zimbabwe ananmu wɔ Caf Confederation no mu no fii beae a edi kan bere a Angolani Libolo hwee wɔn no .
Wɔ 2016 mu no , bere a wɔboroo Harare Kuropɔn a na akansi koro no ara rekɔ so wɔ Zanaco mantam a edi kan wɔ Zanaco mu bere a wɔhwee no 2 - 1 wɔ Rufaro Stadium , na afei owiee 3 - 1 wɔ Zambia no .
Eyi da no adi sɛ ɛhɔnom akuw no ntumi ne Afrikafo akuw afoforo nni nkitaho te sɛ nea na ɛte wɔ mfe bi a atwam no mu bere a Dynamos sii akan yiye de koduu Caf Champions League Apam a etwa to wɔ 1998 mu ne nkaedum a etwa to wɔ 2008 mu no .
Nea ɛyɛ yaw sen biara ne sɛ FC Platinum wɔ agodie anan pɛ mu biako pɛ , nanso wɔmfaa asɛm biako pɛ nhyɛɛ mu , na mpɛn pii no , wɔpenee so mpɛn asia wɔ agodie anan mu .
Asɛmmisa no ne sɛ , sɛ kuw bi rehwe akuw a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe no nyinaa na wɔredi agoru te sɛ eyi wɔ Afrika a , dɛn na ɛkyerɛ ma ɔman no bɔɔlbɔ a emu yɛ den no
Caps Unitedary Tinashe Musebi ka sɛ bɔɔlbɔ asɛe araa ma ɛho abehia sɛ wɔyɛ nsakrae pii ansa na Zimbabwefo kuw ahorow no ahwe ase a ɛboro Lesotho, Botswana ne Swaziland so .
Football ho sɛnkyerɛwfo Farai Kambamura ka sɛ Zimbabwefo akuw no ntumi nni agoru wɔ Afrika efisɛ agumadifo a wɔboa wɔn ma wonyaa abodin a enni ano wɔ Zimbabwe no rekɔ amannɔne , titiriw bere a wɔresi akan wɔ South Africa no .
Afe a etwaam no , FC Platinum hweree Gerald Takwara, Elvis Chipeze ne Talwapiwa , na afe yi wɔhweree Rodwell Chinyafanere , a ɔde afe trophy a ɔkɔɔ Baroka no nkwa .
Nanso John Chikochi , a odii Lengthens kuw a ɛwɔ Premier League no anim no kae sɛ ɛho hia sɛ Zimbabwe bɔ bɔɔ bɔɔlbɔ ho dawuru kɛse wɔ ɔman no mu sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a kuw no betumi atua ka na amma wɔantumi anguan ankɔ South Africa ne Zambia .
Seesei , Zimbabwe wɔ akuw abien pɛ , Castle Lager Remier League ne Chibuku Super Cup . Wodii agoru wɔ afe 2005 mu .
Musa Masepe , a ɔyɛ bɔɔlbɔfo no ka sɛ Zimbabwe nni bɔɔlbɔ mu dwetikɛse biara bere a agumadifo reto dwom anaa biribi foforo te sɛ wɔn nkyereso a ɛwɔ bɔɔlbɔ mu no .
Sɛ eyi kɔ so a , ebegye bere na ama ɛhɔnom akuw no ne Afrikafo akuw foforo asi akan .
Mmara ahorow a wɔde gyina hɔ ma Democratic Amanyɔ Kuw a ɛwɔ US no mu wɔ November mu no retwe adwene asi kan New York mampanyin Michael Bloomberg a wɔtow aba paw wɔn no so .
Bloomberg, a wabɛyɛ ɔdefo kɛse no ammɔ mmɔden sɛ obedi n'ananmusifo no anim wɔ ɔmampanyin abadiakyiri , a Republican Kuw no kasamafo Donal Trump bɛfrɛ no no mu .
Owura Bloomberg bɔɔ amanneɛ wɔ November afe a etwaam no mu sɛ ɔde ne ho rehyɛ kuw no mu , na ɔde bɛboro dɔla ɔpepem 400 na ɛbɔɔ aguade ho dawuru .
Ɔdefo no ammɔ mmɔden wɔ Iowa ne New Hampshire nniso no mu , na saa ara nso na ɔrentu mmirika a wɔnam ahyɛde a ɛwɔ Navada ne South Carolina, a wɔde too abatow no mu , bere a 14 ka sɛ wɔbɛtow aba bi a wɔde rebesi Democratic Party ananmu no .
Bere a Bloomerg de ne nan too fam hwehwɛɛ adwumayɛbea hɔ ara pɛ , te sɛ Bernie Sanders , a ɔyɛ Vermont a ɛwɔ Senate , ne Elizabeth Warren , a ogyina Massachusetts ananmu wɔ Senate no , fii ase buu Bloomberg afebɔɔ .
Bere a Owura Sanders reka Nevada amammuisɛm ho asɛm no , ɔkae sɛ nea ɛbɛyɛ na watumi adi Owura Trump so nkonim no , na ehia sɛ obi a obetumi asiw nnipa pii kwan sen bere biara wɔ Amerika abakɔsɛm mu .
Owura Sanders ka kyerɛɛ Owura Bloomberg sɛ obi a wonim no yiye wɔ New York nkurow mu a ɔpɛ sɛ ohu abibifo , ne afei Latinos a na wɔreyɛ saa no . Ɔkae sɛ , sɛ obi tu kɔ hɔ a , ɔrennya nnipa pii mma wɔnkɔtow aba mma Owura Trump nkyia wɔ November mu .
Nanso Bloomerg bɔɔ Owura Sanders'asɛm no gui , na ɔkae sɛ Owura Sanders , a odi nsra no anim no , wɔapaw Democratic Party Kuw a ɛwɔ ɔmampanyin abadiakyiri no , na Owura Trump adi mfe anan a edi hɔ no .
Amammuisɛm mu nhwehwɛmufo bi ne Zanu PF a ɔyɛ Frank Guni no kae sɛ ɛda adi pefee sɛ na abusuabɔ titiriw a ɛda Sanders ne Bloomberg ntam no yɛ nea ɛda adi pefee sɛ na Sanderfo no wɔ akyitaafo pii saa bere yi .
Guni ka sɛ , wɔ ne fam no , ɛsɛ sɛ Sanders ne Bloomberg bom tow aba paw ɔmampanyin na ama wɔatumi adi Tomp so nkonim .
Ebinom a wɔwɔ Democratic Party no ka sɛ; Barack Obama's kan amrado , Joe Biden; Minnesotator Amy Klobuchar , ne kan South Bend a kan no na ɔyɛ South Indiana , ne ɔbarima bi a wɔfrɛ no pey, Pete Buttigie Buttigieg .
Democratic Party no wɔ nhyiamfo 3,979 , na ɛsɛ sɛ wohu obi sɛ ɔyɛ obi a ɔkorɔn sen ɔmampanyin no , enti ɛbɛyɛ sɛ ɔno ankasa na ɔyɛɛ nhyiamfo 1,990 (1,990).
Nhyiamfo no akyi no , nhyiamfo no wɔ hɔ nso ananmusifo a wɔkorɔn sen wɔn , sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a sɛ wɔyɛ Democratic Nhyiam no wɔ July mu wɔ Wisconsin a , ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde nnipa 4,750 ne wɔn a wɔhwɛ wɔn so , na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔtow aba paw wɔn wɔ nhyiam yi ase no nya ogya 2,200 .
Nnipa pii kɔ sikakorabea anɔpatutuutu , a wɔwɔ anidaso sɛ wobenya sika de ahwɛ wiase nyinaa sikakorabea akɛse a ɛso sen biara no kwan , nanso wɔatra afiri a wɔde asie mu .
Nhwehwɛmu bi a Studio 7 yɛe wɔ sikakorabea ahorow a ɛwɔ Harare, Bulawayo, Chinhoyigo, Masvingo, Mutare, ne nkurow foforo mu no daa no adi sɛ sika foforo ne sikakorabea pii ntumi mfaa dedaw no mmaa nnipa no .
Jossam Marwira a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ sikakorabea hɔ no mu biako kae sɛ na ɔretwɛn sika no da koro , sɛnea na wate wɔ asɛm a ɔkae sɛ wɔde sika foforo bɛka ho no .
Owura Marwira kae sɛ nea ɛhaw no titiriw ne sika a ɔbɛtɔ wɔ mmɔnten so , na ɔkae sɛ ɛbɛyɛ papa sɛ nkurɔfo a wɔte sɛ ɔno betumi anya sika afi sikakorabea a wonnye hwee .
Ɔbarima bi a ɔtɔ sika tɔnee wɔ mmɔnten so a wɔammɔ no din no nso ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ ɔno nso rehwɛ ade foforo no kwan , nanso wanhu hwee .
RBZ, sikakorabea a ɛwɔ mfinimfini fam no bɔɔ amanneɛ nnansa yi sɛ ɛde sikasɛm mu ahokyere foforo bɛba ɔman no mu .
RBZ Amrado John Mangudya abɔ amanneɛ sɛ ɔde sika hama a ne bo yɛ $ 2 ne $ 2.5 a na wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ ɛbɛma obi anya abusuabɔ a emu yɛ den nnɛ no bɛba .
Zimbabwe mampanyin Webster Rusere a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ sikakorabea no titrani no kae nso sɛ wonnya nhuu sɛ ebia sikakorabea no mu bi nsa aka sika no bi , na wɔkae sɛ RBZ nkutoo ne
Sikasɛm ho aguadi ho ɔsɛmpɔw no de akyinnyegye ba ɔman no mu , na ebinom ka sɛ ɛbɛboa nkurɔfo a wɔhaw wɔn ho wɔ sika ho bere a afoforo ka sɛ ɛyɛ ɔhaw no .
Zimbabwefo a wɔreka kar wɔ South Africa no ho adwiriw wɔn wɔ kar a South Africafo a wɔn ani nnye ho sɛ wobenya adwuma ayɛ no ho .
South Africa aban asomfo a wɔyɛ polisifo, Bheki Cele; Transport Minister Fikile Mbalula; ne Laboras Nxesi Asomfo no yɛɛ nhyiam bi a karkafo ne wɔn a wɔyɛ adwumawuranom yɛe de bɔɔ kɔkɔ sɛ wɔnyɛ biribi ntia wɔn a wɔrehyew lɔre no .
Ná Cele abɔ karkafo kɔkɔ wɔ ogya mu sɛ wɔbɛkyere wɔn bere a wɔsɛe sikasɛm mu nsɛm no .
Nanso bere a wowiee kar bi a wɔhyewee wɔ N2 mu wɔ Durban no , ankyɛ na wɔde nnɔnhwerew abien pɛ na ɛyɛɛ saa .
Polisini bi a ɔyɛ kasamafo , Senior Superindent Parboo Sewpersad , gye toom sɛ wɔde kar foforo asi ogya mu .
Wɔyɛɛ lɔre ahorow 18, a Zimbabwefo afoforo suro nso ka ho wɔ KwaZulu - Natal ne Gauteng .
Zimbabwe Exiles Forum, Gabriel Shumba , guamtrani no kae sɛ wɔde lɔre no afa akwantempɔn a ɛwɔ SA no so so , na ɛmaa kwan no so tewee bere tiaa bi .
Bere a Edward Muchatuta a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ South Africas Zimbabwe Ɔmanfo Ahobammɔ Asoɛe no kae sɛ bere a asɛm no sii akyi no , ɔne afoforo a wofi amannɔne nso kasa tiaa bi , na ɔkae sɛ SA aban no mfa ne ho nnye mu .
Wɔn a wɔka kar no mu biako , George Nanyika , ahwehwɛ ayamtu .
Davie Munodawafa , ofirikafo foforo , kae sɛ na osuro sɛ obenya nkwa .
Munadawafa kɔɔ so kae sɛ afirikafo pii nnim wɔn daakye .
South Africas polisi panyin, Bheki Cele, nnɛraday bɔɔ kɔkɔ sɛ polisifo bɛyɛ ade atia wɔn a wɔde ogya to kar no mu no .
Lions ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ asɛm no yɛ nea na South Africafo aka dedaw sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ aman foforo fi SA .
Sumba akasa atia nsɛnkyerɛwfo nso esiane sɛ wɔanka asɛm no ankyerɛ ɔmanfo nti .
Lions toaa so kae sɛ wɔn ahyehyɛde no akyerɛw nkrataa akɔ aman foforo so ananmusifo a wɔwɔ South Africa , a Zimbabwe ka ho , no , asrɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnbom nyɛ adwuma mfa ɔhaw no mma awiei .
Dewa Mavhinga , Human Rights Watch's
Sikasɛm mu ahokyere aka Zimbabweanfo ma wɔakɔhwehwɛ adwuma wɔ South Africa , a ahokyere a emu yɛ den aba Afrikafo so bere a South Africafo nwiinwii sɛ amannɔnefo anyɛ adwuma no .
Asennibea no ahyɛ polisifo sɛ wɔmmara Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Ntam Dɔkta Peter Magombeyi , sɛ wɔnkɔ South Africa nkɔsa wɔn a wɔkyere nkurɔfo sie no yare wɔ September 14 .
United States rema Zimbabwe dɔla ɔpepem 42 . Wɔde sika no bɛtɔ aduan ama nnipa ɔpepem biako fi ɔsram a edi hɔ besi May 2020 mu .
Wɔn a wɔkɔɔ Gwanda nkuraase wɔ Matabeleland South mantam mu ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ aban no mfaa nnwuma titiriw bi nsii , na saa ara na ankorankoro fekuw no nnya nkɔso ahe biara .
United States Ɔmampanyin , Donald Trump , na ɔbɛkyerɛ Amanaman Nkabom Nhyiam Kɛse no ase wɔ New York .
MDC kannifo no ne Harare kurow no baguafo hyiam hwehwɛ akwan a wɔbɛfa so adi nsu ho nsɛnnennen ho dwuma wɔ kurow no mu .
Wɔ dwumadi a ɛne The Connection on LiveTalk no mu no , yesusuw nea mmofra betumi ayɛ de ama ɔman sikasɛm ho nhyehyɛe no ho , sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a mmofra ntumi mfi wɔn aman mu nkɔpɛ aduan a a ahabammono wom wɔ aman foforo a wohyia basabasayɛ a ɛka ahɔho a wɔwɔ wɔn man mu no mu .
Sɛ wopɛ sɛ wunya dwumadi no mu kyɛfa anaa wode nkrasɛm kɔma Studio7 a , fa 001 465 0318.
Ɔpɛ a yɛwɔ sɛ yebetie Studio7 no ka yɛn wɔ 909 mu; 6040, ne 15460 Kilohertz daa wɔ Shortwave .
Wubetumi nso ate Studio7 wɔ 6 - Dwoda kosi Fida , wɔ 909, 7270, ne 985 Shortve .
Zimbabwe Fida kɔkaa wiase no fã a aka a ɛhyɛ Amanaman Ntam Mmea Da agyirae no ho , na mmea pii ka sɛ wɔkɔ so hyɛ wɔn so na wɔhwere wɔn nneɛma , efisɛ atumfoɔ a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu no mfa wɔn ho nhyɛ hokwan koro mu .
Ɛwom sɛ Zimbabwe wɔ amanyɔkuw bi a ɛde hokwan a mmea ne mmarima wɔ yɛ pɛ de , nanso mmea a yɛkaa wɔn ho asɛm kyerɛɛ wɔn no mu pii kae sɛ ɛho nhia anaa ɛho nhia sɛ aban mpanyimfo , amammuifo , anaa nnwumakuw ahorow , na wɔhwɛ ma eyi ba mu .
Ms Jessy Majomeme , a kan no na ɔyɛ mmaranimfo ne mmaranimfo no , ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ mmea rehu amane kɛse wɔ ɔman no mu esiane mmarima a wodi wɔn anim nti .
Wɔka sɛ hokwan kɛse wɔ hɔ a ebetumi ama ɔman no atoto nsonsonoe a ɛda mmea ne mmarima ntam no mu , sɛ wodi amanyɔkuw no akyi a .
Zimbabwe Mmea Mmara Fekuw no titrani , Abigail Matsvai , ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ ɛnnɛ yɛ da a ɛho hia paa , na wɔde di dwuma de hyɛ aban no nkuran ma wodi mmara horow a ɛfa hokwan ahorow a mmarima ne mmea wɔ ho no so .
Owura bi a wɔfrɛ no Ms . Tsungirai Hungwebunde - Chimbunde ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ nhomasua a emu yɛ den ho hia na ama ɔmanfo ahu hia a ɛho hia sɛ wonya hokwan a ɛte saa wɔ mmea ne mmarima ntam no .
Ɔkae sɛ n'asɛyɛde ne sɛ ɔbɛbɔ mmɔden adu amammui akuw ahorow mu ma wɔde hokwan koro no ara ama wɔn akwaa sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a mmea pii betumi atu mmirika akɔ adwumayɛbea .
Afe yi , wodi afahyɛ ahorow wɔ asɛmti no ase , Susuw Equal, Build Smart, Innovate for Change ho .
Ms Majome kae wɔ asɛmti no ho sɛ , ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde anyinam ahoɔden yi di dwuma na ama mmea ne mmarima nyinaa anya akongua koro wɔ po so ahyɛn 2023 no mu .
Ms . Matsvai aboa akuw a wɔyɛ nsakrae yi wɔ wɔn akanni mu no .
Ms Majome kae nso sɛ ɛho hia sɛ mmea yɛ biako na wɔko tia wɔn ntɔkwaw no , na ɛnsɛ sɛ mmarima di wɔn ho fɛw .
Ɔkae sɛ ɛda adi pefee sɛ mmarima pii a wɔwɔ adwumayɛbea no mpɛ sɛ wofi apontow no ase , na ɛno nti na wɔko tia mmea , na wɔmma wɔn hokwan pii a wɔde bɛyɛ adwuma no .
Wɔhyɛ Amanaman Ntam Mmea Da no afe biara wɔ March 8 sɛ ɔkwan a wɔnam so di mmea nya nkɔso wɔ sikasɛm mu , amammui ne nsase foforo so , ne afei hokwan a mmea ne mmarima a wɔwɔ wiase nyinaa nya sɛe no .
Wodii aban afahyɛ ahorow wɔ Gokwe a ɛwɔ Midland mantam mu ne ahyehyɛde ahorow pii nso wɔ mmeae ahorow .
Nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfo afoforo a wɔwɔ hɔ nnɛ , a Zimbabwe Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Hokwan a Nnipa Wɔ So ka ho , kae sɛ ɛyɛ den ma mmea sɛ wɔbɛkɔ wɔn anim wɔ sikasɛm tebea a ɛrekɔ so mprempren no mu bere a obiara mma wɔn kwan no .
Zimbabwe Peace Project no nso de asɛm bi ama de akyerɛ da a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛkasa tia hokwan a nnipa wɔ sɛ wɔyɛ wɔn ayayade , a nea ɛka ho ne hokwan a nnipa wɔ wɔ ɔman bi akyi a wɔtew atua no .
Labor Asennibea no abu atɛn sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ mmofra a wɔyɛ adwuma no san kɔ adwuma wɔ nnɔnhwerew 48 mu bere a wɔn dwumadi no yɛ nea mmara mma ho kwan no .
Asɛnnibea a Ɛhwɛ Ayaresa Ho Nsɛm ne Mmara a Wɔde Maa Murasi no de nnanu ama nnuruyɛfo no sɛ wɔnsan nkɔ adwuma .
Asennibea no san kyerɛe sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔtwe adwene si akasakasa a ɛda mmofra ne aban ntam no so na ama wɔatumi adi asɛm no ho dwuma wɔ nnafua 14 ntam .
Owura Masimba Ndoro , a kan no na ɔyɛ Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Dɔktafo Fekuw no muni no kae sɛ , ɛmfa ho sɛ na atumfoɔ no wɔ tumi no , nnuruyɛfo no antumi ankɔ adwuma .
Bere a Studio7 bisabisaa wɔn nsɛm sɛ sɛ wɔanni bagua no ahyɛde so a , ɛsɛ sɛ Adwumayɛfo no yɛ wɔn ho adwuma na wɔsan de wɔn ho hyɛ adwuma mu .
Oduruyɛfo a ɔhwɛ Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Ntam Dɔmyɛn , Doug Coltart , no kae sɛ onnye nea ebefi mu aba no ntom , na mmom ɔhwehwɛɛ nea enti a ɛte saa no mu .
Coltart kae nso sɛ ɔwɔ hokwan sɛ ɔde asɛm no kɔdan Asɛnnibea Kunini no bere a nnuruyɛfo pɛ sɛ wɔyɛ ho biribi no .

Dɔktafo no kɔɔ so kunkum wɔn September 3 , na wɔkae sɛ wonni adwuma biara a wɔbɛyɛ .
Dapɛn a etwaam no mu no , nnuruyɛfo a wɔhwɛ ayarefo a wɔn mfe akɔ anim a na wɔwɔ adwuma no mu nso de wɔn ani kyerɛɛ baabi a wɔtra no , na wonwiinwii wɔ nyarewa ne tebea a ɛwɔ ayaresabea ahorow mu no ho .
US aban no ka sɛ Cyclone Idai sɛee Manicaland ɔmantam no pasaa , na awerɛhosɛm no bɛkɔ so aka nkurɔfo no .
Bere a Jason Taylor , USAID's kwankyerɛfo reka Studio 7 ho asɛm wɔ US nhyiam no ase no , ɔkae sɛ bere a wɔne nnwumakuw foforo reyɛ adwuma na wɔasan asi adan a asɛe no , afei de wɔde wɔn ani asi aduan ho nhyehyɛe a ɛbɛma wɔanya ahobammɔ no so .
Taylor kae sɛ Manicaland ho nsɛnnennen no mu yɛ den araa ma Zimbabwe aban no ankasa antumi anyɛ .
Taylor, a ɔkɔsraa Manicaland ɔmantam bi a ɛwɔ Wiase Nyinaa Aduan Ho Nhyehyɛe , a ɛhɔ na ɔde ne ho hyɛ mu no kae sɛ ne ho dwiriw no sɛ ohuu adwennwen a ɛwɔ ɔmantam no mu no .
Ɔkae sɛ mmofra a ohuu wɔn no nni anigye . Ɔkae sɛ , sɛ nnipa a wɔwɔ Manicaland no nya nneɛma te sɛ aduan ne atrae so mfaso a , ɛsɛ sɛ wɔboa wɔn nso ma wonya ahotɔ .
Taylor kae nso sɛ , wɔ Chimani ne Chipinge no , wɔanhu wɔn a wɔte hɔ no anaa wɔne wɔn a wɔkae sɛ wɔnhwehwɛ mmoa mfi amanyɔkuw no hɔ no .
USAID aka nso sɛ ɔwɔ nimdeɛ a ɔde bɛtete Zimbabweans ma wahu bere a ahum no besi , ne baabi a ɛda adi sɛ ebetumi asi , ne nneɛma a wobetumi ayɛ de asiw asetra ne asase a aban no srɛe no kwan .
Efi bere a Cyclone Idai fii ase no , United States ama Zimbabwe anya dɔla ɔpepem 2.6 .
Saa bere no ara mu no , aban no , Amanaman Nkabom no ne ahyehyɛde ahorow a wɔnyɛ asraafo a wɔwɔ hɔ nnɛ no de sika dɔla ɔpepem 60 a egye ntɛmpɛ maa Cyclone Idai .
Wobu akontaa sɛ nnipa bɛyɛ 300,000 na wohia mmoa wɔ Manicaland mantam mu , na wɔn mu 129,000 yɛ mmofra .
Wɔ amantam akron a Cyclone Idai, 113 no mu no , wɔsɛee sukuufo 90,000 a na wonni afie pa no .
Aban no ka sɛ nnipa bɛboro 300 na wɔammɔ wɔn din , na nnipa 399 na wowuwui wɔ ɔbotan no mu .
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ saa dodow yi bɛsɔre .
Ayarefo bi ka sɛ mmofra ayarehwɛfo a wɔka sɛ wobetumi awu wɔ ayaresabea ahorow a wɔmma wɔn ayaresa no resa wɔn yare wɔ amannɔne .
Nhwehwɛmu bi a Studio 7 yɛe no ama ada adi sɛ seesei ayarefo bi retu kwan akɔ aman foforo te sɛ South Africa, Botswana ne Zambia akɔhwɛ wɔn wɔ hɔ .
Ayarefo a yɛkaa wɔn ho asɛm kyerɛɛ wɔn wɔ Parirenyatwa , Ms Molline Chindove no mu biako kae sɛ na waba ayaresabea hɔ nna pii , nanso na onni baabiara .
Ms Chindove kae sɛ ɔrekɔ South Africa akɔhwɛ no yare esiane sɛ na osuro sɛ ɔde ne nan bekum sukɔm wɔ nsu no mu nti .
Fiona Muchabaiwa a ɔyɛ n'abusuafo no mu biako kae sɛ onni hokwan biara sɛ ɔde ne ɔyarefo no bɛkɔ Zambia ɔkyena akɔsa no yare , na ɔkae sɛ ne bo yɛ den dodo .
Nhwehwɛmu bi a Studio 7 yɛe no ama ada adi sɛ ɔmanfo ayaresabea pii a kan no na wɔwɔ hɔ no rema nnipa pii anya ayaresa a wɔde bɛhwɛ wɔn ho wɔn ho .
Wilbert Kasanze kae sɛ wafa ne yere afi Chegutu General Ayaresabea hɔ sɛ wɔnkɔsa no yare wɔ ayaresabea bi a ɛwɔ Chitungwiza .
Kasaze ka sɛ da biara bɔs no te Chegutu , baabi a ɔte kɔ Chitungwiza no , na ɔma ne bokiti no tu mmirika .
Akwahosan Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Mmofra Ho Nsɛm So no abɔ amanneɛ sɛ mmofra a wɔakɔ pɛnhyen no bɛsan aba fie ntɛm ara .
Na baguafo no san kɔ wɔn a wokunkum wɔn no mu biara nkyɛn kɔ , na wɔhyɛɛ wɔn nkuran sɛ sɛ wɔda so ara pɛ adwuma a , wɔnsan mfa wɔn ho nhyɛ mu .
Eyi akyi no , asɛm bi a Ɔmampanyin Constantino Chiwenga ka kyerɛɛ ayarehwɛfo a wɔboro wɔn nyinaa sɛ wonnyae no .
Nanso Zimbabwe Doctors for Human Rights ka sɛ mmara mma a aban no bɔ mmofra gu sɛ ɔyarehwɛfo a ɔmmɔ wɔn din no yɛ nea mmara mma ho kwan .
Football , Lionel Messi , a ɔbɔ mmɔden ma Argentina ne Spaniafo fekuw Barcelona no ka sɛ , bere a ɔne ne man no agyae aware no , ɔne ne man no retetew mu .
Messi kaa nsɛm no bere a Copa America nsrahwɛfo a wɔwɔ United States de wɔn ho hyɛɛ mu bere a Argentina hweree Chile nea etwa to koraa wɔ Chile bere a Chile maa kar no so no .

Yɛabɔ mmɔden sɛ yɛbɛte tebea no afi ayaresabea hɔ panyin , Leonard Mabande , nanso ɔkae sɛ yɛakasa akyerɛ oduruyɛfo panyin , Oduruyɛfo Xolani Ndlovu , a ɔkae sɛ ontumi nkasa nkyerɛ yɛn sɛnea na ɔwɔ adwuma pii yɛ no .
Wɔ United Bulawayo Ayaresabea a Ɛhwɛ Ayaresa Ho Nsɛm So no , ayaresabea ahorow no atotom , na nnuruyɛfo panyin , Oduruyɛfo Narcisaus Dzvanga nso ahu sɛ ayarefo a wɔyare no ani gye ho ara kwa .
Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Ntam Dɔkta Mthabisi Bhebhe kae sɛ nnuruyɛfo akɔ so abɔ ɔman no afanan nyinaa ɛmfa ho sɛ aban hwehwɛ sɛ wɔsan kɔ adwuma no , na wɔka sɛ wɔntee wɔn mfii aban no nsam .
Oduruyɛfo Ndlovu kae sɛ ahiafo a wɔwɔ ayaresabea , a nnuru ne nneɛma foforo a wonni ka ho , ne ade titiriw nti a wɔbɔɔ wɔn no .
Studio 7 antumi ante asɛm no ase bere a na yentumi ne akwahosan ho somfo , Oduruyɛfo Obadia Moyo , nni nkitaho no .
Nanso Ɔbenfo John Mangwiroro, ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 wɔ telefon so sɛ wontumi nka asɛm no ho asɛm bere a wofi ɔman no mu ne Dwumadibea a Ɛhwɛ Nsɛm Ho Nsɛm So no .
Bulawayo Metropolitan Province MPANYIN (Amanaman Nkabom), Dorcas Sibanda , ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ nnuruyɛfo no akɔ so abɔ wɔn ho ban kakra , na ɛde ka ho sɛ ɛyɛ awerɛhow sɛ aban no de nnipa pii nkwa too asiane mu .
Aban dɔktafo a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ aban ayaresabea akɛse mu no yɛ nnuruyɛfo a wɔde mfe pii ayɛ adwuma sɛ wɔn a wɔhwɛ ayarefo , anaa nnuruyɛfo .

Ɔkae sɛ wɔyaree Kwasida , bere a na wɔrefi nsra bi mu wɔ Barbourfields Agumadibea no , na wosusuw sɛ wanya yare bi a ɛma obi fã dwudwo .
Akuw a wɔyɛ Ɔsorosoroni no de nkrasɛm bi too gua wɔ Twitter mu sɛ " owu no maa wɔn werɛ howee paa , na wɔkae sɛ wɔredi wɔn abusuafo ne afoforo a wɔwɔ agumadi ho asɛmpa no .

Owura Mapfumo kae sɛ ɔremmɔ sanku no bere a ɔrekasa atia Zimbabwefo no de reyi wiase nyinaa nniso , ne titiriw no Ɔmampanyin Mugabe , a ehia sɛ nneɛma sesa wɔ ɔman no mu
" MEYƐ odwontofo , nanso wɔ New York no , merento dwom mfa me ho mmɛka afoforo ho mmɛkasa ntia Zimbabwefo kɛtɛasehyɛ ne nhyɛso a Mugabe nniso a agye din no de ba no , na" Asase mfoninifumo ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 .
Ahyehyɛde ahorow te sɛ ÉTsFlag a Pastor Evan Mawarire, Tajamumuka, Ocupy Africa Unity Square ne NGOs ne amammuikuw afoforo a wɔka Zimbabweanfo a wofi nkurow akɛse mu di wɔn anim no hwɛ kwan sɛ wɔde wɔn ho bɛhyɛ atuatew no mu .
Afoforo hwɛɛ kwan sɛ nea ɛka ho ne Patson Dzamara , onipa hokwan ho aberante Itai Dzamara , a ɔyerae afe a etwaam no .
Amalgamated Rural Teachers Union of Zimbabwe (ARTUZ) no ka sɛ , kasa biara nni hɔ a ɛkyerɛ sɛ aban no ne akyerɛkyerɛfo retew akyerɛkyerɛfo a wɔn ani gye wɔn ho no so .
TUZ Obert Masaraure ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ n'ahyehyɛde no nni anigye bere a ohui sɛ sukuufo nni nhomasua ho anigye no , bere a akyerɛkyerɛfo no nni sika a wɔde bɛkɔ adwuma no .
Masaraure kae sɛ n'adwumakuw no mufo pii akyerɛw nkrataa a ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔrehwehwɛ nnwuma foforo bere a wɔn sala ahorow no nnɔɔso sɛ wɔbɛboa wɔn mmusua no .
Yɛantumi ne Ɔkyerɛkyerɛfo Paulo Mavhima Asomfo no anhyia , na yɛate n'asɛm no .
Sɛnea wiase agyiraehyɛde a wɔfrɛ no Breast Cancer Huness Month , Cancer Association of Zimbabwe no ka no , nnipa bi a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu a wɔnte wɔn ase no ho asɛm haw wɔn yiye .
Ahyehyɛde no bɔ amanneɛ sɛ nnipa pii a wɔkyerɛ sɛ kokoram ayɛ wɔn no di kan kɔ adwenemyare anaa adwenemhaw bi mu , na afei wɔma ɛyɛ den ma wɔn sɛ wɔbɛsa wɔn yare a emu yɛ den no .
Zimbabwe sohwɛfo Priscilla Mangwiro a ɔyɛ Cancer Association no kae sɛ ɛho hia sɛ nkurɔfo kɔ oduruyɛfo bi a ne ho akokwaw nkyɛn bere a wɔwɔ ɔhaw no .
Ms Mangwiro ka sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔma nkurɔfo hu kokoram , titiriw nufu mu kokoram .
Ms . Mangwiro ka sɛ nufu mu kokoram ne ade a ɛto so abien a ɛma mmea wu wɔ Zimbabwe .
Ms . Mangwiro ka sɛ efi October 1 no , efi bere a wɔyɛɛ ɔsatu a wɔde bɛhyɛ October ase sɛ Kokoram mu no , n'ahyehyɛde no asɔ mmea bɛboro 50 ahwɛ , na wɔn dodow bɛkɔ soro akosi ɔsram yi awiei .
Bere a ɔbea bi a wɔfrɛ no Gertrude Magwaniza tee Zimbabwe Cancer Association no , ɔkae sɛ ɔde ne babea no kɔtoo ne nufu mu .
Ms Mangwiro ka sɛ nneɛma pii wɔ hɔ a ɛma mmea nya nufu mu kokoram .
Ms Mangwiro ka sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔhwɛ mmea wɔ nsakrae a wɔayɛ wɔ wɔn nufu mu ho , na sɛ wɔyɛ saa a , ɛsɛ sɛ wohu wɔn ntɛm ara .
Ms Mangwiro ka sɛ nnipa pii susuw sɛ kokoram a wohu no kyerɛ sɛ wɔrewuwu , nanso pii wɔ hɔ a wobetumi ayɛ de aboa mmea ma wɔatra ase akyɛ .
Ms . Mangwiro ka nneɛma titiriw a ɛde kokoram ba no biako ho asɛm sɛ aduan a srade ne asikre pii wom .
Ms . Mangwiro rehyɛ mmea nkuran sɛ wɔmfa hokwan a October wɔ sɛ wɔbɛsɔ wɔn ahwɛ wɔ kokoram ho no nni dwuma , na wɔmfa nnuru no ntete wɔn nso .

Afifide ho dwumayɛni bi a wagye din a wɔfrɛ no Petertrade ka sɛ , sɛ aban no kɔ so sɛe sika a wɔde tɔ kar na wɔtɔ no a , fango ho haw no rentwam .
Bere a kan Petrotrade a ɔyɛ Onyankopɔnfrey Ncube mu panyin no rebua nhyehyɛe bi a ɛfa pɛtro ho no , ɔkae sɛ sɛ wɔma aguadifo nya hokwan de wɔn ankasa sika totɔ pɛ a , wobetumi ayɛ eyi .
Owura Ncube gye toom sɛ saa a ɔbɛyɛ no bɛma ne bo so atew , nanso ɔkae sɛ ɛno nkutoo ne ɔkwan biako pɛ a ɔbɛfa so afi fango ho nsɛnnennen ase wɔ ɔman no mu .
Owura Ncube kae sɛ , sɛ aban no nya fango a , ne bo nkyɛ fuw ntɛmntɛm wɔ ɔman no mu bere a wonya fango pii no .
Owura Ncube daa no adi sɛ ogya a aban no de boaa nhwɛso a ɔyɛe no adi , na ɔkae sɛ wɔ asram asia a edi kan no mu no , wɔtɔn lita ɔpepem 50 , nanso wɔ afe koro no ara mu no , wɔtɔn liter ɔpepem 36 pɛ .
Bere a wobisabisaa Gloria Magombo nsɛm bere a n'adwumam panyin no hwɛɛ kwan sɛ obetumi de nnyina ho nsɛnnennen ama no no , ɔkae sɛ , sɛ aman foforo no annya kwan ankɔ hɔ a , ɔhaw no befi hɔ .
Ɔkae nso sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔka asɛm no kyerɛ ɔman mũ no nyinaa , na ɛnyɛ n'adwumayɛbea nko .
Bere a John Mangudya a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ sikakorabea a ɛwɔ mfinimfini fam no amrado no kaa Smart Card ho asɛm no , obisae sɛ ebia adwene no ne sɛ , bere a ɔkae sɛ krataa no bɛkyerɛ pɛtro dodow a ɛwɔ kar biara a wɔde tɔ pɛtro a ɛwɔ Ms Magombo mu no , ɔkae sɛ A COD no ama wɔayɛ nhyehyɛe no foforo wɔ China .
Ms Magombo kae sɛ ontumi nka bere a nhyehyɛe no bɛyɛ yiye no , ɛwom sɛ Owura Mangudya ka kyerɛɛ boayikuw no sɛ ebedu June awiei no , na ɔhwɛ kwan sɛ wɔde kratasin no bedi dwuma ma ayɛ yiye de .
Eyi ahyɛ mmarahyɛ bagua boayikuw bi a ɛka sɛ ogya adwuma no rentumi nyɛ n'adwuma no abufuw bere a Ms Magombo kae nso sɛ wate afi boayikuw no mufo a wɔwɔ hɔ nnɛ a wɔn dodow no ara yɛ adwuma wɔ ɔman no mu sɛ wɔretɔn US dɔla anaa ɔman foforo so sika no .
Boayikuw no kae sɛ " nea ɛhaw adwene yiye " ne sɛ , fango ho nneɛma pii a ɛrekɔ so wɔ ɔman no mu no rehaw adwene .

Sɛnea abibifo te no maa nnipa pii nyaa anidaso sɛ awiei koraa no , wɔn mu pii benya abodin fitaa , na na wɔn mu pii afow wɔn agu bun no mu bere a wɔfaa wɔn asase pa no nyinaa no .
Nanso , mfe 40 a ɔman no nyaa ahofadi akyi no , wɔn mu binom aka sɛ nneɛma asɛe koraa esiane sɛ wɔde wɔn toto aborɔfo ho nti , bere a wonni adwuma a wɔde bɛhwɛ wɔn mmusua no .
Wɔka sɛ sikasɛm tebea no nye araa ma ɛyɛ den sɛ yebehu nea ɛbɛba daakye .
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ akwahosan ho nsɛm haw adwene bere nyinaa wɔ ayaresabea pii a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu no mu sɛnea wɔhwɛ kwan no .
Wɔn mu kakraa bi a wɔda so ara yɛ adwuma ka sɛ wɔtaa de di dwuma wɔ mmɔnten so kasa tia sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobenya asetrade .

Nanso wɔn mu dodow no ara redi abayifo ne abayifo , nanso bere a wɔka sɛ nneɛma resɛe no , wɔn ho retɔ wɔn .

Owura Charumbira kae sɛ afei de na n'adidikuw no awie n'adwuma a na wanya mfuw pii sen afoforo no , na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔn a wonnya nnya nnya nnyaa asase , a Zimbabweanfo a wɔte amannɔne ka ho no nya .

Wɔka nsɛm a asɛe mfe pii wɔ sikasɛm mu , akwahosan ne adwuma mu asiane mu , na ɛma adwumayɛfo pii a wɔwɔ mmɔnten so nya adwuma yɛ .

Bere a Zimbabwe Aduruyɛ Fekuw , Sacrifice Chirisa kyerɛwfo no rekasa akyerɛ nsɛnkyerɛwfo wɔ Harare , no , ɔkae sɛ onyaa krataa bi fii nnuruyɛfo mpanyimfo hɔ anaa oduruyɛfo bi a ɔhwɛ wɔn hɔ , na ɔhyɛɛ wɔn nkuran sɛ , sɛ aban no ammɔ nnuruyɛfo a wɔboro wɔn no amanneɛ a , wɔn nsa nka .
Chirisa , a ɔno nso bɛyɛɛ oduruyɛfo panyin no kae sɛ , adwuma no ama nnuruyɛfo a wɔn ho akokwaw no dodow anya nkɔanim wɔ ɔsram biako mu .
Chirisa kae sɛ nea ɛbɛyɛ na wɔatumi ayɛ wɔn adwuma yiye no , wohia nnuruyɛfo nkumaa ma wɔne wɔn ayɛ adwuma .
Owura Chirisa kae sɛ adɔkotafo nkumaa ne nnuruyɛfo 533 a wɔde wɔn ho hyɛɛ Akwahosan Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Akwahosan Ho Nsɛm So no na ɛmaa ayarefo a wɔwɔ ayaresabea
Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Dɔktafo Fekuw no kyerɛwfo panyin , Mthabisi Anele Bhebhe , nso kae sɛ n'ani nnye nsɛm a kan no na ɔyɛ ɔmampanyin Constantino Chiwenga a na nnuruyɛfo da so ara kɔ sukuu no ho .
Chiwenga , a aban no ne nnuruyɛfo a wɔkorɔn no paw no sɛ ɔmmɛhwɛ ayarehwɛfo no bere a ɔbɔɔ wɔn no .
Nnipa pii a wɔka sɛ Owura Chiwenga de asraadi ho nsɛm a ehia sɛ wodi ho dwuma no akasa atia wɔn nneyɛe no .
Adɔkotafo ka sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ aban no ma wɔn nnuru , nnuru ne ntade a wɔbɔ ho ban bere a wɔreyɛ wɔn adwuma , ne sala ahorow a wɔka sɛ ɛyɛ po so tow ahorow no .
Nanso , aban no san ka sɛ wɔn a wodi wɔn ho dɔm no ahwe ase araa ma ɛrentumi mma wɔn ho nkyere wɔn .
Bere a Owura Obadiah Moyo kɔɔ nhyiam bi a na ɔhwɛ ayarefo a wɔwɔ hɔ saa bere no , ntɛm ara na ɔne no kɔɔ nhyiam bi .
Labor Asennibea no apow aban mpanyimfo no abisade no bere a aban no mfaa nkrataa biara a ennii dwuma ntiaa nnuruyɛfo a wɔrenkɔ adwuma no .
Doug Coltart, mmaranimfo bi a ɔyɛ Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Fekuw a Ɛhwɛ Ayaresa Ho Nsɛm So no kae sɛ asɛnnibea no kae sɛ krataa biara nni hɔ a ɛdɔɔso a efi Health Services Board, HSB , hɔ , ma enti wontumi nte asɛm no ase wɔ mmara kwan so .
Asennibea no ka kyerɛɛ HSB mmaranimfo no sɛ ɔnkyerɛw nkrataa a wɔayera no ɔkyena , Wukuda .
Nanso nnuruyɛfo aka nso sɛ ɛnyɛ asɛnnibea a wɔbɛkɔ no ne ade titiriw a ɛbɛma wɔatumi akɔ adwuma , enti entumi nni ɔhaw no ho dwuma .
Bere bi a atwam a na Doctor Masimba Ndoro a ɔyɛ Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Ntam Dɔkta Fekuw no muni panyin no kae sɛ n'adwuma no hwehwɛ sɛ ɔda n'adwuma no ase da biara , na ɛsɛ sɛ otua no ka .
Dɔktafo no kɔɔ so kunkum wɔn September 3 , na wɔkae sɛ wonni sika pii a wɔde bɛyɛ adwuma .
Adɔkotafo a wofi Zimbabwe Ayaresabea a Ɛhwɛ Nnuruyɛfo Ayaresa Ho Nsɛm So no nso kɔɔ so boroo Yawda , na wonwiinwii wɔ sika a wotua ne ayaresa a ɛho nhia ho .
Nnuruyɛfo a wɔn mfe akɔ anim no kyerɛw krataa de nwiinwii wɔ asiane a na wɔreyɛ no ho , na wɔkae sɛ mfaso biara nni so sɛ nnuruyɛfo bɛkɔ ayaresabea a wɔmma ayarefo no kwan mma wɔmmɔ wɔn nkwa ho ban .
Dɔktafo no kasa tiaa aban no , na wɔkae sɛ sika no anya nkɔanim ɔha biara mu 60 , na wɔkae sɛ wɔne no nyɛ adwene .
Saa bere no ara mu no , nnuruyɛfo baanu a wɔn mfe akɔ anim de wɔn ho ahyɛ Zimbabwe Sukuupɔn no mu a wontuaa wɔn ka bere a wɔbɔɔ wɔn sobo sɛ wɔde wɔn ho rehyɛ ɔtopae no mu na wɔama afoforo anya wɔn so nkɛntɛnso no .

Zimbabwe Nnuruyɛfo Fekuw a Ɛhwɛ Hokwan a Nnipa Wɔ Ho Nsɛm So no akasa atia sɛnea Oduruyɛfo Mbuvayegano ne Oduruyɛfo Sɔre di no denneennen .
Yɛantumi ante asɛm amfi Zimbabwe Sukuupɔn no mu anaasɛ yɛate afi aban no hɔ wɔ akwahosan ho nsɛm ho .
Nanso asɛm bi a efi Health Minister Obadia Moyo hɔ no gye toom sɛ nnuruyɛfo no antie aban mpanyimfo no sɛ wɔnsan nkɔ adwuma .
Moyo kae sɛ na aban no retwɛn nea ebefi asennibea no mu aba , na ɛno akyi no , ɔkaa tebea no ho asɛm kyerɛɛ no .
Nnuruyɛfo kɔɔ so bɔɔ wɔn tuo September 3 , na wɔkae sɛ wonni sika pii a wɔde bɛkɔ adwuma .

Nanso bere bi a kan no na ɔyɛ sikani panyin wɔ aban a ɛwɔ Gifthimanikire no mu no , ɔkae sɛ onhu hia a ehia sɛ Zimbabwe kɔ amannɔne kɔtɔn , a mprempren enni sika pii wɔ ɔman no mu no .
Sikasɛm ho nimdefo , Nyasha Muchichwa , nso kae sɛ onhu hia a ehia sɛ Zimbabwe nya adwumakuw bi a wɔn ani gye ho wɔ Zimbabwefo gua so .
Owura Muchichwa kae nso sɛ ɛyɛ papa sɛ wo ne aman foforo bɛbɔ .

Shungudzemoyo Kache a ɔyɛ ɔpanyin no nso bedi n'asɛm wɔ ne fie .
Adiyifo Ayaresa ne Ogye a Wɔde Ma (FD) Adwenemyare , Walter Magaya , ti no ada ne ho adi wɔ ne tirimbɔ no ho , na ɛka sɛ ɔne aman foforo reyɛ adwuma de Aguma nnubɔne bi a ɔka sɛ ɛsa HIV / AIDS , kokoram , ne nea ɛkeka ho ama .
Bere a Owura Magaya reka Studio7 ho asɛm wɔ mpaebɔ adwuma bi a wɔyɛe wɔ Francistown, Botswana wɔ Wukuda anadwo mu ho asɛm no , ɔkae sɛ ɔnsan ntwe ne ho mfi ne nhyehyɛe a na wayɛ sɛ ɔbɛkyere no wɔ November 2018 mu bere a ɔkae sɛ wanya HIV / AIDS ano aduru no ho .
Bere a Owura Magaya too nsa frɛɛ no wɔ HIV / AIDS no , wɔbɔɔ no ka dɔla 700 wɔ February mu .
Nanso asɛm no ammɔ Owura Magaya, a ɔka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ wɔne aman foforo a wɔmpɛ sɛ wɔbɔ wɔn din na wɔkae sɛ wohu Aguma sɛ wɔanya HIV / AIDS yare no ano aduru no .
Owura Magaya kae sɛ HIV / AIDS yɛ ɔhaw wɔ Afrika , enti na ehia sɛ aman nyinaa bom yɛ adwuma na ama wɔatumi adi ɔhaw no ho dwuma .
Owura Magaya kae sɛ otumi ne aman foforo yɛ adwuma efisɛ na Zimbabwe nni ahotoso sɛ nnubɔne no bɛsa ɔman no mu nyarewa a edi awu no .
Nanso , wɔ Magaya a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe, Aretha Medical Company adwumakuw mu no , wohui sɛ wɔmpene Ayaresa So Ayaresa So Ayaresa no so , na wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ Akwahosan Asoɛe no amma kwan sɛ wɔnhwehwɛ mu nhwɛ sɛ Agumas Agus nom nnubɔne anaa .
Oduruyɛfo bi a ɔwɔ Francistown , Sengaphi Khuzwayo , kasa tiaa Magaya sɛ ɔrehwehwɛ sika .
Bere a wɔkyeree Owura Magaya too ɔbea foforo mmonnaa wɔ ɔman no mu , nanso akyiri yi , asɛnnibea bi de asɛm no too gua wɔ mmara kwan so .
Ayaresa ho abenfo a wonni aban ayaresabea ahorow no ama mmea a wonyinsɛn no nkwa da asiane mu bere a wɔwɔ ɔhaw te sɛ nea wɔwɔ Chinhoyi General Ayaresabea no .
Ms . Lisa Sibanda yɛ ɔbea a wanya awo akyi adwenemhaw .
Ms Sibanda ka kyerɛɛ ne ba no sɛ , bere a wɔde no kɔɔ Benada no , na ɔda so ara wu wɔ awotwaa mu , nanso oduruyɛfo biara antumi ammoa no , na ɔkae sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ ɔyarehwɛfo a ɔmaa abofra no wui no boa no .
Ms . Sibanda ka sɛ ɔhaw a emu yɛ den sen biara ne sɛ wɔbɛhohoro wɔn sẽ akyi sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ebetumi asɛe wɔn akwahosan .
Ms . Sibanda ka sɛ nsu ho ayɛ na , na nsu ntumi ntɔ wɔ ayaresabea hɔ bio .

Nanso , ogye toom sɛ ɛnyɛ ayarehwɛfo nkutoo ne wɔn a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔne mmea a wɔwɔ yafunum di , sɛnea ɛte wɔ Chinhoyi Ayaresabea no .

Junior Mavhu ka sɛ wɔayɛ nhyehyɛe a wɔde bɛhwɛ mmea ne mmarima nufu mu kokoram sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobetumi aboa wɔ bere ano .
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ Cancer rekunkum nnipa pii wɔ ɔman no mu , ɛnkanka mmea , ɛmfa ho sɛ mmarima dodow no ara na wɔwɔ hɔ no .
Beae foforo a Ɛwɔ Cancer Center ne mmea ne mmarima a wɔhyɛ wɔn nkuran sɛ wɔmfa hokwan no nni dwuma wɔ October mu mfa nhwehwɛ kokoram , ne afei bere a wodi yare no ho agoru wɔ baguam no .
Wiase no rehwɛ kwan ɔsram yi sɛ bere a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔkae nkurɔfo ma wohu nufu mu kokoram ne sɛnea wobetumi anya so mfaso .
Ms Mavhu's kamfo kyerɛ sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ obiara hwɛ yiye bere nyinaa sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobetumi asa ɔyare no na wɔahwɛ no ansa na atrɛw .
Zimbabwe dii mfe abien Memeneda fi bere a nnipa baasia kunkum nnipa baasia wɔ Harare bere a nnipa pii de wɔn ani kyerɛɛ mmɔnten so kyerɛɛ sɛnea wɔn ani nnye ho no .
Nnipakum no kɔɔ so wɔ wiase nyinaa sɛ nsɛnkyerɛwfo a wofi aman horow so , a na wɔwɔ Zimbabwe a na wɔhwɛ abatow a edi kan a ɛwɔ Zanu Porson Mnangagwa kannifo no , rehwɛ adwumakuw no dwumadi a basabasayɛ wom a na Robert Mugabe a na ɔyɛ ɔmampanyin panyin no de di dwuma no .
Ná Mnangagwa reko atia Nelson Chamisa of the MDC Alliance no , a na wɔn a wɔsɔre tia wɔn no mu bi ka ho .
Bere a aban no dii tuo no akyi no , wɔhyɛɛ no ma ɔyɛɛ adwuma bi a na ɛsɛ sɛ ɔyɛ mu nhwehwɛmu . Ná adwuma no wɔ South Africa kan South Africa ɔmampanyin Kgalema Motlanthe sɛ n'adwumam panyin .
Adwuma a woyii no adi no kyerɛe sɛ asraafo ne polisifo akum nnipa baasia no , na wɔka kyerɛɛ awudifo no sɛ wɔmfa wɔn nkɔ atemmu mu . Ɛsan kae sɛ aban no ntua wɔn a wokunkum wɔn no abusuafo ka .
Owura Motlanthes kae nso sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ aban no de nea wawu no mma kɔ sukuu , na ɛnsɛ sɛ polisifo ne asraafo no de mmara no hyɛ wɔn nsa bere a nkurɔfo kasa tia no .
Nnipa ho animdefo ka sɛ aban no nnya mfaa Motlanthe Asoɛe no mmae .
Nanso Monica Mutsvangwa a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ ɔman no mu no kae sɛ aban no nim Motlanthe Asoɛe no , na na wɔwɔ nhyehyɛe a ɛbɛma wɔatumi adi ahyɛde no ho dwuma .
Adwumayɛfo no mu biako a ɔde amanneɛbɔ no too gua , Lovemore Madhuku , a ɔno nso ne Ɔman Mmarahyɛ Bagua Bagua no guamtrani no kae sɛ n'adwuma no awie , na ɔde maa Mnangagwa aban no , na ɔhwɛ ma wɔyɛɛ adwuma no .
Madhuku nso kae sɛ n'asɛyɛde no ayɛ ahyɛde ama aban no sɛ ɔmfa wɔn a wɔn asɛm ato wɔn no abusuafo mma wɔn efisɛ na asraafo ne polisifo ato wɔn tuo .
Dewa Mavhinga a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ Afrika Atifi fam no ka sɛ , hokwan a nnipa wɔ ne hokwan ahorow a nnipa wɔ no mfa Motlanthe Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Hokwan a Nnipa Wɔ So no ho .
Mavhinga kae sɛ efi bere a woyii amanneɛbɔ no fii afiase mfe abien no , na wɔakyere ɔsraani biara a Motlanthe's kamfo kyerɛe sɛ ɔnkɔsra no .
Wɔatutu mmeae pii wɔ ɔmampanyin , Emmerson Mnangagwa , n'asɔfo , ne adwumakuw no mufo , akyi no , wɔde wɔn ho kɔbɔɔ amanfo ma wɔtew wɔn nnwuma ho na wodii dwuma wɔ National Clean - Campign no ase asram abiɛsa a atwam ni .
Mnangagwa kɔɔ Parirenyatwa Ayaresabea anɔpatutuutu ne n'asɔfo a wɔboa ma woyii ayaresabea tebea bɔne no fii hɔ .
Bere a Owura Mnangagwa a na wasiesie ne ho wɔ ayaresabea hɔ kasa wiei no , ɔkae sɛ wɔn nsa aka dwumadi no yiye , na ɛmaa nkurɔfo akwahosan tuu mpɔn .
Ɔkae sɛ ɔkwan a ɔfaa so kaee nkurɔfo sɛ saa na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ da biara .
Owura Mnangagwa kae nso sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ nkurɔfo yi nwura fi hɔ na wosua biribi fi aman te sɛ Rwanda a wɔmma nkurɔfo kwan mma wɔnkyere wɔn afie ne sare anaa mpapo bio no mu .
Agumadi so Asomfo , Kirsty Coventry , ne n'adwumayɛfo , a wofii ase de wɔn ani kyerɛɛ Simon Muzenda Street , na wɔde wɔn ani kyerɛɛ Afrika Biakoyɛ Square , baabi a wɔde Meikles Hotel ne TMpermarket pomarket poo wɔn no .
Wɔkae sɛ ɔmanfo no ho dwiriw wɔn sɛ wohuu wɔn wɔ mmɔnten so , na ɛsɛ sɛ nkurɔfo siesie wɔn mpɔtam hɔ bere nyinaa .
Zimbabwe Newspapers adwumakuw no afa bɔs adwumayɛbea ti no mmɔnten so , na adwumakuw no nso atɔ bi ama wɔn wɔ mmɔnten so .
Zimpapers kasamafo Beatrice Tonhodzayi ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ efĩ abu so araa ma enti wotumi hu sɛ ɛfata sɛ wɔne aban no siesie kurow no ne ɔman no .

Harare , Hebert Gomba , kurow no mu baguafo , ne council po so adwumayɛfo no nso sui , na wɔboaboaa nkura a ɛwɔ nkuraase a ɛwɔ Harare no ano .
Gomba ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 bere a ɔne OK Machipisa adwumayɛfo a wɔwɔ Machipipisa adwumakuw a ɛwɔ Highfields mu no bɔɔ nkɔmmɔ wiei no , ɔkae sɛ na n'ani agye sɛ afei wanka sɛ kurow no ho tew nnɛ .
Ɛwom sɛ na ehia sɛ wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ nkurow akɛse mu de , nanso na bagua no rebɔ mmɔden biara sɛ wɔbɛma kurow no ho atew .
Owura Mnangagwa de da a wodi no ɔsram biara Fida a edi kan no too gua sɛ ɔkwan a nkurɔfo bɛfa so ama wɔn mpɔtam hɔ atew na ayɛ akwahosan pa .
Finance Asoɛe no aka sɛ ɛbɛma nkurɔfo ani agye kɛse , na ɛde sika pii aba ɔman no mu sɛ ɔkwan a wɔbɛfa so adi ɔman no sikasɛm mu ahokyere ho dwuma .

Guvamatanga nso kae sɛ n'adwumayɛbea no nim sɛ ɔman no sikasɛm mu ayɛ den , na aban no bedi ɔhaw no ho dwuma .
Bere a wobisaa wɔn nea wɔbɛfa so adi sikasɛm ho haw ho dwuma no , Ɔman Soafo Panyin Clemence Chiduwa kae sɛ wobebisa wɔn a wɔtɔ nneɛma no sɛnea wonyaa sika no .
Sikasɛm ho nimdefo bi a ɔwɔ Labor ne Economic Development Research Institute of Zimbabwe, Nyasha Muchichwa mu no kae sɛ , sɛ aban no de sika fam nhyehyɛe a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu no di dwuma nkutoo a , gye sɛ aman foforo na wotumi di so .

Sikasɛm ho som adwuma no agye atom nso sɛ anigye a wobenya ama akwahosan ho kuw no yɛ nea wontumi mfa ntoto akwahosan ho nsɛnnennen a ɛwɔ hɔ mprempren no ho , nanso wɔaka sɛ ɛbɛkɔ so ayɛ yiye .
Ɔman Soafo Panyin , Mculi Ncube nso ka kyerɛɛ nsɛnkyerɛwfo sɛ n'ani gyee akwan a ɔfaa so maa ɔman no sikasɛm yɛɛ yiye ne nkɔso no ho .
Nanso bere a ɔman no sikasɛm mu ahokyere no mu reyɛ den no , ka sɛ , sika sɔfo Tendai Biti , a kan no na ɔyɛ MDC akannifo baasa no mu biako no , ɛka a wɔbɔ wɔ ɔman no mu no sɛe koraa bere a ɔman no sikasɛm ho hia no , na Reserve Bank of Zimbabwe no reyɛ nea ɛsen nea ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ no , na ama ɔman no anya sika pii . . .
Owura Biti, a ɔyɛɛ sikasɛm ho nhyehyɛe ho nhyehyɛe no guamtrani no kae sɛ , ɛsɛ sɛ adwumakuw no yɛ wɔn ade ma ɛne mmara no hyia , na wɔ ɔkwan bi so no , ɔman no sikasɛm nhyehyɛe no nyera , sɛnea aban mpanyimfo bi yɛe no .
Nanso , ɛsɛ sɛ sikasɛm ho som adwuma no ka sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ ɔmanfo hu sɛ mfe pii ni a ɔman no de wɔn sika bɛhyɛ ɔman no mu no , saa ara na sɛ wodi ɔhaw no ho dwuma a , ebegye bere .

Holden bisabisaa Advocate Matthew Chaskalson ho nsɛm .
Holden ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ n'adansedi no gyina amanneɛbɔ ne sɛnea na wotua sika ma Gupta nnwumakuw no so .
Ɔkae sɛ Guptas no de R287 a wofi Estina Dairy Farmct no ɔpepem biako na ɛyɛɛ saa .
Ná nhyehyɛe no ne sɛ wɔbɛyɛ akuafo wɔ Ɔman a Wɔade Wɔn Ho no mu .
Holden kae sɛ Guptas no fii ase tɔn sika afe biara ansa na Estina dwumadi no refi ase .
Ɔman a Ahofadi Wom no fii ase gyee Estina nhyehyɛe no toom wɔ June 2011 mu , nanso Guptas fii ase de sika hyɛɛ dwumadi no mu wɔ May 2011 mu .
Holden kae sɛ: " Amanaman no de Estina nhyehyɛe no yɛɛ adwuma de sika siee , ansa na dwumadi no refi ase no , na wɔfrɛ no Holden .
Sɛnea amanneɛbɔ no kyerɛ no , aban no tuaa R287 maa Gupta abusua no , na wɔde sika no hyehyɛɛ adwumayɛkuw ahorow mu ma ɛyɛɛ te sɛ nea mfaso wɔ R880 kosi 2016 ntam .
Adwuma no kɔ so .

Ɛte sɛ nea ɔkɔɔ asɔrefie a ɛbɛn wɔn fie no mu .
Oyii ne mpaboa fii asɔrefie hɔ na ɔpaa mmarima baanu no kyɛw .
Wɔka sɛ , bɛyɛ anibu 40 akyi no , wohui sɛ Ayeforokunu no refi fie hɔ akɔpa awarefo no kyɛw .
Saa bere no ara na ɔbea bi yii ne ho adi frɛɛ no 911, na ɔbɔɔ korɔnbɔ ho amanneɛ .
Ɔbea no ka kyerɛɛ polisini no sɛ ne kunu da wɔn fie mu .
Sɛnea afiewuranom kyerɛ no , wɔannya hwee mfi wɔn fie .

Wɔ nsɛm bi a Bickerton ne Owura William Denselow bisabisaa no mu no , ɔdaa no adi sɛ bere a Ayeforokunu no fii fie no , ne bo amfuw .
