Wɔ video a edi kan no mu no , ɛte sɛ nea polisifo a woyii wɔn adi kyerɛɛ Ayeforokunu a ɔsrɛɛ wɔn sɛ wonkum no bere a owui wɔ ayaresabea no .
Ɔkae sɛ wonnim Myenini no , na polisini no wɔ video no bi , nanso wɔfrɛɛ no atesɛm krataa bi sɛ wɔntow nhyɛ wɔn so sɛnea ɛnsɛ .
Bickerton kae sɛ wɔbɛkɔ so ahwehwɛ nokware no sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobehu nea ɛrekɔ so .
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ IFP pae gui wɔ Melmoth
Wɔbɔɔ INTuncilors a na ɔhwɛ wɔn a wɔbɔ wɔn ho ban a wɔbɔɔ wɔn tuo piraa ɔmanfo no mu baasa wɔ nhyiam bi ase wɔ Thubalethu , Mthonjaneni (Melmoth), Kwasida awia .
Wɔka sɛ awɛnfo a Mayorfo no de wɔn ani kyerɛɛ nnipadɔm a na wɔka bha·tararch a ɛwɔ nhyiam asa no ano no .
Ɔman no fã bi de asodi too gua sɛ kuw no di anim esiane sɛ wɔbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔde wɔn kotodwe bɛkɔ wɔn kotodwe mu bere a wɔhyɛɛ IFP - pipilor a ɔwɔ hɔ no san bae no nti .
IFP kannifo a ɔwɔ King Cetshwayo mantam mu no frɛɛ nhyiam no sɛ ɔnkyerɛ ɔsɛmpɔw a apaapae ɔmanfo no mu no ase , bere a nnawɔtwe a etwaam no , ɔkasa tiaa baguafo a wɔpam wɔn , a nea na kan no wɔfrɛ no Bonginkosi Bila ka ho no .
Baguam no muni bi a na ɔyɛ ɔtopae no ho ɔkasatiafo a na ɔmpɛ sɛ wɔbɔ no din no , bɔɔ IFP akannifo ne baguafo a na wɔwɔ hɔ no sobo denam awɛmfo a na wɔbɔ wɔn ho ban sɛ wɔbɛtow wɔn tuo no so sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wontumi nni wɔn abufuw no so .
" Esiane sɛ wɔamma yɛn kwan amma yɛankɔ asa no so esiane sɛ na nnipa a wofi mmeae foforo ayɛ wɔn ma nti , na wɔkasa tia yɛn .
Ɔhaw no fii ase bere a yekum ɔmanfo a na wɔrebɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛhyɛ no ma wafa ɔkwan bi a emu yɛ den so , ne awɛmfo ne aban mpanyimfo a na wɔwɔ hɔ sɛ wobetumi atow tuo no " no muni foforo no .
NÁ IFP kannifo a ɔwɔ Mthonjaneni , a ɔmpɛ sɛ wɔbɔ no din no , ka sɛ ɔmanfo a wɔwɔ mpɔtam hɔ no mu apaapae .
" Wɔ dapɛn a etwaam no mu no , na wɔkasa tia wɔn baguafo no .
Wɔayɛ nhyiam bi ho nhyehyɛe ama baguafo ne IFP ɔmantam no mu akannifo nyinaa ma wɔadi wɔn ho dɔm wɔ baguam .
" Ɔhaw no fii ase bere a ɔmanfo no bi sɔre gyinagyinaa asa no akyi , na bere a nhyiam no fii ase no , wosiw abotan a ɛwɔ asa no ano , na wɔbɔɔ wɔn ho ban hyɛɛ wɔn ma wɔbɔɔ wɔn tuo esiane sɛ na ɔmanfo no retow ahyɛ wɔn so nti .
Abanfo no bi de tuo guu wɔn so . "
Mbangiseni Biyela , ne panyin Phumlani Ntombela ne Mthonjaneni Municipality , baa nhyiam no bi .
Mmɔden a wɔbɔe sɛ wɔbɛma mmuae afi ɔmantam no kannifo hɔ no yɛ nea ɛho nhia bere a na wontumi mfa nsɛm ne nkrasɛm mma wɔn no .
Thami Shangase a ɔyɛ kasamafo no kae sɛ ɛnyɛ kurow no mu akunini no na wɔyɛɛ nhyiam no ho nhyehyɛe , na ɔde kaa ho sɛ asɛm no wɔ polisifo nsam .
IFP a ofi ɔman no kasamafo Mkhuleko Hlengwa kae sɛ apontow no bɛyɛ ɔsɛmpɔw bi a ɛfa asɛm no ho nnɛ .
Biyela (a ɔyɛkyerɛfo) ne baguafo baanan na wofii ase de mpaapaemu baa ɔmanfo no mu , ne titiriw no , IFP kuw no mufo a wodii wɔn ho fɛw no .

Mbete ka sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ wobu ani gu ɔporɔw so
ABAKƆSƐM ho ɔbenfo Baleka Mbethe akasa atia dwowtwa , na ɔkae sɛ emu bi fa akyinnyegye ho .
Ms Mbete buaa nsemmisa bi a nnipa kakraa bi na wobisabisaa wɔn nsɛm , a nea ɛkyerɛ ne sɛ na Mmarahyɛ Bagua no mufo bi de wɔn ho hyɛ ɔporɔw mu no kae wɔ nsɛm bi mu sɛ wontumi nni wɔn ho so , bere a na ɛte sɛ nea afoforo ho yɛ hu esiane sɛ na wonni adanse biara nti .
Ɔtwee adwene mpo sii akode a kan no na ɔyɛ ɔmampanyin Yakob Zuma yɛe no so sɛ nhwɛso a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ne nsa kaa krataa bi a wɔkyerɛw faa nsɛm a emu yɛ den ho nanso na onnim nea efi mu bae no .
" Minim sɛ nnipa bi wɔ hɔ a wɔadi adanse wɔ ha , na ɔkwan a wɔfa so yɛ ade no tu mmirika .
Minim nso sɛ ɔkasafo no aba ha , na ɔkae sɛ wubetumi aka nea wote no ho asɛm akyerɛ wo .
" Yebetumi aka akode no ho asɛm , asɛm a wɔde too gua nnɛra (Monday) no .
Krataa bi wɔ m'adwumam .
Ná nsɛm a ɛyɛ ahodwiriw na ɛyɛ ahodwiriw wɔ krataa no mu , nanso wɔamfa wɔn nsa anhyɛ ase , na na obiara nkyerɛw .
Mmarahyɛ bagua no nni adagyew koraa , enti na mintumi mfa nhoma yi , a minnim nea ɔkyerɛw na yɛka ho asɛm no .
Ɔhaw no ne nea ɔkyerɛw no , na ɛsɛ sɛ onii no ba me nkyɛn na ɔte me ase .
Mɛbɔ mmɔden sɛ mebua seesei a yɛrentumi nka ahonhonsɛm no ho asɛm wɔ Parliament no
Wɔ June 2017 mu no , wobisaa no nea ɔreyɛ wɔ Gupta abusua no mu .
" MEMMOƆFO no kae no yiye , nanso minim sɛ asɛntitiriw a ɛwom no ka Guptas no ho asɛm .
Misusuw sɛ bere a saa nsɛm no bae no , anka wɔbɛfrɛɛ wɔn a wɔkyerɛwee no .
Ma yɛnhwɛ nea wɔka fa wiase a atwa wo ho ahyia no ho .
Sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a yebetumi anya nkyerɛkyerɛmu na yɛatumi ayɛ yɛn adwuma no , " Msaid Mbethe .
Wɔbɔɔ NSFAS sobo wɔ sukuuni bi wu ho
NSRAFO de NSFAS retoto sukuuni bi a owui bere a na wada nnanu wɔ ɔman no akyi , Durban Tvet College , wɔ Cato Manor , Memeneda no wu ho .
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ nea wawu no , Yonbo Manyanya (26), Electric Infrastruction a Electrical Infrastruction (26), no , n'asomfo a na wɔwɔ Yonbo no faa wɔn nnommum .
Wɔhyɛɛ nea wawu no ma ɔkɔdaa abɔnten nnanu , efisɛ na onni baabi foforo biara a ɔde ne ho bɛhyɛ ne dan mu wɔ Dwoda .
Wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ wɔ Wednesday ho sɛ na nea wawu no nni akwahosan pa .
Wɔbɔ amanneɛ sɛ ne mfɛfo sukuufo no ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ ohu baabi a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔde sie .
Wɔbɔ amanneɛ sɛ Yowabo, a wɔkyerɛ sɛ na ɔte mpɔtam hɔ no wui Memeneda wɔ ɔdan a n'adamfo te Durban North no mu .
Sukuufo no mu biako , a na wabɛn nea wawu no , kae sɛ nea asi no maa wɔn ho dwiriw wɔn , na ɔbɔɔ NSFAS sobo sɛ ɔtwe wɔn nan ase de gyigye wɔn ani .
" Yenni tebea pa mu bere a asɛm no sii no .
Mepɛ sɛ NSFAS de ne ho gye nsɛm mu efisɛ ɛte sɛ nea asiane pii wɔ hɔ a ebesi wɔ awɔw bere mu wɔ " osuani no nsam .
Abusua no muni bi a na ontumi nka nea wawu no ho asɛm nkyerɛ wɔn no kae sɛ wontumi nka ho asɛm nkyerɛ nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfo .
KwaZulu - Nasi polisifo kasamafo Captain Nqobile Gwala kae sɛ wɔammɔ ho amanneɛ biara .

Oduruyɛfo foforo a wɔfrɛ no Tawanda Manjonjonjonjon , a ɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔne Oduruyɛfo Magombeyi na ɛyɛ adwuma no kae sɛ afei na nnuruyɛfo pii suro sɛ ne nkwa da asiane mu , nanso ɔde kaa ho sɛ Doctor Magombeyi nni hɔ a , gye sɛ wɔsan kɔ adwuma ansa .
Mpilo Hospital kwankyerɛfo , Leonard Mabandi , kae sɛ , wɔ bere tiaa bi akyi no , na nnuruyɛfo ahyɛ bɔ sɛ ɔbɛsan akɔ adwuma .
Ɔbarima bi a ɔdaa ne ho adi sɛ Walter , a ɔkyerɛ sɛ ne yere na ɔsaa no yare no ka sɛ nnuruyɛfo pii nhu wɔn .

" Yɛahu sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ yedi wɔn a wogyina ɔman no ananmu na wowuwu te sɛ Muhammad Ali ni bere a yehuu saa okunkɛse yi no . Kurow no mufo ne kuromfo a wɔabedi Ali ho awerɛhow da foforo a yehuu ne adaka a ofi wimhyɛn gyinabea hɔ no . Ɛkaa me koma ma mihui sɛ wɔbɛyɛ eyi wɔ yɛn fie bere a Sletefo a wɔn ho yɛ fɛ no .
Zimbabwe Asɔre Ahorow Bagua (ZCC) no ka sɛ Matabelland South, Matabeleland Atifi fam ne Bulawayo mantam ahorow no werɛ ahow kɛse bere a wɔde ntade a ɛmfata maa ayarehwɛfo a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ ayaresabea wɔ ɔmantam no mu no .
ZCC no ahyɛ ntade a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde ma ayarehwɛfo , nnuruyɛfo ne adwumayɛfo foforo wɔ asɔre ayaresabea ahorow abiɛsa mu .
SC kyerɛwfo panyin , Pastor Doctor Kenneth Mta ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ wohuu nnipa pii a ɔkɔm de wɔn , na ɛhaw wɔn a wɔyɛ kuw no mufo no .

Nanso wɔ ɔsram a etwaam no mu no , na nnipa a wɔwɔ nkuraase no mu ɔha mu 1 pɛ na wohia aduan .
Nneɛma a enye koraa ne Matabeleland North, Masvingo ne Midlands .
Ahyehyɛde bi a ɛyɛ adwuma a sika wom a ɛde aduan ba no mu kakraa bi na ɛka sɛ nnipa a wɔte nkurow akɛse mu no hia mmoa afe yi , bere a ɔman no sikasɛm sɛe no .

Nanso , Nyasha Mahwende a ɔte hɔ no kae sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wobu nkurɔfo no animtiaa sɛnea Zimbabweanfo ne afoforo nnamfo yɛ no .
Wɔkae nso sɛ yare no a wɔbɛtrɛw mu akyi no , na ɛhaw wɔn nso sɛ saa nnipa yi bi betumi ayɛ nneɛma a mmara mma ho kwan na wɔasi hia a ahobammɔ a emu yɛ den ho hia so dua .
Studio 7 biara nni hɔ a aban mpanyimfo betumi akɔ mmeae abien a ahobammɔ wɔ no , na wɔka sɛ wohia hokwan afi Midland aban adwumayɛbea hɔ .
Yɛate fi Midlands Minister Larry Mavima ne kan ayaresabea dwumayɛni Oduruyɛfo Reginald Mhene hɔ , nanso bere a yeduu n'adwumam no , wɔkyerɛ sɛ na ɔwɔ nhyiam bi ase .
Abenfo ka sɛ wɔ Botswana ne South Africa no , na wɔka wɔn a wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔyɛ atubrafo a wonni mmara so a wɔkyeree wɔn no ho , na na
Gweru Mayor Yosia Makombe sii so dua kyerɛɛ VOA's Studio 7 wɔ Zimbabwe sɛ wɔda so ara resi amantam Ayaresabea no .
Ɔhyɛɛ wɔn a wɔte hɔ no nkuran sɛ wonnyina akwankyerɛ a wɔde ma de siw mogya mu nyarewa ano no so , nanso ɔkae sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ wosuro , na wɔkae sɛ wɔwɔ ahotoso sɛ wobetumi asa wɔn a ɔyare no bi ayɛ wɔn no yare .
Nnipa a wɔwɔ Democratic Party kannifo Lucia Matibenga , a ɔno nso yɛ Gweru no kae sɛ ɛyɛ aban no asɛyɛde sɛ ɔhwɛ ma wɔn a wɔaba hɔ foforo no nya ahobammɔ .
Nnipa a wɔwɔ Midland no nnyaa bi mmaa obiara a ɔyare no bi wɔ hɔ . Nanso Zimbabwefo a wofi aman a ɛbemmɛn hɔ mu no kɔ so ma ebinom de wɔn ti bɔ yare no ho hu .
Efi bere a dɔktafo no fii ase kunkum wɔn afe a etwaam no , ɔmampanyin a ɔwɔ Wednesday no ne nnuruyɛfo yɛɛ nhyiam a edi kan .
Nnuruyɛfo ne abenfo anaa Registrars ne Consultantfo bi nso akɔ so akunkum wɔn Wukuda . Ɔman no mu nnipa pii ka sɛ esiane sɛ nnuruyɛfo no bɔ wɔn nkwa nti , wɔn nkwa resa .
Ɔmampanyin , Emmerson Mnangagwa , fi Benada , kɔkaa n'adiyifo no ho , Ɔsahene Constantin Chiwenga , na ɔbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ obedi oduruyɛfo no ho dwuma .
Spokesman Nick Mangwana kae sɛ ogye di sɛ Mnangagwa asan akɔyɛ adwuma de aboa ma wɔayi nwanwa no afi hɔ .
Wɔ Benada no , na Owura Chiwenga aka akyerɛ nnuruyɛfo sɛ wɔnsan nkɔ adwuma .
Adɔkotafo a wɔwɔ Zimbabwe Aduruyɛ Fekuw no ase de nnɔnhwerew 48 ama aban no sɛ wɔmfa nni dwuma wɔ nnuruyɛfo ho , na wonkum wɔn .
Nanso Mnangagwa's office ne Zimbabwe Ayaresa Fekuw no akannifo yɛɛ nhyiam bi , Oduruyɛfo Elias Muzoremba , tiee nnuruyɛfo no .
Wɔ krataa bi a dɔktafo de kɔmaa wɔn mu no , nnuruyɛfo no ka kyerɛɛ titrani no sɛ Akwahosan Asoɛe no na ɛredaadaa wɔn .
Dɔktafo no ka sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ aban no ka nnuru a wɔde di dwuma wɔ ayaresabea ne mmeae foforo ho asɛm , na wɔde US dɔla US ka ho ma RTGS .
Mprempren , saa nnuruyɛfo yi renya $ 329 ɔsram biara . Nanso saa sika yi fi RTGS .
Nanso sikasɛm ho ɔbenfo bi a ɔwɔ Nelson Mandela Metropolitan Sukuupɔn mu ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ aban no ntumi ntua sika no koraa .
Afei nso yebisaa Dɔkta Mugano sɛnea seesei nnwumakuw bi de US dɔla ma wɔn aguade no , sɛnea wobetumi ayɛ no yiye
Studio 7 no panyin ka kyerɛɛ Studio sɛ ɛho hia sɛ aban no ma akwahosan ho kuw no sika pii wɔ sikasɛm mu .
Nnipa pii a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu nso renwiinwii sɛ ɛnyɛ adwuma ne bere a wɔka kyerɛ wɔn sɛ wɔmfa US dɔla US dɔla US no nkɔ fie no .
Amanaman ntam aguadi kuw no akɔ South Africa ama Cosafa nsrahwɛ no .
Kuw no mufo hyia ako abien wɔ Cosafa Cup ne Africa Cup of Nations , a ɛsɛ sɛ wodi ho dwuma ntɛm ara wɔ Cosafa Cup a ɛwɔ Memeneda no mu .
Nea ɛka Cosafa Cup ho sɛ ahosiesie a wɔbɛyɛ ama Afcon, Zimbabwe ho no , ɛsɛ sɛ wokoyi trophy no ano bio wɔ afe a ɛto so asia a etwa to no mu , na wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ ɛbɛhyɛ ne din no mu den sɛ Afrika Atifi fam bɔɔlbɔ fekuw bio wɔ afe yi mu .
Due a ɛde sikasɛm mu ahokyere ba no , Zimbabwe ntumi nhuu akuw a wodi agoru wɔ Afcon ne Warriors coach Sunday Chidzambwa ka sɛ Cosafa nkutoo ne ɔkwan koro pɛ a wɔfa so hyɛ n'asen mu den .
Afei nso , Chidzambwa rehwehwɛ din kɛse wɔ Cosafament no mu bere a ɔbɛyɛɛ coach a edi kan a obedii abodoo no mpɛn anan fi bere a wɔhyɛɛ nsrahwɛ no ase wɔ 1997 mu no .
Chidzambwa nyaa Cosafa Cup wɔ afe 2003, 2009, 2017, ne 2018 mu .
Zimbabwefo agodifo afoforo te sɛ Tendai Darikwa, Admiral Muskwe , ne Alec Mudimu nso pɛ sɛ wohu wɔn wɔ Cosafa Cup a wonnim wɔn ho hwee no mu .
Afe yi , Zimbabwe wɔ kuw a emu yɛ den sen biara wɔ nsrahwɛ no nyinaa mu , bere a ɛrebɔ kuw a wɔde wɔn ani kyerɛ Afcon a agodifo afoforo te sɛ Nimdeɛ Musona , ne Marvelous Nakamba ka ho no .
Zimbabwe Warriors Fan Club , Shingirai Miti , no muni bi ka sɛ akansi biara nni Cosafa ho efisɛ bere nyinaa na trophy no wɔ Zimbabwean .
Bere a Apuei ne Atɔe Ntam Ntawntawdi no rekɔ so no , na Warrifo no rehwɛ kwan sɛ wɔn a wodii kan duu Afcon nsrahwɛbea a wohyiaa Misraim wɔ bere a edi kan a na wɔbɛn wɔn no mu nea edi kan .
Ronald Pfumbidzai , ka sɛ wɔnkɔ Egypt nkodi akuw a ɛwɔ hɔ no bi .
Zimbabwe wɔ Group A With Egypt , Democratic Republic of Congo ne Uganda , baabi a Warriors Wellington Mpandare ho dwumayɛni no wɔ ahotoso sɛ obefi hɔ .
Zimbabwe refi South Africa , bere a Cosafament no rekɔ n'awiei wɔ June 8 , bere a ɔrekɔ Nigeria no .
Wɔ agumadifo pii fam no , Buronya bere yɛ bere a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔne wɔn abusuafo ne wɔn nnamfo bɔ , na afoforo nso de hokwan yi yɛ nneɛma foforo . Nanso afe yi , bere a ebinom rekɔsra wɔn abusuafo ne wɔn nnamfo ne FClatinum coach Lizwe akɔsra wɔn ho wɔn ho no , ɛnyɛ bere a wɔwɔ Carofly no .
Eyi bɛyɛ FC Platinum Nkyerɛwee a ɛto so abiɛsa a ɛne akansi no hyia , bere a Sudan's Al Hilal hwee wɔ ne nan a edi kan no mu no , ne hwere a ɔhweree nkyem 3 - 0 kɔɔ Tunisia's Etoile duSahel no .
Sweswe ka sɛ bere a edi hɔ a Spois behyia no , ɔne n'abusua bedi agoru wɔ agodibea bi a wɔfrɛ no Owifo a wodi agoru wɔ hɔ no mu .
Amalgamated Rural Teachers Union of Zimbabwe (ARTUZ) ka sɛ ennii aban no adanse sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ edi ne tebea no ho dwuma wɔ nnafua 14 mu , nanso ɛrentumi nyɛ yiye .
Biako no ka sɛ , ɛsɛ sɛ akyerɛkyerɛfo bɔ mmɔden sɛ wobenya dɔla US , anaasɛ wobetua wɔn ka bɛyɛ US dɔla ahanum .
Wɔde ARTZ amanneɛbɔ no too gua Fida wɔ aban no nsam wɔ ɔman adwuma no mu , Baguam Som Adwuma ne Hokwan a Ɔmanfo Wɔ no .
Studio7 ntumi ntee asɛm no mfii aban no afã , na saa ara nso na wɔntaa nhu Studio Mutswa wɔ telefon a wokura kyin so .
ARZZ Obert Masaraure , ka sɛ , sɛ́ agumadifo no , wɔpɛ asetra pa , nanso ɛrensi bere a wɔpɛ no .
Masaraure ka sɛ , ɛwom sɛ aban no ka sɛ sikasɛm ho haw de , nanso sɛ ɛko tia ɔporɔw wɔ ne nnubaa mu a , ebetumi ama nneɛma ayɛ yiye .
Masaraure ka sɛ wɔde sika a aban no de ma no mu fã kɛse no ara di dwuma wɔ amannɔne akwantu te sɛ amannɔne akwantu mu , kar akwanhyia ne nneɛma foforo a wobetumi ayi afi hɔ na ama ɔmanfo anya sika pii .
Masaraure ka wɔ n'adwene mu sɛ sika bi wɔ ɔman no mu a ebetumi de ɔhaw no aba , nanso ɔhaw no ne sɛ wɔmfa ɔman no hokwan no nni dwuma ɔkwampa so , na wonhu hia a ehia sɛ aban mpanyimfo de wɔn ho hyɛ mu no .
Amannɔne amanfo renwiinwii wɔ ka a wɔbɔ sɛ wobenya hyɛn gyinabea foforo anaasɛ wɔbɛyɛ nhyehyɛe foforo wɔ hɔ no ho .
Eyi di eyi akyi wɔ Dwoda dapɛn yi mu kɔbɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔama Atipɛnfo Panyin no Kyerɛwfo Panyin no kwan ma wafi Zimbabwefo ɔpepem 388 ase .
Bere a Kazembe Kazembe a ɔyɛ Interior soafo no rekasa akyerɛ amanneɛbɔfo no , ɔkae sɛ n'adwumam panyin no nim sɛnea nkurɔfo hwɛ kwan sɛ wɔn nsa bɛka wɔn hyɛn gyinabea bere tiaa bi , ne sɛ nkurɔfo a wɔrebɔ mmɔden sɛ wobenya saa nkrataa yi , ne titiriw no , wɔn a wofi amannɔne no atutu nkrataa no .
Kazembe kae sɛ nea ɛbɛyɛ na aman a wofi aman foforo so anya mmara kwan so nkrataa wɔ wɔn man mu no , aban no ahu sɛ ɛfata sɛ wɔma wɔn bo yɛ den , na wɔde saa nkrataa yi bɛma ntɛm ara .
Nanso ebinom a wɔatu wɔn ho ama no te nka sɛ aban no abɔ mmɔden sɛ ɔbɛma amannɔnefo adan wɔn ho wɔn ho .
Sɛ wɔkyekyem pɛpɛɛpɛ a , sɛ wɔkyekyem pɛpɛɛpɛ a , po so hyɛn gyinabea bi tua dɔla 53 ma RTGS no , bere a wɔbɔ nea ɔpɛ sɛ ofi hɔ nnansa no ka $ 250 no .
Wɔbɔ ahwehwɛde a wɔde betwa po so hyɛn gyinabea ho asɛm ho ka $ 380 .
Amrado Paradza , guamtrani no kae sɛ ne boayikuw no boaa po so hyɛn gyinabea adwumayɛfo no denneennen ma woyii po so ahyɛn ho nkrataa sɛ ɔkwan a wɔnam so boa saa nkurɔfo yi ma wotumi nya wɔn nkrataa no , a wɔn atrae a ɛwɔ wɔn man mu no nka ho .
Paradza kae sɛ nnipa pii a wɔatu wɔn ho ama no ate sɛ wɔn abusuafo ne wɔn nnamfo korɔn , na wotuaa sika pii maa wɔn akwantu ho adwumayɛfo no .
Isaac Nyaumba , a ofi Zimbabwe no , kae sɛ n'ani gyei sɛ onyaa hokwan hyiaam , na ɔbɔɔlbɔfo Neymar a wagye din no twaa no mfonini .
Neymar , a wɔwoo no wɔ Sao Paulo, Brazil , na ne din nyinaa ne Neymar da Silva Santos Júnior .
Mprempren Neymar redi agoru wɔ Barcelona's Spanishfo fekuw bi a bɔɔlbɔfo , Lionel Messi ka ho . Ɔno nso di agoru wɔ Brazil , na ɔno na odii kan de sika kɔkɔɔ kɔyɛɛ adwuma wɔ Olympics no .
Nanso , ɛwom sɛ wɔde Nyaumba ne Neymarfo mfonini no too Victoria Falls mu de , nanso wɔka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ bere a wɔreyɛ adwuma wɔ Ukutula Conservation Center, a ɛbɛn Pretoria wɔ South Africa no , wɔde yɛɛ ho mfonini .
Mighty Warriors mmea kuw no redi agoru kɛse bi wɔ wɔn abakɔsɛm mu , na ɔmanfo pɛ sɛ Zimbabwe di so nkonim na ama wɔatumi akɔ ɔman no agumadi mu abakɔsɛm mu .
Mighty Warriors no rehyɛn Rufaro Stadium Kwasida wɔ wɔn agumadibea a ɛso sen biara fi 1980 bere a Zimbabwe fii amanaman ntam akansi ase no .
Mmea a wɔte hɔ no rehyia Indomitable Lionesses a ɛwɔ Cameroon no wɔ ɔkwan bi a ɛbɛma wɔahu sɛ ebia Zimbabwe betumi afata ama afe a etwaam no Olympic Games a ɛwɔ Rio de Janeiro no so .
Wɔhwee Mighty Warriors no 2 - 1 bere a akuw abien no hyiaam wɔ Yaounde adapɛn abien a atwam ni no , nanso ɛho hia sɛ wonya 1 - 0 ansa na wɔatumi afata ama Wiase Ko no .
Bere a Mighty Warriors no afata ama nsrahwɛfo no , wɔmaa wɔn mu baanu a ɔto so abien no sii akan wɔ mfe 35 mu sɛ wonsi akan wɔ nsrahwɛ no akyi wɔ 1980 mfe no mu
Nanso , Mighty Warriors no kɔ so fi abakɔsɛm mu bere a kuw a edi kan a wɔatumi asi akan wɔ nsrahwɛ no mu no , bere a wɔtoo nsa frɛɛ mmeawa no kɔɔ Moscow bere a wɔtoo nsa frɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔmmra akuw a wontwaa twetia no .
Warriors Fan Club , Zivanai Moroyiwa , ka sɛ wɔtwentwɛn wɔn nan ase wɔ agodie no ho sɛ Mighty Warriors no bɛma ɔmanfo ani agye denam nea kuw no anaa kuw bi ayɛ wɔ mfe 35 a etwaam no mu no so .
Caps United bɔn Tonderayi Matimura ka sɛ bere a akuw abien no hyiam adapɛn abien a atwam ni no , wɔwɔ ahotoso sɛ Mighty Kofofo no bedi wɔn ho so na wɔadi nkonim bio .
Zimbabwe Fekubɔ Fekuw no ahu hia a ɛho hia sɛ ɔmanfo di agoru no , na wɔayɛ nhyehyɛe ama ɔmanfo no sɛ wontua ka bi mfa nhwɛ agodie a ɛho hia yi .
Agumadi ho sɛnkyerɛwfo Andrew Rwodzi ka sɛ nnipa pii bɛba agumadibea hɔ bere a agodibea no yɛ sika a obiara betumi atua de ahwɛ agodie a ɛho hia yi .
Owura Matimura kae sɛ ɔbɛkɔ agumadibea hɔ nso bere a agodibea no yɛ ade a ne bo yɛ den sen dɔla abiɛsa a Zifa hwehwɛ no .
Kuw no mufo a wɔyɛ coach , Shadreck Mlauzi , no ayɛ kuw a emu yɛ den a wɔn a wodi gua ne wɔn a wodi agoru te sɛ Rudo Neshamba ne Rutendo Machingura de ogya besi wɔn akyi Kwasida .
Bere koro no ara , Warriors kuw no bɛba Bourfields Stadium , baabi a Lesotho hyia wɔ Afrika Amanaman Nkabom no Adwumayɛbea a ɛhwɛ nneɛma a atwa wɔn ho ahyia a emu yɛ den sen Mighty Warri
Nnipa baasa a wɔbɔ bɔɔl wɔ Hardlife Zvirekwi ne Ɔtemmufo Jangano a ɔwɔ Caps United ne Ronald Chitiynamos a ɛwɔ Dynamos no de wɔn ho hyɛɛ ɔbarima ne ɔbea nna mu ɔbrasɛe mu , nanso Murorororo kae sɛ Warriors no nsiw akuw a ɛte sɛ Lesotho no kwan .
Ɔkofo no rehwɛ kwan sɛ wobedi agoru abien wɔ akuw abien no ntam de adi Afrika Amanaman Nkabom no Tipione a etwa to no ho dwuma akosi bere a ɛto so anan wɔ afe 2012, ne 2014 mfe no mu .
Nanso ɔmanfo ani ne wɔn adwene wɔ Mighty Warriors agodie no ho .
Abɔnten so ahwɛfo a wɔwɔ Harare's mfɛfo ne Tajamuka / Sesijikile fekuw no mufo abɛka asraafo a wɔne kurow no mu polisifo ne Zimbabwe Police , a wɔbɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔapam wɔn afi wɔn nnwuma ho no ho .
Saa ara na esii wɔ Norton kurow mu , baabi a wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔremma kwan mma wɔnkɔtɔ nneɛma bere a na wɔretɔn wɔ Katanga no .
Tajamuka / Sesijikile kasamafo, Makomborero Haruzivishe , kae
Haruzivishe kae sɛ bere a yɛkɔɔ wim no , na wɔda so ara wɔ polisifo adwumam hɔ rebɔ mmɔden sɛ yebehu nnipa dodow a wɔakyere wɔn wɔ asɛm no mu , nanso ɔkae sɛ wonim wɔn mu biako .
Harare Kuropɔn Bagua no kasamafo Michael Chideme kae sɛ wɔntee asɛm no bere a na wonni kurom no .
Nanso aban no nam Information Asoɛe no so de nkrasɛm bi too gua sɛ polisifo akunkum mmofra pii .
Aban no aka nso sɛ ɛyɛ video a ɛkyerɛ sɛ mmofra a wɔadu wɔn mpanyin afe so no de polisifo , a wɔde wɔn bedi dwuma wɔ asɛnnibea de atoto ɔkorɔmfo no ho .
Yɛantumi ante asɛm no amfi polisifo hɔ .
Zimbabwe Community ahyehyɛde bi a egyina Zimbabwefo a wɔte South Africa ne wɔn a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ hɔ so ka sɛ nea ɛhaw adwene kɛse wɔ nneɛma a adwowtwafo a wɔwɔ Johannesburg borɔn bi so a wosusuw sɛ Zimbabweanfo na wɔwɔ hɔ no ho .
Kuw no ka sɛ nsɛmmɔnedi a ɛkɔ so wɔ Hillrow, Berea ne Yeoville no yɛ aman pii , a Zimbabweanfo , a wɔn a wɔkyere nkurɔfo sie , wɔn a wɔkyere nkurɔfo sie , ne awudifo ka ho .
Zimbabwe Ɔmanfo Nkabom Kuw a ɛwɔ South Africa no kasamafo Bongani Mkwananzi kae sɛ wɔreyɛ nhyehyɛe ne polisifo adi nkitaho ma wɔama asɛm no ho aba asɛm , na wɔhyɛ polisifo nkuran sɛ wɔnyɛ biribi a anibere wom .
Ɔkae sɛ February 6, a ɛbɛba ɔsram a edi hɔ no , n'ahyehyɛde no rehwɛ kwan sɛ wɔne polisifo a wɔwɔ amansin no mu no behyiam ayɛ adwuma abom de adi ɔhaw no ho dwuma .
Wɔka nso sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ polisifo bɔ wɔn ho mmɔden wɔ mpɔtam hɔ , nanso mpɛn pii no , wontumi mfa wɔn ho nhyɛ mu , na ɛno na ɛde awifo ne adwowtwafo a wɔyɛ Jojina'ss ka ho .
Owura Mkwananzi kae sɛ wɔn a wokunkum wɔn no mu pii nim wɔn a wɔka wɔn ankasa kasa no bi , enti ɛsɛ sɛ polisifo a wodi nsɛmmɔne no ne Zimbabweanfo a wɔte saa mmeae yi yɛ adwuma .
Afoforo a wɔaka asɛm no akyerɛ Studio7 no nso ka ho bi na wɔkamfo asraafo a wɔdɔɔso wɔ saa mmeae yi na ama wɔatumi agyae saa nsɛmmɔnedi yi .
Efi bere tenten na South Africafo abɔ aman pii sobo sɛ nsɛmmɔnedi , nnubɔne , ne tuutuusi renya nkɔanim .
Nnipa pii ka sɛ afe 2019 na amammui ne sikasɛm mu ahokyere befi ase wɔ ɔman no mu .
The New Patriotic Party (NPP) Member of Parliament (Twiriw East), Owura Paul Apraku Twum Barimah , de asɛmmisa bi a egye ntɛmpɛ a ɛwɔ Parliament (NPPP) no ato gua sɛ wɔmma nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn a kan Ɔmampanyin John Mahama de dii dwuma wɔ amannɔne akwantu ho wɔ 2013 ne 2017 mu no mmɔ ka .
Ɔkaa asɛmmisa no ho asɛm , na wɔmaa Owurayere Ken Ofori - Attah , somaifo boaa no ne Ghanafo ma wɔkɔɔ so ne wɔn bɔɔ nkɔmmɔ wɔ baguam ɔkasa no mu wɔ wimhyɛn no titrani a na kan no
Kyakyatow ho nsɛm a wɔakyere agu hama so no ama yɛahu sɛnea ɔman yi bo yɛ den fi afe 2013 kosi 2017 kosi 2017 , bere a kan no na Mahama de nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn tu kwan no .
Obiara ne no nsɛ
Bere a Owura Barimah reda ne botae a ɛne sɛ obedi asɛmmisa a egye ntɛmpɛ no ho dwuma , a mprempren ɛwɔ Ɔmantam Nhyiam no ase no , ɔkae sɛ n'asɛmmisa no nni amammuisɛm mu ahotoso biara .
Bere bi a atwam no , na yetumi si gyinae sɛ yɛbɛyɛ ɔman bi a amampanyin atwa yɛn ho ahyia , na sɛ yenim nea ɛrekɔ so a ɛsɛ sɛ yesi ho gyinae no a , gye sɛ yesi gyinae a ɛte saa ansa na yɛatumi asi .
Asorɔkye a edi kan bi wɔ hɔ , na sɛ obi di kan de ne ho hyɛ dwumadi bi mu a , na ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɔkwankyerɛfo bi wɔ hɔ a obetumi afa so ama saa ɔmampanyin akwantu yi anya nkɔanim ma emu ada hɔ pefee , na mempɛ sɛ metumi ayɛ amammuisɛm mu adeyɛ a ɛte saa ara , na ɔkae sɛ ɔno nso wɔ hɔ .
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ: " Nea yɛpɛ ara ne sɛ yebenya anobaabae ne ɔkasa a ɛfata na ama yɛatumi aka nsɛm a ɛfata ho asɛm nnɛ .
Ablakwa ma asɛmmisa a egye ntɛmpɛ sɔre
Owura Samuel Okudzeto Ablakwa a ɔyɛ Amannɔne Bagua no muni no nso de asɛmmisa bi a egye ntɛmpɛ a ɛwɔ Parliament mu too gua sɛ aban no kyerɛkyerɛ nea enti a Ɔmampanyin Addo Dankwairay - Akudo de wimhyɛn no anyɛ adwuma mfa wimhyɛn no nkɔ France nnansa yi no mu .
Sɛnea National Democratic Congress (NDC) North Tongugugugugument (Franse) kyerɛ no , "It yɛ adwuma a ɛyɛ den , na ɛda adi pefee sɛ Ghana yɛ ɔmampanyin a ɔyɛ adwuma pɛpɛɛpɛ , na ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ ɔkwan a edi mu so sɛ " wimhyɛn a edi mũ a wɔde wimhyɛn tu kwan kɔ beae a wɔhwɛ adwuma no .
Afei nso , obuu akontaa sɛ Ɔmampanyin no bɔ ka wɔ GH ho sɛ ɔde bɛyɛ ɔpepem2 .
Bono East Regional Ministeral Minister, Owura Kwasi Adu - Gyan , akamfo Asɛnnikuw Foforo no kannifo (NPP) ne National Democratic Congionress (NDC) a wɔyɛ de boa ma asomdwoe ba ɔmantam no mu no .
NKURUYƐFO hoahoa wɔn ho , na wɔn ani gye kɛse sɛ wobehu NP ne NDC a ɛwɔ Bono Supɔw so sɛ wɔbom yɛ adwuma asomdwoe mu , denam amammui mu adwenhorow a ɛda wɔn ntam no so no , ɔkae sɛ .
Owura Adu - Gyan kae sɛ asomdwoe na ɛmaa nneɛma kɔɔ so yiye , na ɔde kaa ho sɛ , sɛ asomdwoe nni hɔ a , ɛbɛyɛ den ama yɛn sɛ yebenya nkɔso wɔ ɔmantam no mu .
Ɔsomfo a ɔwɔ ɔmantam no mu de nkamfo no mae wɔ asɛm bi a wɔkyerɛw too hɔ wɔ Techiman no akyi no mu .
Ananmusifo a wogyina NP ne ADC , atetesɛm mu atumfoɔ , ahobammɔ ahyehyɛde ahorow , Adwinnade a Edi Kan (ECs), ne Ɔman Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Nhomasua Ho Nsɛm So (NCCE) ne ɔmanfo asetra kwan (CSOs) no so na wɔbaa nhyiam no ase .
Ná Amanaman Ntam Asomdwoe Bagua no de ahyɛde a efi Ahintasɛm mu Ba no ama wɔ so: Atirimɔden Asɛnni a Wɔde Maa Nnipa 2020 Atrae , ne Nsi a Wɔde Siei a Wɔhwehwɛɛ Amanyɔne Kɛse a Wodi So wɔ Ghana .
Topics kaa sɛnea wɔne afoforo di nsɛm wɔ kɔmputa so basabasayɛ ne abatow mu nyiyim ho asɛm .
Owura Adu - Gyan kae sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ Ghanafo ani gye ɔman no mu asomdwoe a ɛto so abien a ɛsen biara wɔ Afrika no ho denam Wiase Nyinaa Asomdwoe Index Report 2021 so , na wɔmaa ɛho behiae sɛ NP ne NDC no boa ma wɔkora asomdwoe a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu no so .
Ntawntawdi ho nhyehyɛe a wɔayɛ no yɛ mmɔden kɛse a sodifo , amammui mu akuw , ahobammɔ nnwuma , ne afei Executcut , Legislature , Judiciary ne nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfo bɔe .
Ɔmaa wɔn awerɛhyem sɛ wɔbɛkɔ so de Ɔmantam Nhyiam (RCC) no adi dwuma ma asomdwoe aba .
Alhaji Suallah Quandah , a ɔyɛ ɔpanyin wɔ Atɛntrenee Ho Bagua a Ɛhwɛ Asomdwoe Ho Nsɛm So no kae wɔ ne dwumadi bi a wɔyɛe wɔ Electoral Ɔtemmufo no ase no mu sɛ , ɔkwan a wɔfa so bu atɛntrenee no dii dwuma titiriw maa amammui nhyehyɛe no gyinaa pintinn wɔ ɔman no mu .
Wɔahu dwuma titiriw a wɔnam anyinam ahoɔden so paw atɛntrenee no , ɛwom sɛ ɛnyɛ foforo de , nanso wɔasan ahu sɛ ɛno ne ade a ɛho hia a ɛde basabasayɛ ba , sɛ́ ebia ɛbɛda adi anaasɛ ɛde ba no , ɛno ara na ɛmaa asɛm no bae , na wɔkyerɛkyerɛɛ mu sɛ mmara a wɔnam so bu atɛn no yɛ ade a wogyina so siw amammui ne abatow ano .
Alhaji Quandah sii so dua sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔde bere ne bere mu hwehwɛ ɔman no mmara a wɔnam so bu atɛntrenee no mu sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɛbɛma abatow a edi mũ no anya mmamu .
ABAKƆSƐM Abuakwa South Samuel Atta Abubua no ama Ghanafo bi a wɔfrɛ wɔn Nana Akufo - Addo nniso no anya wɔn tebea no ho awerɛhyem bere a NP no di tumi fi January 7, 2017 no .
Sɛnea ne ho kyerɛ no , Ghanafo benya sikasɛm mu ahofadi wɔ Nana Akufo - Addo , sikasɛm mu nhyehyɛe a wɔyɛ de gyigye wɔn ani a wobeyi afi hɔ no anim .
January 7 bɛyɛ bere foforo a ɛde yɛn yiyedi ne yɛn ahofadi bɛba , ne titiriw no , Ghanafo a wɔpɛ sika fam ahofadi a wɔn ani gye ho . Ghanafo behu sɛ Onyankopɔn agye ɔman no afi ahokyere mu , Attabia , na waka wɔ ntoboa a ɔde kɔmaa Asiafo a wɔwɔ Apuei fam mantam mu no mu .
Ɔkae sɛ wayɛ krado sɛ ɔbɛsom wɔ asafo no mu sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a Ɔmampanyin Akufo - Addo betumi de bi ama no .
Nneɛma a ɔde mae no bi ne ɛmo , ngo , nkyene , nufusu , nufusu , ne dwetɛbona ason .
Wɔahu anuanom mmea baasa bi a wɔbow nsa wɔ wɔn nkurow mu no sɛ wɔawuwu wɔ Tarkwa - Nasuta a ɛwɔ Tarkwa - Naguta mantam a ɛwɔ Atɔe fam no mu .
Nnipa baasa no wui bere a awosu mu nkwaadɔm bi kunkum wɔn no .
Owura bi a wɔfrɛ no George Sekyi a ɔwɔ Tarkwa - Nasuta adwumayɛbea no kae wɔ December 18 mu sɛ , wɔtoo nsa frɛɛ mmofra baasa wɔ baabi a wɔnom nsa .
Ɔkae sɛ ɔne ne mpanyimfo no de ahopere kɔɔ hɔ , nanso wɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ Abena Amos , 15, Arabi Paapazi, 13 , ne Aka Paapazi, 7, na wɔapo no dedaw wɔ Tarkwa Aban Ayaresabea a Wodi So no .
Bere a Starr News bisabisaa Emmanuel Ohene Gyan Gyan Sekyi nsɛm no , ɔkae sɛ nea wawu no ne wɔn maame te , na ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ Kitchen Kuropɔn Kitchen mu a n'adidibea nom nsa wɔ Tarkwa Asuem ahotew mu .
Ɔkae sɛ wosii gyinae sɛ wobetwa anadwo no wɔ asanombea hɔ bere a wɔboaa wɔn maame ma ɔtɔn nnuan no .
Aban panyin no kae wɔ December 17, sɛ bere a ade resã kɛse bi sii wɔ da no mu , ne ɛno nti Madam Paapazi de akorade bi a ɛwɔ akorade no mu maa nea wawu no tumi nyaa hann bere a ɔdae no . Akyiri yi mmeawa no maame huu wɔn sɛ wɔawu bere a ɔkɔɔ beae a edi hɔ anɔpa no .
Onuawa bi a ɔto so anan a ohui sɛ ne ho nni asɛm nso renya ayaresa . Police a ɛwɔ mpɔtam hɔ no rehwehwɛ asɛm no mu .
Flagbearer a ɔyɛ Ɔman Democratic Congress (NDC) John Mahama no ka sɛ obedi Ɔsahene a Ɔhwɛ Nnipa a Wɔakyere Wɔn Ho Nsɛm So a Ɔfrɛ no Nana Appiah Mensah Mensah Mensah Mensah a wagye din sɛ NAM 1, no akyi no , sɛ odi gua wɔ December mu a .
Bere a Owura Mahama reka asɛm no wɔ Tarkwa - Paulem a ɛwɔ Western Region no , obisaa nea enti a ɛte sɛ nea Akufo - Addo nniso no ani nnye ho sɛ wɔbɛpene nneɛma pa a ɛwɔ NAM1 no so , na mmom wɔde wɔn abufuw bɛhyɛ adetɔfo no abufuw so .
SƐNEA NAM 1 te no yɛ soronko koraa wɔ NAM 1 ho araa ma Akufo - Addo rebɔ ne ho ban , nea enti a wommɔ polisifo a wɔn ho nni asɛm no ho ban bere a NAM 1 nnantew no .
Ɔhyɛɛ no bɔ sɛ n'ahenni a edi hɔ no bɛhwehwɛ NAM1 ne n'adwumam mpanyimfo no mu yiye , na ɔde nneɛma a ɛfata nyinaa adi dwuma de ayi ntoboa no .
Circuit Asennibea a Her Honour Ellenmoah dii n'anim September 7 no de asɛm no too gua wɔ Menzgold Nana Appiah Mensah Mensahsah Mensah (NAM1) no mu .
Ná Ɔman no adi kan abɔ NAM 1 sobo foforo wɔ Circuit Abangua no so wɔ June 24,20, 2020, na wodii kan bɔɔ no sobo foforo .
Sɛnea Superindent a ɔwɔ Police (ASP) Sylvester Asare ka kyerɛɛ Asennibea no sɛ n'atemmu no ne sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ okura sobo foforo no ne wɔn a wɔabɔ wɔn sobo no adesrɛ no mu .
Wɔ July 20, ASP Asare ka kyerɛɛ asɛnnibea no sɛ , wɔreyɛ adwuma a emu yɛ duru de afotu ama asɛnnibea no .
Nea ɛbɛyɛ na eyi aba awiei no , ɔbɔɔ asɛnnibea no mpae sɛ wɔmma wɔn ani nnye bere tenten bi a anka wobetumi de afotu ama asɛnnibea no bere a na wɔpɛ sɛ wɔde asɛm no kɔ asɛnnibea no .
Ɔkae sɛ bere a afotu no ayɛ krado no , wɔn a wɔabɔ wɔn sobo no behu wɔn a wɔabɔ wɔn sobo no sɛ wɔmmra asɛnnibea hɔ mmɛboa wɔn a wohia mmoa no .
Nanso wɔ asennibea wɔ Dwoda no , mmaranimfo no bɔɔ mpae sɛ wɔmma obi ani nnye , na wɔmaa hokwan .
Ná onipa a wɔabɔ no sobo no ne NAM 1 wɔ asɛnnibea .
Circuit Asennibea a ɛwɔ July 26,19 no de NAM nkankyee a ɛwɔ GH sum ase no ɔpepepem 1 a emu duru yɛ ɔpepepem 1 a wogye di sɛ ɛfata sɛ wodi ho dwuma
Ná onni fɔ wɔ sobo 13 a Ɔman no bɔɔ no mfiase no nyinaa ho . Efi saa bere no na ɔman no
Afei nso , ɛsɛ sɛ ɔde nnɔnhwerew 10:00 bɔ polisifo amanneɛ .
Nea edi kan no , wɔbɔɔ no sobo sɛ wayɛ bɔne , na wadi atoro , na ɔde ne ho ahyɛ adwuma bi a sika nnim mu a onni hokwan sɛ ɔyɛ , otuo a onni hokwan biara , a n'ani nnye ho , ne sika ho .
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ na wɔn a wɔbɔɔ wɔn sobo no afa sika pii , GH a ne dodow si ɔpepepem 1.6 .
Okada kɛse a wɔde di dwuma wɔ aguadi mu no rehaw adwene kɛse .
Polisifo akyerɛ nso sɛ nsɛmmɔnedi , akwanhyia , ne kar kwan ho mmara a ɛfa moto ho no anya nkɔanim .
Akyinnye biara nni ho sɛ , Okadafo no rehwehwɛ nsa ne biribi a ɛho hia paa a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ de tew wɔn ho .
Yɛaka Okada ho asɛm pii mpɛn pii .
Wɔ saa bere yi mu no , ɔman no hyia asɛnnennen a ɛne sɛ wobedi moto ne ɛmo so , ne titiriw no , wɔ aguadi mu .
Mmarahyɛ bagua a wɔyɛe wɔ afe 2012 mu no de Karffic Regulations, 2012 (L.I . 2180) kɔɔ mmara mu sɛ wɔmfa kar nkɔ ɔman no mu .
Nea ɛka nneɛma foforo ho no , Regulation 128 a ɛwɔ afã horow no mu biako kosi anan (Legislative Instrument (L.I .) 2180) yi motorbike a wɔde di dwuma no fi motorom a agye din a wɔde dii dwuma sɛ teaseɛnam a wɔde di dwuma no mu .
Saa mmara yi a wɔahyehyɛ no , ɛmfa ho sɛ okada ne tricycle (mogya) agye kar ho nhyehyɛe no wɔ ɔman no afã pii no .
Wɔ nkuraa a ɛbemmɛn hɔ ase no , okada ne nnaka no nkutoo na ɛde kar kɔ gua so , mmeae a wɔhwɛ akwahosan ne nkurow afoforo mu , wɔ mmeae foforo .
Wɔ nnipa a wɔwɔ nkurow akɛse mu fam no , wotumi hwe kar a emu yɛ duru no denam awɔ a wɔbɛhwɛ wɔn no so .
Awɔ no nso yɛ kar a ne bo yɛ den bere a ne bo nyɛ den no .
Esiane sɛ wonni kar ho nhyehyɛe a ɛyɛ fɛ na wotumi de ho to so nti , wɔsan de wɔn ho hyɛ mu .
Nanso , nnipa pii yɛ okada na wɔn ani da hɔ esiane sɛ wɔn ani nnye karka ho nti , na wɔn mu dodow no ara
Asiane a emu yɛ den a efi Okada a wɔmfa nni dwuma yiye mu ba no nso haw adwene .
Nokwarem no , mmeae pii , a nea ɛka ho ne Ghana Ayaresa ne Ɔman Akwantu Asoɛe no , ahwehwɛ sɛ wɔabara wɔn koraa sɛ wɔmfa kar nkɔ ɔman no mu .
Eyi agyaw ɔman no wɔ po a emu dɔ mu .
Nea enti a ɛte saa ne sɛ , ɛmfa ho sɛ wɔhyɛɛ mmara sɛ wɔmfa wɔn ho nhyɛ aguadi mu no , ɛyɛ ade titiriw a ɛmaa Ghanafo pii ho tɔ wɔn .
Wɔ yɛn fam no , yesusuw sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ ɔman no de wɔn adwene si mmara no so na wɔde akwan a ɛfata sen biara a ɛbɛma nnipa nsa aka nea wohia no so .
Sɛ nhwɛso no , wɔ India no , amumɔyɛ yɛ ɔkwan titiriw a wɔfa so tu kwan , nanso yɛntee anwiinwii ho asɛm bere a yɛwɔ Ghana no .
Enti , nea yebetumi asua afi India na yɛde ahyɛ yɛn nhyehyɛe yi mu
Ɛsɛ sɛ yɛma ɛtena yɛn adwenem sɛ bere a nnipa dodow no ara nnya adwuma nyɛ no , okada ne mfiri a wɔde yɛ adwuma no bu no sɛ ade a ɛma wonya sika fi mu ma wɔne wɔn mmusua .
Nanso te sɛ nnɛyi , okadas ne nkontaabu yɛ ade a yɛn ani gye ho , na yegye di wɔ Daily Graphic no mu sɛ , ɛdenam nhomasua so no , ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ nnwumakuw a ɛfata no de di dwuma sɛ sɛ wohu sɛ ɔman no nni wɔn akyi a , ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ wɔn ade ma ɛne no hyia .
Nea ɛbɛyɛ na wɔatumi ahu mmara anaa nhyehyɛe a ɛwɔ hɔ nnɛ a wɔyɛ ho adwuma , ntetee a wɔde ma wɔ nhomasua mu no , wobetumi ayɛ nhyehyɛe a wɔde bɛhwɛ wɔn a wɔte mo moto so ne wɔn a wɔhwɛ sini so yiye .
Bere a nhyehyɛe a ɛte saa wɔ hɔ no , ɛbɛyɛ mmerɛw ama Ghana Polisi Adwumakuw no sɛ wobedi mmara so , na wɔadi motorbi awɔ a wɔnhyɛ da ne wɔn a wɔde wɔn ho hyɛ nsɛmmɔnedi mu no nso ho dwuma .
Mprempren , Ghanafo mu apaapae wɔ akwan atitiriw abien a wɔfa so tu kwan yi mu esiane wɔn mfaso ne wɔn a wɔn ho nni asɛm nti .
The Daily Graphic gye di sɛ sɛ yɛpɛ sɛ yɛsakra yɛn akwan mu na yɛma yɛn akwantu nhyehyɛe no tu mpɔn a , ɛnde ɛsɛ sɛ yɛde abɛn no bɔ yɛn ho ban , na yɛde torobɛnto no gyina ɔhaw no ano nnɛ anaa ɛnsɛ sɛ yɛyɛ saa .
Mekae da bi a na m'ani agye paa wɔ Ghana nnansa yi sen Fida a etwaam no , Green Ghana .
Saa da no na wɔhyɛɛ yɛn nyinaa nkuran sɛ yemfi adi na yendua dua .
Esiane sɛ mesan baa Ghana mfe 20 a atwam ni , na m'ani gye ho paa sɛ yɛn man no yɛ soronko koraa wɔ nea ɛwɔ Geography nhoma no mu ho nti , na eyi ne mmɔden a edi mũ sen biara a wɔbɔe sɛ wɔbɛyɛ biribi de asiw asiane a ɛwɔ yɛn nsase yi so no ano .
Afifide ne Adwenemyare Ho Asoɛe no de aba ɔpepem anum maa yɛn na ɛmaa yenyaa anigye tebea bi a na ɛyɛ anigye a na mahwɛ kwan bere tenten .
Ebetumi aba sɛ na Ghanafo ahu sɛ ade biako a ehia sɛ yɛde yɛn adwene si so sen biribi foforo biara ne asase no so okunkɛse a yɛfrɛ no Ghana no
Sɛ́ anka kar kwan a aporɔw biara so no , sukuu biara a emu apaapae , ayaresabea biara a wonni mpa so anaa sukuu mmofra a wonni kɔmputa ne I daresay no , nea enye koraa wɔ ɔyare mmoawa biara ho no , nea ɛsɛ sɛ yɛn nyinaa nya na yɛkɔ so bɔ ho ban no ne yɛn asase no so tebea no , asase a na asubɔnten no ayow no , ne nea ɛsɛ sɛ anka ɛsɛ sɛ yɛde di dwuma ɔsram biara no .
Mahwehwɛ Geography nhoma a wɔde di dwuma wɔ yɛn sukuu ahorow mu nnɛ no mu , nanso minim sɛ su horow a ɛwɔ Ghana asase no so wɔ nhoma a mede dii dwuma wɔ sukuu mu no nte sɛ Ghana a ɛwɔ hɔ nnɛ no .
Yɛda so ara ka kwaebirentuw ho asɛm , nanso ɛnte saa wɔ yɛn nsase yi so .
Yɛda so ara ka wuram mmoa ho asɛm , nanso na wɔakyere wɔn agu wɔn atrae bere tenten a atwam ni .
Mprempren kwaebirentuw ne wuram mmoa a wɔwɔ hɔ nnɛ no ka yɛn kasa ho , na ɛnyɛ yɛn ankasa de no .
Wɔayi nea na yesusuw sɛ ɛyɛ kwae no mpo afi hɔ de ahwehwɛ sika kɔkɔɔ ne mineral foforo .
Ebia yɛn mu dodow no ara huu yɛn ankasa , na mehwɛ kwan sɛ wɔn a wɔamfa wɔn ho anhyɛ mu no wɔ ntease pa bi nti a wɔanyɛ saa .
